### [Sessão Paralela: PM]
Vamos definir o backlog V12 com foco em estabilidade autônoma. Primeiro, preciso entender:

Qual é o maior problema de estabilidade atual que os usuários enfrentam?

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Arquitetura Técnica

## 1. ARQUITETURA DE SISTEMA V12

### 1.1. Visão Geral da Arquitetura
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┐
│                    DIYAPP V12 - ARCHITECTURE                │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│  LAYER                  COMPONENTS                          │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│  Presentation Layer    • Web Dashboard (React 18 + Vite)    │
│                        • Mobile App (React Native)          │
│                        • API Gateway (Fastify)              │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│  Application Layer     • Core Services (Node.js 20+)        │
│                        • Task Orchestrator                  │
│                        • LLM Integration Service            │
│                        • Authentication Service             │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│  Domain Layer          • Domain Models (TypeScript)         │
│                        • Business Rules                     │
│                        • Value Objects                      │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│  Infrastructure Layer  • PostgreSQL (Primary DB)            │
│                        • Redis (Cache & Queue)              │
│                        • MinIO (Object Storage)             │
│                        • Elasticsearch (Search)             │
├─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┤
│  Observability         • OpenTelemetry                      │
│                        • Prometheus + Grafana               │
│                        • Structured Logging                 │
└─────────────────────────────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### 1.2. ADR-001: Arquitetura de Microserviços com Comunicação por Eventos
```markdown
# ADR-001: Arquitetura Baseada em Eventos para DIYAPP V12

**Data:** 2024-01-15
**Status:** Aceita
**Autores:** Tech Lead + Especialista Infra

## CONTEXTO:
A versão atual do DIYAPP enfrenta problemas de acoplamento forte entre componentes, dificultando a evolução independente das squads. Necessitamos de uma arquitetura que permita:
- Desenvolvimento paralelo por múltiplas squads
- Escalabilidade horizontal independente por componente
- Tolerância a falhas e resiliência
- Manutenção de consistência eventual entre serviços

## DECISÃO:
Adotar arquitetura baseada em eventos com os seguintes padrões:
1. **Event Sourcing** para estado crítico do negócio
2. **CQRS** para separação de leitura/escrita
3. **Message Broker** (Redis Streams) para comunicação assíncrona
4. **Saga Pattern** para transações distribuídas

## OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:
- **Opção A:** Monolito modularizado (atual) - Prós: Simples deploy, debugging fácil. Contras: Acoplamento forte, escala limitada.
- **Opção B:** Microserviços REST - Prós: Independência de deploy. Contras: Acoplamento temporal, complexidade de transações.
- **Opção C:** Arquitetura baseada em eventos - Prós: Desacoplamento total, escalabilidade, resiliência. Contras: Complexidade inicial, debugging assíncrono.

**Opção escolhida:** C - Justificativa: Alinha com objetivo de 100% autonomia das squads e permite evolução paralela.

## CONSEQUÊNCIAS:
**Positivas:**
- Squads podem desenvolver e deployar independentemente
- Sistema tolerante a falhas parciais
- Escalabilidade granular por componente
- Audit trail completo via event sourcing

**Negativas:**
- Maior complexidade operacional
- Necessidade de ferramentas de monitoramento robustas
- Curva de aprendizado para novos devs
- Latência eventual para consistência

**Riscos:**
- Eventos perdidos: Mitigar com DLQ e retry policies
- Debugging complexo: Implementar correlation IDs e tracing distribuído
- Volume de eventos: Implementar compaction e arquivamento

## REVISÃO:** 2024-07-15 (6 meses)
```

module.exports = {
  preset: 'ts-jest',

  roots: ['<rootDir>/src'],
  testMatch: ['**/__tests__/**/*.ts', '**/?(*.)+(spec|test).ts'],

    '^.+\\.ts$': 'ts-jest'
  },
  collectCoverageFrom: [
    'src/**/*.ts',
    '!src/**/*.d.ts',
    '!src/**/index.ts',
    '!src/**/__tests__/**'

      branches: 80,
      functions: 80,
      lines: 80,
      statements: 80

## 4. FLUXO DE CI/CD

### 4.1. GitHub Actions Workflow
```yaml
# .github/workflows/ci-cd.yml
name: CI/CD Pipeline

on:
  push:
    branches: [main, develop]
  pull_request:
    branches: [main, develop]

env:
  NODE_VERSION: '20'
  DOCKER_REGISTRY: ghcr.io
  IMAGE_NAME: ${{ github.repository }}

jobs:
  quality-gate:
    name: Quality Gate
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Setup Node.js
      uses: actions/setup-node@v3
      with:
        node-version: ${{ env.NODE_VERSION }}
        cache: 'npm'
    
    - name: Install Dependencies
      run: npm ci
    
    - name: Lint
      run: npm run lint
    
    - name: Type Check
      run: npm run type-check
    
    - name: Unit Tests
      run: npm test -- --coverage
    
    - name: Upload Coverage
      uses: codecov/codecov-action@v3
      with:
        file: ./coverage/lcov.info
        fail_ci_if_error: true
    
    - name: Security Scan
      uses: snyk/actions/node@master
      env:
        SNYK_TOKEN: ${{ secrets.SNYK_TOKEN }}
      with:
        args: --severity-threshold=high
    
    - name: Build
      run: npm run build

  integration-tests:
    name: Integration Tests
    runs-on: ubuntu-latest
    needs: quality-gate
    
    services:
      postgres:
        image: postgres:15-alpine
        env:
          POSTGRES_PASSWORD: testpassword
          POSTGRES_DB: diyapp_test
        options: >-
          --health-cmd pg_isready
          --health-interval 10s
          --health-timeout 5s
          --health-retries 5
        ports:
          - 5432:5432
      
      redis:
        image: redis:7-alpine
        options: >-
          --health-cmd "redis-cli ping"
          --health-interval 10s
          --health-timeout 5s
          --health-retries 5
        ports:
          - 6379:6379
    
    steps:
    - uses: actions/checkout@v3
    
    - name: Setup Node.js
      uses: actions/setup-node@v3
      with:
        node-version: ${{ env.NODE_VERSION }}
    
    - name: Install Dependencies
      run

# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Infraestrutura e Monitoramento

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v12-infra/
├── k8s/
│   ├── namespaces/
│   ├── deployments/
│   ├── services/
│   ├── configmaps/
│   ├── secrets/
│   └── ingress/
├── serverless/
│   ├── functions/
│   └── triggers/
├── monitoring/
│   ├── prometheus/
│   ├── grafana/
│   ├── loki/
│   └── alertmanager/
├── ci-cd/
│   ├── github-actions/
│   └── argocd/
├── terraform/
│   ├── main.tf
│   ├── variables.tf
│   └── outputs.tf
├── scripts/
├── docs/
└── index.html
```

## 1. Configuração Kubernetes (k8s/)

### k8s/namespaces/production.yaml
```yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Namespace
metadata:
  name: diyapp-production
  labels:
    name: diyapp-production
    environment: production
    managed-by: terraform
---
apiVersion: v1
kind: Namespace
metadata:
  name: diyapp-monitoring
  labels:
    name: diyapp-monitoring
    purpose: monitoring
```

### k8s/deployments/api-deployment.yaml
```yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: diyapp-api
  namespace: diyapp-production
  labels:
    app: diyapp-api
    version: v12
    component: backend
spec:
  replicas: 3
  revisionHistoryLimit: 3
  strategy:
    type: RollingUpdate
    rollingUpdate:
      maxSurge: 1
      maxUnavailable: 0
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: diyapp-api
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: diyapp-api
        version: v12
      annotations:
        prometheus.io/scrape: "true"
        prometheus.io/port: "3000"
        prometheus.io/path: "/metrics"
    spec:
      containers:
      - name: api
        image: diyapp/api:v12
        imagePullPolicy: IfNotPresent
        ports:
        - containerPort: 3000
          name: http
        - containerPort: 3001
          name: metrics
        env:
        - name: NODE_ENV
          value: "production"
        - name: LOG_LEVEL
          value: "info"
        - name: PORT
          value: "3000"
        resources:
          requests:
            memory: "256Mi"
            cpu: "250m"
          limits:
            memory: "512Mi"
            cpu: "500m"
        livenessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health
            port: 3000
          initialDelaySeconds: 30
          periodSeconds: 10
          timeoutSeconds: 5
          failureThreshold: 3
        readinessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /ready
            port: 3000
          initialDelaySeconds: 5
          periodSeconds: 5
          timeoutSeconds: 3
        startupProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health
            port: 3000
          initialDelaySeconds: 10
          periodSeconds: 5
          failureThreshold: 30
        volumeMounts:
        - name: config-volume
          mountPath: /app/config
      volumes:
      - name: config-volume
        configMap:
          name: api-config
---
apiVersion: autoscaling/v2
kind: HorizontalPodAutoscaler
metadata:
  name: diyapp-api-hpa
  namespace: diyapp-production
spec:
  scaleTargetRef:
    apiVersion: apps/v1
    kind: Deployment
    name: diyapp-api
  minReplicas: 3
  maxReplicas: 10
  metrics:
  - type: Resource
    resource:
      name: cpu
      target:
        type: Utilization
        averageUtilization: 70
  - type: Resource
    resource:
      name: memory
      target:
        type: Utilization
        averageUtilization: 80
  behavior:
    scaleDown:
      stabilizationWindowSeconds: 300
      policies:
      - type: Percent
        value: 10
        periodSeconds: 60
    scaleUp:
      stabilizationWindowSeconds: 60
      policies:
      - type: Percent
        value: 100
        periodSeconds: 60
```

### k8s/services/api-service.yaml
```yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
  name: diyapp-api-service
  namespace: diyapp-production
  annotations:
    prometheus.io/scrape: "true"
    prometheus.io/port: "3001"
spec:
  selector:
    app: diyapp-api
  ports:
  - name: http
    port: 80
    targetPort: 3000
    protocol: TCP
  - name: metrics
    port: 3001
    targetPort: 3001
    protocol: TCP
  type: ClusterIP
---
apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
  name: diyapp-api-external
  namespace: diyapp-production
spec:
  selector:
    app: diyapp-api
  ports:
  - port: 443
    targetPort: 3000
    protocol: TCP
  type: LoadBalancer
  loadBalancerIP: ${LOAD_BALANCER_IP}
```

### k8s/configmaps/api-config.yaml
```yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  name: api-config
  namespace: diyapp-production
data:
  NODE_ENV: "production"
  LOG_LEVEL: "info"
  API_TIMEOUT: "30000"
  MAX_BODY_SIZE: "10mb"
  CORS_ORIGIN: "https://diyapp.example.com"
  RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW: "900000"
  RATE_LIMIT_MAX: "100"
  DATABASE_URL: "postgresql://user:pass@postgres:5432/diyapp"
  REDIS_URL: "redis://redis:6379"
  JWT_SECRET: "change-in-production"
  SENTRY_DSN: ""
  NEW_RELIC_LICENSE_KEY: ""
```

### k8s/ingress/production-ingress.yaml
```yaml
apiVersion: networking.k8s.io/v1
kind: Ingress
metadata:
  name: diyapp-ingress
  namespace: diyapp-production
  annotations:
    kubernetes.io/ingress.class: "nginx"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/ssl-redirect: "true"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/force-ssl-redirect: "true"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/proxy-body-size: "10m"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/proxy-read-timeout: "300"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/proxy-send-timeout: "300"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/enable-cors: "true"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/cors-allow-origin: "https://diyapp.example.com"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/cors-allow-methods: "GET, POST, PUT, DELETE, OPTIONS"
    nginx.ingress.kubernetes.io/cors-allow-headers: "DNT,User-Agent,X-Requested-With,If-Modified-Since,Cache-Control,Content-Type,Range,Authorization"
    cert-manager.io/cluster-issuer: "letsencrypt-prod"
spec:
  tls:
  - hosts:
    - api.diyapp.example.com
    secretName: diyapp-tls
  rules:
  - host: api.diyapp.example.com
    http:
      paths:
      - path: /
        pathType: Prefix
        backend:
          service:
            name: diyapp-api-service
            port:
              number: 80
```

## 2. Configuração Serverless (serverless/)

### serverless/functions/api-serverless.yaml
```yaml
AWSTemplateFormatVersion: '2010-09-09'
Transform: AWS::Serverless-2016-10-31
Description: DIYAPP Serverless API

Resources:
  DIYAppApiFunction:
    Type: AWS::Serverless::Function
    Properties:
      FunctionName: diyapp-api-v12
      Description: DIYAPP Main API Function
      Runtime: nodejs18.x
      Handler: index.handler
      CodeUri: ../dist/
      MemorySize: 1024
      Timeout: 30
      Environment:
        Variables:
          NODE_ENV: production
          LOG_LEVEL: info
          DATABASE_URL: !Ref DatabaseSecret
          REDIS_URL: !Sub "redis://${RedisCluster.EndpointAddress}:${RedisCluster.EndpointPort}"
      Events:
        ApiGateway:
          Type: Api
          Properties:
            Path: /{proxy+}
            Method: ANY
            RestApiId: !Ref DIYAppApiGateway
      Policies:
        - AWSLambdaVPCAccessExecutionRole
        - AmazonDynamoDBFullAccess
        - SecretsManagerReadWrite
        - CloudWatchLogsFullAccess
      VpcConfig:
        SecurityGroupIds:
          - !Ref LambdaSecurityGroup
        SubnetIds: !Ref PrivateSubnetIds
      Layers:
        - !Ref NodeModulesLayer
      ReservedConcurrentExecutions: 100
      Tracing: Active

  DIYAppApiGateway:
    Type: AWS::Serverless::Api
    Properties:
      Name: diyapp-api-gateway
      StageName: v12
      Cors:
        AllowMethods: "'GET,POST,PUT,DELETE,OPTIONS'"
        AllowHeaders: "'Content-Type,Authorization,X-Amz-Date,X-Api-Key,X-Amz-Security-Token'"
        AllowOrigin: "'https://diyapp.example.com'"
      Auth:
        DefaultAuthorizer: DIYAppAuthorizer
        AddDefaultAuthorizerToCorsPreflight: false

  NodeModulesLayer:
    Type: AWS::Serverless::LayerVersion
    Properties:
      LayerName: diyapp-node-modules
      Description: Node.js dependencies for DIYAPP
      ContentUri: ../node_modules/
      CompatibleRuntimes:
        - nodejs18.x
      LicenseInfo: MIT
      RetentionPolicy: Retain

  ApiLogGroup:
    Type: AWS::Logs::LogGroup
    Properties:
      LogGroupName: !Sub "/aws/lambda/${DIYAppApiFunction}"
      RetentionInDays: 30

Outputs:
  ApiEndpoint:
    Description: "API Gateway endpoint URL"
    Value: !Sub "https://${DIYAppApiGateway}.execute-api.${AWS::Region}.amazonaws.com/v12/"
  ApiFunctionName:
    Description: "Lambda Function Name"
    Value: !Ref DIYAppApiFunction
```

### serverless/triggers/scheduled-tasks.yaml
```yaml
AWSTemplateFormatVersion: '2010-09-09'
Transform: AWS::Serverless-2016-10-31

Resources:
  CleanupFunction:
    Type: AWS::Serverless::Function
    Properties:
      FunctionName: diyapp-cleanup-v12
      Runtime: nodejs18.x
      Handler: cleanup.handler
      CodeUri: ../dist/tasks/
      MemorySize: 256
      Timeout: 300
      Environment:
        Variables:
          NODE_ENV: production
      Events:
        DailyCleanup:
          Type: Schedule
          Properties:
            Schedule: "cron(0 2 * * ? *)"  # Daily at 2 AM
            Name: daily-cleanup
            Description: "Daily cleanup of temporary data"
        HourlyMetrics:
          Type: Schedule
          Properties:
            Schedule: "rate(1 hour)"
            Name: hourly-metrics
            Description: "Hourly metrics aggregation"

  BackupFunction:
    Type: AWS::Serverless::Function
    Properties:
      FunctionName: diyapp-backup-v12
      Runtime: nodejs18.x
      Handler: backup.handler
      CodeUri: ../dist/tasks/
      MemorySize: 512
      Timeout: 900
      Environment:
        Variables:
          NODE_ENV: production
          BACKUP_BUCKET: !Ref BackupBucket
      Events:
        WeeklyBackup:
          Type: Schedule
          Properties:
            Schedule: "cron(0 3 ? * SUN *)"  # Every Sunday at 3 AM
            Name: weekly-backup
            Description: "Weekly database backup"

  BackupBucket:
    Type: AWS::S3::Bucket
    Properties:
      BucketName: !Sub "diyapp-backups-${AWS::AccountId}"
      LifecycleConfiguration:
        Rules:
          - Id: TransitionToGlacier
            Status: Enabled
            Transitions:
              - TransitionInDays: 30
                StorageClass: GLACIER
          - Id: ExpirationRule
            Status: Enabled
            ExpirationInDays: 365
      VersioningConfiguration:
        Status: Enabled
      Encryption:
        ServerSideEncryptionConfiguration:
          - ServerSideEncryptionByDefault:
              SSEAlgorithm: AES256
```

### monitoring/prometheus/prometheus-config.yaml
```yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: ConfigMap
metadata:
  name: prometheus-config
  namespace: diyapp-monitoring
data:
  prometheus.yml: |
    global:
      scrape_interval: 15s
      evaluation_interval: 15s
      external_labels:
        cluster: 'diyapp-production'
        environment: 'production'

    rule_files:
      - /etc/prometheus/rules/*.yml

    scrape_configs:
      - job_name: 'kubernetes-pods'
        kubernetes_sd_configs:
          - role: pod
        relabel_configs:
          - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_annotation_prometheus_io_scrape]
            action: keep
            regex: true
          - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_annotation_prometheus_io_path]
            action: replace
            target_label: __metrics_path__
            regex: (.+)
          - source_labels: [__address__, __meta_kubernetes_pod_annotation_prometheus_io_port]
            action: replace
            regex: ([^:]+)(?::\d+)?;(\d+)
            replacement: $1:$2
            target_label: __address__
          - action: labelmap
            regex: __meta_kubernetes_pod_label_(.+)
          - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_namespace]
            action: replace
            target_label: kubernetes_namespace
          - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_pod_name]
            action: replace
            target_label: kubernetes_pod_name

      - job_name: 'diyapp-api'
        static_configs:
          - targets: ['diyapp-api-service.diyapp-production.svc.cluster.local:3001']
            labels:
              service: 'diyapp-api'
              component: 'backend'
              version: 'v12'

      - job_name: 'kubernetes-nodes'
        scheme: https
        tls_config:
          ca_file: /var/run/secrets/kubernetes.io/serviceaccount/ca.crt
        bearer_token_file: /var/run/secrets/kubernetes.io/serviceaccount/token
        kubernetes_sd_configs:
          - role: node
        relabel_configs:
          - action: labelmap
            regex: __meta_kubernetes_node_label_(.+)
          - target_label: __address__
            replacement: kubernetes.default.svc:443
          - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_node_name]
            regex: (.+)
            target_label: __metrics_path__
            replacement: /api/v1/nodes/${1}/proxy/metrics

      - job_name: 'kubernetes-cadvisor'
        scheme: https
        tls_config:
          ca_file: /var/run/secrets/kubernetes.io/serviceaccount/ca.crt
        bearer_token_file: /var/run/secrets/kubernetes.io/serviceaccount/token
        kubernetes_sd_configs:
          - role: node
        relabel_configs:
          - action: labelmap
            regex: __meta_kubernetes_node_label_(.+)
          - target_label: __address__
            replacement: kubernetes.default.svc:443
          - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_node_name]
            regex: (.+)
            target_label: __metrics_path__
            replacement: /api/v1/nodes/${1}/proxy/metrics/cadvisor

      - job_name: 'kubernetes-apiservers'
        kubernetes_sd_configs:
          - role: endpoints
        scheme: https
        tls_config:
          ca_file: /var/run/secrets/kubernetes.io/serviceaccount/ca.crt
        bearer_token_file: /var/run/secrets/kubernetes.io/serviceaccount/token
        relabel_configs:
          - source_labels: [__meta_kubernetes_namespace, __meta_kubernetes_service_name, __meta_kubernetes_endpoint_port_name]
            action: keep
            regex: default;kubernetes;https

      - job_name: 'blackbox'
        metrics_path: /probe
        params:
          module: [http_2xx]
        static_configs:
          - targets:
            - https://api.diyapp.example.com/health
            - https://api.diyapp.example.com/ready
        relabel_configs:
          - source_labels: [__address__]
            target_label: __param_target
          - source_labels: [__param_target]
            target_label: instance
          - target_label: __address__
            replacement: blackbox-exporter:9115
```

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Sistema de Design e Protótipos

Vou criar um sistema de design completo com wireframes de alta fidelidade e protótipo interativo para todas as interfaces V12, seguindo rigorosamente os princípios de UX baseado em evidências.

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
DIYAPP-V12-DesignSystem/
├── index.html                    # Dashboard principal do Design System
├── style.css                     # Estilos do Design System
├── design-system.js              # Componentes e funcionalidades
├── prototypes/                   # Protótipos interativos
│   ├── index.html               # Navegador de protótipos
│   ├── dashboard.html           # Protótipo do Dashboard
│   ├── agent-manager.html       # Protótipo do Gerenciador de Agentes
│   ├── hive-mode.html           # Protótipo do Modo Hive
│   └── logs-monitor.html        # Protótipo do Monitor de Logs
├── assets/                       # Recursos visuais
│   ├── icons/                   # Ícones do sistema
│   └── screenshots/             # Capturas de tela
└── documentation/               # Documentação do Design System
    ├── tokens.html              # Tokens de design
    ├── components.html          # Componentes
    └── patterns.html            # Padrões de interação
```

## 2. Design System Components (design-system.js)

```javascript
// DIYAPP V12 Design System - Component Library

class DesignSystem {
  constructor() {
    this.components = {};
    this.init();
  }

  init() {
    this.loadComponents();
    this.setupEventListeners();
    this.initializeAccessibility();
  }

  loadComponents() {
    // Button Component
    this.components.button = {
      primary: {
        base: 'inline-flex items-center justify-center px-4 py-2 rounded-lg font-medium transition-colors focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-offset-2',
        default: 'bg-primary-600 text-white hover:bg-primary-700 focus:ring-primary-500',
        disabled: 'bg-primary-300 text-white cursor-not-allowed',
        loading: 'bg-primary-600 text-white opacity-75 cursor-wait'
      },
      secondary: {
        base: 'inline-flex items-center justify-center px-4 py-2 rounded-lg font-medium transition-colors focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-offset-2',
        default: 'bg-secondary-200 text-secondary-800 hover:bg-secondary-300 focus:ring-secondary-500',
        disabled: 'bg-secondary-100 text-secondary-400 cursor-not-allowed'
      },
      outline: {
        base: 'inline-flex items-center justify-center px-4 py-2 rounded-lg font-medium transition-colors border focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-offset-2',
        default: 'border-secondary-300 text-secondary-700 hover:bg-secondary-50 focus:ring-secondary-500',
        disabled: 'border-secondary-200 text-secondary-400 cursor-not-allowed'
      }
    };

    // Card Component
    this.components.card = {
      base: 'bg-white rounded-xl shadow-md overflow-hidden',
      elevated: 'bg-white rounded-xl shadow-lg overflow-hidden',
      interactive: 'bg-white rounded-xl shadow-md overflow-hidden hover:shadow-lg transition-shadow cursor-pointer'
    };

    // Input Component
    this.components.input = {
      base: 'w-full px-3 py-2 border rounded-lg focus:outline-none focus:ring-2 focus:ring-offset-1 transition-colors',
      default: 'border-secondary-300 text-secondary-900 placeholder-secondary-400 focus:border-primary-500 focus:ring-primary-500',
      error: 'border-error-300 text-secondary-900 placeholder-secondary-400 focus:border-error-500 focus:ring-error-500',
      success: 'border-success-300 text-secondary-900 placeholder-secondary-400 focus:border-success-500 focus:ring-success-500',
      disabled: 'border-secondary-200 bg-secondary-50 text-secondary-500 cursor-not-allowed'
    };

    // Badge Component
    this.components.badge = {
      base: 'inline-flex items-center px-2.5 py-0.5 rounded-full text-xs font-medium',
      default: 'bg-secondary-100 text-secondary-800',
      primary: 'bg-primary-100 text-primary-800',
      success: 'bg-success-100 text-success-800',
      warning: 'bg-warning-100 text-warning-800',
      error: 'bg-error-100 text-error-800'
    };

    // Alert Component
    this.components.alert = {
      base: 'p-4 rounded-lg border',
      info: 'bg-primary-50 border-primary-200 text-primary-800',
      success: 'bg-success-50 border-success-200 text-success-800',
      warning: 'bg-warning-50 border-warning-200 text-warning-800',
      error: 'bg-error-50 border-error-200 text-error-800'
    };
  }

  setupEventListeners() {
    // Setup keyboard navigation for all interactive elements
    document.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
      if (e.key === 'Tab') {
        document.body.classList.add('keyboard-navigation');
      }
    });

    document.addEventListener('mousedown', () => {
      document.body.classList.remove('keyboard-navigation');
    });

    // Setup focus traps for modals
    document.addEventListener('focusin', (e) => {
      const modal = e.target.closest('[role="dialog"]');
      if (modal) {
        this.trapFocus(modal);
      }
    });
  }

  initializeAccessibility() {
    // Add ARIA labels to interactive elements without visible text
    const iconButtons = document.querySelectorAll('button[aria-label=""]');
    iconButtons.forEach(button => {
      const icon = button.querySelector('svg');
      if (icon && icon.getAttribute('aria-hidden') !== 'true') {
        const label = icon.getAttribute('title') || 'Icon button';
        button.setAttribute('aria-label', label);
      }
    });

    // Ensure all images have alt text
    const images = document.querySelectorAll('img:not([alt])');
    images.forEach(img => {
      if (img.getAttribute('role') !== 'presentation') {
        img.setAttribute('alt', '');
      }
    });
  }

  trapFocus(element) {
    const focusableElements = element.querySelectorAll(
      'button, [href], input, select, textarea, [tabindex]:not([tabindex="-1"])'
    );
    
    if (focusableElements.length === 0) return;

    const firstElement = focusableElements[0];
    const lastElement = focusableElements[focusableElements.length - 1];

    element.addEventListener('keydown', (e) => {
      if (e.key !== 'Tab') return;

      if (e.shiftKey) {
        if (document.activeElement === firstElement) {
          lastElement.focus();
          e.preventDefault();
        }
      } else {
        if (document.active

### [Sessão Paralela: Data Engineer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Data Engineering Implementation

## 1. Esquema de Banco de Dados Otimizado V12

```sql
-- File: database/schema/v12_schema.sql
-- Schema otimizado para V12 com particionamento, clustering e histórico

-- ============================================
-- CAMADA RAW (Bronze) - Dados brutos preservados
-- ============================================

CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS raw_v12;

-- Eventos brutos do produto (preserva schema original)
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS raw_v12.events (
    event_id STRING NOT NULL,
    event_type STRING NOT NULL,
    user_id STRING,
    session_id STRING,
    device_info JSON,
    app_version STRING,
    event_timestamp TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    event_data JSON,
    source_system STRING NOT NULL,
    ingested_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(),
    batch_id STRING NOT NULL
)
PARTITION BY DATE(event_timestamp)
CLUSTER BY event_type, source_system
OPTIONS(
    description = 'Tabela raw de eventos - nunca deletar',
    require_partition_filter = true
);

-- Logs de chamadas LLM brutos
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS raw_v12.llm_calls (
    call_id STRING NOT NULL,
    request_id STRING,
    model_name STRING NOT NULL,
    provider STRING NOT NULL,
    feature_name STRING,
    user_id STRING,
    input_tokens INTEGER,
    output_tokens INTEGER,
    total_tokens INTEGER,
    cost_usd NUMERIC,
    latency_ms INTEGER,
    status_code INTEGER,
    request_body JSON,
    response_body JSON,
    error_message STRING,
    call_timestamp TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    ingested_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(),
    batch_id STRING NOT NULL
)
PARTITION BY DATE(call_timestamp)
CLUSTER BY model_name, provider, feature_name
OPTIONS(
    description = 'Tabela raw de chamadas LLM - auditoria completa',
    require_partition_filter = true
);

-- Dados de infraestrutura e métricas
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS raw_v12.infrastructure_metrics (
    metric_id STRING NOT NULL,
    metric_name STRING NOT NULL,
    resource_type STRING NOT NULL,
    resource_id STRING NOT NULL,
    value NUMERIC NOT NULL,
    unit STRING NOT NULL,
    tags JSON,
    collected_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    ingested_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(),
    batch_id STRING NOT NULL
)
PARTITION BY DATE(collected_at)
CLUSTER BY metric_name, resource_type
OPTIONS(
    description = 'Tabela raw de métricas de infraestrutura',
    require_partition_filter = true
);

-- ============================================
-- CAMADA STAGING (Silver) - Limpeza e padronização
-- ============================================

CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS staging_v12;

-- Eventos padronizados
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS staging_v12.events (
    event_id STRING NOT NULL,
    event_type STRING NOT NULL,
    user_id STRING,
    session_id STRING,
    device_type STRING,
    os_version STRING,
    app_version STRING,
    event_timestamp TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    event_date DATE NOT NULL,
    event_hour INTEGER NOT NULL,
    event_data JSON,
    source_system STRING NOT NULL,
    is_valid BOOLEAN NOT NULL,
    validation_errors ARRAY<STRING>,
    processed_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP()
)
PARTITION BY event_date
CLUSTER BY event_type, source_system, is_valid
OPTIONS(
    description = 'Eventos padronizados e validados',
    require_partition_filter = true
);

-- Chamadas LLM padronizadas
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS staging_v12.llm_calls (
    call_id STRING NOT NULL,
    request_id STRING,
    model_name STRING NOT NULL,
    provider STRING NOT NULL,
    feature_category STRING NOT NULL,
    feature_name STRING,
    user_id STRING,
    input_tokens INTEGER,
    output_tokens INTEGER,
    total_tokens INTEGER,
    cost_usd NUMERIC,
    latency_ms INTEGER,
    status STRING NOT NULL,
    is_success BOOLEAN NOT NULL,
    error_type STRING,
    call_timestamp TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    call_date DATE NOT NULL,
    call_hour INTEGER NOT NULL,
    processed_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP()
)
PARTITION BY call_date
CLUSTER BY model_name, provider, feature_category, status
OPTIONS(
    description = 'Chamadas LLM padronizadas com categorização',
    require_partition_filter = true
);

-- ============================================
-- CAMADA MARTS (Gold) - Dados prontos para consumo
-- ============================================

CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS marts_v12;

-- Mart de produto para PM
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS marts_v12.product_daily_metrics (
    metric_date DATE NOT NULL,
    metric_name STRING NOT NULL,
    user_segment STRING,
    feature_name STRING,
    value NUMERIC NOT NULL,
    previous_value NUMERIC,
    change_percentage NUMERIC,
    trend_direction STRING,
    calculated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(),
    PRIMARY KEY(metric_date, metric_name, user_segment, feature_name) NOT ENFORCED
)
PARTITION BY metric_date
CLUSTER BY metric_name, user_segment
OPTIONS(
    description = 'Métricas diárias de produto para PM',
    require_partition_filter = true
);

-- Mart de custo LLM para AI Ops
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS marts_v12.llm_cost_hourly (
    cost_date DATE NOT NULL,
    cost_hour INTEGER NOT NULL,
    model_name STRING NOT NULL,
    provider STRING NOT NULL,
    feature_category STRING NOT NULL,
    feature_name STRING,
    total_calls INTEGER NOT NULL,
    total_input_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    total_output_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    total_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    total_cost_usd NUMERIC NOT NULL,
    avg_latency_ms NUMERIC,
    success_rate NUMERIC,
    p95_latency_ms NUMERIC,
    calculated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP()
)
PARTITION BY cost_date
CLUSTER BY model_name, provider, feature_category
OPTIONS(
    description = 'Custo LLM por hora para AI Ops',
    require_partition_filter = true
);

-- Mart de dados para fine-tuning
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS marts_v12.fine_tuning_datasets (
    dataset_id STRING NOT NULL,
    dataset_name STRING NOT NULL,
    dataset_type STRING NOT NULL,
    model_target STRING NOT NULL,
    total_samples INTEGER NOT NULL,
    avg_tokens_per_sample INTEGER,
    quality_score NUMERIC,
    anonymization_status STRING NOT NULL,
    compliance_approved BOOLEAN NOT NULL,
    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(),
    data_location STRING NOT NULL,
    metadata JSON
)
CLUSTER BY dataset_type, model_target
OPTIONS(
    description = 'Catálogo de datasets para fine-tuning'
);

-- ============================================
-- TABELAS DE CONTROLE E METADADOS
-- ============================================

CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS metadata_v12;

-- Controle de pipelines
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS metadata_v12.pipeline_runs (
    run_id STRING NOT NULL,
    pipeline_name STRING NOT NULL,
    pipeline_type STRING NOT NULL,
    start_time TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    end_time TIMESTAMP,
    status STRING NOT NULL,
    records_processed INTEGER,
    records_failed INTEGER,
    error_message STRING,
    duration_seconds INTEGER,
    batch_id STRING NOT NULL,
    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP()
)
CLUSTER BY pipeline_name, status, DATE(start_time)
OPTIONS(
    description = 'Controle de execução de pipelines'
);

-- Catálogo de dados
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS metadata_v12.data_catalog (
    dataset_id STRING NOT NULL,
    dataset_name STRING NOT NULL,
    schema_name STRING NOT NULL,
    table_name STRING NOT NULL,
    description STRING,
    owner STRING NOT NULL,
    data_domain STRING NOT NULL,
    sla_refresh STRING NOT NULL,
    sla_availability STRING NOT NULL,
    quality_rules JSON,
    pii_level STRING,
    retention_days INTEGER,
    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP(),
    is_active BOOLEAN NOT NULL DEFAULT TRUE,
    PRIMARY KEY(dataset_id) NOT ENFORCED
)
CLUSTER BY data_domain, schema_name
OPTIONS(
    description = 'Catálogo de dados da squad V12'
);

-- Alertas de qualidade
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS metadata_v12.quality_alerts (
    alert_id STRING NOT NULL,
    dataset_id STRING NOT NULL,
    alert_type STRING NOT NULL,
    alert_severity STRING NOT NULL,
    alert_message STRING NOT NULL,
    metric_value NUMERIC,
    threshold_value NUMERIC,
    check_date DATE NOT NULL,
    check_timestamp TIMESTAMP NOT NULL,
    resolved_at TIMESTAMP,
    resolution_notes STRING,
    created_at TIMESTAMP NOT NULL DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP()
)
PARTITION BY check_date
CLUSTER BY alert_type, alert_severity, dataset_id
OPTIONS(
    description = 'Alertas de qualidade de dados'
);
```

## 2. Modelos dbt para Transformação V12

```sql
-- File: dbt/models/staging/stg_events.sql
-- Modelo staging para eventos

{{ config(
    materialized = 'incremental',
    partition_by = {'field': 'event_date', 'data_type': 'date'},
    cluster_by = ['event_type', 'source_system', 'is_valid'],
    unique_key = 'event_id',
    incremental_strategy = 'insert_overwrite'
) }}

WITH raw_events AS (
    SELECT
        event_id,
        event_type,
        user_id,
        session_id,
        device_info,
        app_version,
        event_timestamp,
        event_data,
        source_system,
        ingested_at,
        batch_id
    FROM {{ source('raw_v12', 'events') }}
    WHERE DATE(event_timestamp) >= DATE_SUB(CURRENT_DATE(), INTERVAL 7 DAY)
    {% if is_incremental() %}
        AND DATE(event_timestamp) >= DATE_SUB(DATE('{{ var("run_date") }}'), INTERVAL 2 DAY)
    {% endif %}
),

parsed_events AS (
    SELECT
        event_id,
        event_type,
        user_id,
        session_id,
        -- Extração e padronização de device_info
        JSON_VALUE(device_info, '$.device_type') AS device_type,
        JSON_VALUE(device_info, '$.os_version') AS os_version,
        app_version,
        event_timestamp,
        DATE(event_timestamp) AS event_date,
        EXTRACT(HOUR FROM event_timestamp) AS event_hour,
        event_data,
        source_system,
        ingested_at,
        batch_id,
        -- Validações
        event_id IS NOT NULL AS is_valid_id,
        event_type IS NOT NULL AS is_valid_type,
        event_timestamp IS NOT NULL AS is_valid_timestamp,
        event_timestamp <= CURRENT_TIMESTAMP() AS is_valid_timestamp_range
    FROM raw_events
)

SELECT
    event_id,
    event_type,
    user_id,
    session_id,
    COALESCE(device_type, 'unknown') AS device_type,
    COALESCE(os_version, 'unknown') AS os_version,
    app_version,
    event_timestamp,
    event_date,
    event_hour,
    event_data,
    source_system,
    -- Flag de validade consolidada
    is_valid_id 
    AND is_valid_type 
    AND is_valid_timestamp 
    AND is_valid_timestamp_range AS is_valid,
    -- Coleta de erros de validação
    ARRAY(
        SELECT error
        FROM UNNEST([
            IF(NOT is_valid_id, 'event_id is null', NULL),
            IF(NOT is_valid_type, 'event_type is null', NULL),
            IF(NOT is_valid_timestamp, 'event_timestamp is null', NULL),
            IF(NOT is_valid_timestamp_range, 'event_timestamp is in future', NULL)
        ]) AS error
        WHERE error IS NOT NULL
    ) AS validation_errors,
    CURRENT_TIMESTAMP() AS processed_at
FROM parsed_events
```

```sql
-- File: dbt/models/staging/stg_llm_calls.sql
-- Modelo staging para chamadas LLM

{{ config(
    materialized = 'incremental',
    partition_by = {'field': 'call_date', 'data_type': 'date'},
    cluster_by = ['model_name', 'provider', 'feature_category', 'status'],
    unique_key = 'call_id',
    incremental_strategy = 'insert_overwrite'
) }}

WITH raw_calls AS (
    SELECT
        call_id,
        request_id,
        model_name,
        provider,
        feature_name,
        user_id,
        input_tokens,
        output_tokens,
        total_tokens,
        cost_usd,
        latency_ms,
        status_code,
        request_body,
        response_body,
        error_message,
        call_timestamp,
        ingested_at,
        batch_id
    FROM {{ source('raw_v12', 'llm_calls') }}
    WHERE DATE(call_timestamp) >= DATE_SUB(CURRENT_DATE(), INTERVAL 7 DAY)
    {% if is_incremental() %}
        AND DATE(call_timestamp) >= DATE_SUB(DATE('{{ var("run_date") }}'), INTERVAL 2 DAY)
    {% endif %}
),

categorized_calls AS (
    SELECT
        call_id,
        request_id,
        model_name,
        provider,
        feature_name,
        -- Categorização de features
        CASE 
            WHEN feature_name LIKE '%chat%' THEN 'chat'
            WHEN feature_name LIKE '%summarize%' THEN 'summarization'
            WHEN feature_name LIKE '%translate%' THEN 'translation'
            WHEN feature_name LIKE '%generate%' THEN 'generation'
            WHEN feature_name LIKE '%classify%' THEN 'classification'
            ELSE 'other'
        END AS feature_category,
        user_id,
        input_tokens,
        output_tokens,
        total_tokens,
        cost_usd,
        latency_ms,
        call_timestamp,
        DATE(call_timestamp) AS call_date,
        EXTRACT(HOUR FROM call_timestamp) AS call_hour,
        -- Determinação de status
        CASE 
            WHEN status_code BETWEEN 200 AND 299 THEN 'success'
            WHEN status_code BETWEEN 400 AND 499 THEN 'client_error'
            WHEN status_code BETWEEN 500 AND 599 THEN 'server_error'
            ELSE 'unknown'
        END AS status,
        status_code BETWEEN 200 AND 299 AS is_success,
        -- Classificação de erros
        CASE 
            WHEN error_message LIKE '%timeout%' THEN 'timeout'
            WHEN error_message LIKE '%quota%' THEN 'quota_exceeded'
            WHEN error_message LIKE '%invalid%' THEN 'invalid_request'
            ELSE 'other_error'
        END AS error_type,
        ingested_at,
        batch_id
    FROM raw_calls
)

SELECT
    call_id,
    request_id,
    model_name,
    provider,
    feature_category,
    feature_name,
    user_id,
    COALESCE(input_tokens, 0) AS input_tokens,
    COALESCE(output_tokens, 0) AS output_tokens,
    COALESCE(total_tokens, 0) AS total_tokens,
    COALESCE(cost_usd, 0) AS cost_usd,
    COALESCE(latency_ms, 0) AS latency_ms,
    status,
    is_success,
    error_type,
    call_timestamp,
    call_date,
    call_hour,
    CURRENT_TIMESTAMP() AS processed_at
FROM categorized_calls
```

```sql
-- File: dbt/models/marts/mart_product_daily_metrics.sql
-- Mart de métricas de produto para PM

{{ config(
    materialized = 'table',
    partition_by = {'field': 'metric_date', 'data_type': 'date'},
    cluster_by = ['metric_name', 'user_segment'],
    unique_key = ['metric_date', 'metric_name', 'user_segment', 'feature_name']
) }}

WITH daily_events AS (
    SELECT
        event_date,
        event_type,
        user_id,
        feature_name,
        COUNT(*) AS event_count,
        COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) AS unique_users,
        COUNT(DISTINCT session_id) AS unique_sessions
    FROM {{ ref('stg_events') }}
    WHERE is_valid = TRUE
    GROUP BY 1, 2, 3, 4
),

user_segments AS (
    SELECT
        user_id,
        CASE 
            WHEN COUNT(DISTINCT event_date) >= 20 THEN 'power_user'
            WHEN COUNT(DISTINCT event_date) >= 5 THEN 'regular_user'
            ELSE 'casual_user'
        END AS user_segment
    FROM {{ ref('stg_events') }}
    WHERE is_valid = TRUE
        AND event_date >= DATE_SUB(CURRENT_DATE(), INTERVAL 30 DAY)
    GROUP BY 1
),

feature_adoption AS (
    SELECT
        event_date,
        'feature_adoption' AS metric_name,
        us.user_segment,
        fe.feature_name,
        COUNT(DISTINCT fe.user_id) AS value,
        LAG(COUNT(DISTINCT fe.user_id), 7) OVER (
            PARTITION BY us.user_segment, fe.feature_name 
            ORDER BY event_date
        ) AS previous_value
    FROM {{ ref('stg_events') }} fe
    JOIN user_segments us ON fe.user_id = us.user_id
    WHERE fe.is_valid = TRUE
        AND fe.event_type = 'feature_used'
    GROUP BY 1, 2, 3, 4
),

daily_active_users AS (
    SELECT
        event_date,
        'daily_active_users' AS metric_name,
        us.user_segment,
        NULL AS feature_name,
        COUNT(DISTINCT fe.user_id) AS value,
        LAG(COUNT(DISTINCT fe.user_id), 7) OVER (
            PARTITION BY us.user_segment 
            ORDER BY event_date
        ) AS previous_value
    FROM {{ ref('stg_events') }} fe
    JOIN user_segments us ON fe.user_id = us.user_id
    WHERE fe.is_valid = TRUE
    GROUP

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
```javascript
// ============================================
// DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core Architecture
// Technical Architecture Decision Record (ADR)
// ============================================

// ADR-001: V12 Core Architecture Specification
// Date: 2024-01-15
// Status: ACCEPTED
// Authors: Tech Lead, Infra Specialist, Backend Lead
// ============================================

/**
 * CONTEXT:
 * DIYAPP V11 has scaling limitations due to monolithic architecture.
 * We need a microservices-based architecture that supports:
 * - 100% autonomous squad operations (Hive Mode)
 * - Independent deployment of AI agents
 * - Zero-downtime deployments
 * - Real-time observability
 * - Cost-effective scaling
 */

/**
 * DECISION:
 * Adopt a microservices architecture with:
 * 1. Node.js + Fastify for API services (performance over Express)
 * 2. Next.js 14 (App Router) for frontend with React Server Components
 * 3. Event-driven communication via NATS JetStream
 * 4. Containerized deployment on Kubernetes with GitOps
 * 5. Multi-region PostgreSQL with logical replication
 */

// ============================================
// 1. STACK DEFINITION
// ============================================

const V12_STACK = {
  // Backend Services
  runtime: {
    primary: "Node.js 20.x (LTS)",
    alternatives: ["Bun 1.0 (for performance-critical services)"],
    justification: "Node.js ecosystem maturity, excellent Fastify support"
  },

  // Web Framework
  apiFramework: {
    primary: "Fastify",
    version: "4.x",
    plugins: [
      "@fastify/helmet",      // Security headers
      "@fastify/cors",        // CORS configuration
      "@fastify/rate-limit",  // Rate limiting
      "@fastify/swagger",     // OpenAPI documentation
      "@fastify/metrics"      // Prometheus metrics
    ],
    justification: "2x faster than Express, built-in validation, better async support"
  },

  // Frontend Framework
  frontend: {
    framework: "Next.js 14",
    features: [
      "App Router",
      "React Server Components",
      "Server Actions",
      "Incremental Static Regeneration"
    ],
    styling: "Tailwind CSS + shadcn/ui",
    stateManagement: "Zustand (client) / React Query (server)",
    justification: "Full-stack capabilities, excellent DX, built-in optimizations"
  },

  // Database Layer
  database: {
    primary: "PostgreSQL 16",
    orm: "Prisma 5.x",
    caching: "Redis 7.x (for session/store)",
    vectorDb: "pgvector (for AI embeddings)",
    justification: "Transactional consistency, JSONB support, logical replication"
  },

  // Message Queue
  messaging: {
    primary: "NATS JetStream",
    features: [
      "At-least-once delivery",
      "Stream replication",
      "Durable subscriptions",
      "Key-value store"
    ],
    justification: "Lightweight, cloud-native, excellent Go/Node.js clients"
  },

  // Containerization
  container: {
    runtime: "Docker 24.x",
    baseImage: "node:20-alpine",
    multiStage: true,
    justification: "Small image size, security scanning support"
  },

  // Orchestration
  orchestration: {
    primary: "Kubernetes 1.28",
    ingress: "NGINX Ingress Controller",
    serviceMesh: "Linkerd (for mTLS)",
    justification: "Industry standard, excellent GitOps support"
  },

  // Monitoring & Observability
  observability: {
    metrics: "Prometheus + Grafana",
    tracing: "OpenTelemetry + Jaeger",
    logging: "Loki + Grafana",
    alerting: "AlertManager",
    justification: "CNCF stack, excellent integration"
  },

  // CI/CD Pipeline
  cicd: {
    versionControl: "GitHub",
    ci: "GitHub Actions",
    cd: "ArgoCD (GitOps)",
    registry: "GitHub Container Registry",
    justification: "Single platform, excellent Kubernetes integration"
  }
};

// ============================================
// 2. MICROSERVICES ARCHITECTURE
// ============================================

const MICROSERVICES_ARCHITECTURE = {
  // Core Services (Independent Deployment Units)
  services: [
    {
      name: "api-gateway",
      description: "Entry point for all external requests",
      port: 3000,
      responsibilities: [
        "Request routing",
        "Authentication/Authorization",
        "Rate limiting",
        "Request/Response transformation"
      ],
      tech: ["Fastify", "@fastify/jwt", "@fastify/rate-limit"]
    },
    {
      name: "auth-service",
      description: "Authentication and user management",
      port: 3001,
      responsibilities: [
        "JWT token issuance/validation",
        "User registration/login",
        "OAuth2/OIDC integration",
        "Session management"
      ],
      tech: ["Fastify", "bcrypt", "jsonwebtoken", "PostgreSQL"]
    },
    {
      name: "agent-orchestrator",
      description: "Manages AI agent lifecycle",
      port: 3002,
      responsibilities: [
        "Agent instantiation",
        "Task distribution",
        "Health monitoring",
        "Resource allocation"
      ],
      tech: ["Fastify", "NATS", "Redis", "PostgreSQL"]
    },
    {
      name: "task-processor",
      description: "Processes tasks from AI agents",
      port: 3003,
      responsibilities: [
        "Task queue management",
        "Priority scheduling",
        "Result aggregation",
        "Error handling"
      ],
      tech: ["Fastify", "BullMQ", "Redis", "PostgreSQL"]
    },
    {
      name: "knowledge-base",
      description: "Vector database for agent knowledge",
      port: 3004,
      responsibilities: [
        "Embedding storage",
        "Semantic search",
        "Knowledge retrieval",
        "RAG operations"
      ],
      tech: ["Fastify", "pgvector", "OpenAI API", "PostgreSQL"]
    },
    {
      name: "monitoring-service",
      description: "Collects and aggregates metrics",
      port: 3005,
      responsibilities: [
        "Metrics collection",
        "Health checks",
        "Alert generation",
        "Performance tracking"
      ],
      tech: ["Fastify", "Prometheus", "OpenTelemetry", "NATS"]
    }
  ],

  // Communication Patterns
  communication: {
    synchronous: "REST/GraphQL (for client-facing APIs)",
    asynchronous: "NATS JetStream (for inter-service communication)",
    events: "CloudEvents specification",
    apiVersioning: "URL versioning (v1/, v2/)",
    documentation: "OpenAPI 3.0 + Swagger UI"
  },

  // Data Management
  dataManagement: {
    databasePerService: true,
    sharedDatabases: ["monitoring", "audit"],
    eventSourcing: "For critical business flows",
    cqrs: "For complex write/read separation",
    replication: "Logical replication for reporting"
  }
};

// ============================================
// 3. DEPLOYMENT STRATEGY
// ============================================

const DEPLOYMENT_STRATEGY = {
  // GitOps Workflow
  gitops: {
    repositoryStructure: {
      "apps/": "Application manifests",

      "charts/": "Helm charts"
    },
    syncPolicy: {

    }
  },

  // Kubernetes Configuration
  kubernetes: {

    resourceLimits: {

    },
    scaling: {
      hpa: { min: 2, max: 10, cpu: 70 },
      vpa: { enabled: true, updateMode: "Auto" }
    },

  },

  // Deployment Patterns
  deploymentPatterns: {
    canary: {
      enabled: true,
      steps: ["10%", "25%", "50%", "100%"],

  // Multi-region Strategy

  }
};

// ============================================
// 4. CI/CD PIPELINE
// ============================================

const CICD_PIPELINE = {
  // GitHub Actions Workflow
  workflows: {
    pr: {
      triggers: ["pull_request"],
      steps: [
        "Code linting (ESLint, Prettier)",

      ]
    },
    main: {
      triggers: ["push to main"],
      steps: [

        "Performance tests (k6)",

        "Update ArgoCD manifests",
        "Deploy to staging",
        "Run smoke tests",
        "Auto-approve for production"
      ]
    },
    release: {
      triggers: ["tag v*"],
      steps: [

        "Generate changelog",
        "Create GitHub release",
        "Deploy to production",
        "Run post-deployment verification"
      ]
    }
  },

  // Quality Gates
  qualityGates: {
    testCoverage: "Minimum 80%",
    securityScan: "Zero critical vulnerabilities",
    performance: "P95 latency < 200ms",
    availability: "99.9% SLA"
  },

  // Environment Promotion
  environments: {
    development: {
      autoDeploy: true,
      validation: "Automated tests"
    },

      validation: "Manual approval + automated tests"
    },

      validation: "Manual approval + canary analysis"
    }
  }
};

// ============================================
// 5. CODE STANDARDS & PATTERNS
// ============================================

const CODE_STANDARDS = {
  // TypeScript Configuration
  typescript: {
    strict: true,
    noImplicitAny: true,
    strictNullChecks: true,
    noUnusedLocals: true,
    noUnusedParameters: true
  },

  // Code Structure
  structure: {
    src: {
      "controllers/": "Request handlers",
      "services/": "Business logic",
      "repositories/": "Data access",
      "models/": "Type definitions",
      "middlewares/": "Request middleware",
      "utils/": "Shared utilities",
      "types/": "TypeScript types",
      "tests/": "Test files"
    },
    naming: {
      files: "kebab-case",
      classes: "PascalCase",
      functions: "camelCase",
      constants: "UPPER_SNAKE_CASE",
      interfaces: "I{PascalCase}",
      types: "T{PascalCase}"
    }
  },

  // API Design
  apiDesign: {
    rest: {
      resources: "plural nouns (/users, /posts)",
      actions: "HTTP methods (GET, POST, PUT, DELETE)",
      filtering: "query parameters (?status=active)",
      pagination: "cursor-based with next/prev links",
      versioning: "URL path (/api/v1/resource)"
    },
    graphql: {
      schemaFirst: true,
      codegen: true,
      depthLimit: 10,
      complexityLimit: 1000
    }
  },

  // Error Handling
  errorHandling: {
    httpErrors: {
      400: "BadRequestError",
      401: "UnauthorizedError",
      403: "ForbiddenError",
      404: "NotFoundError",
      409: "ConflictError",
      429: "RateLimitError",
      500: "InternalServerError"
    },
    logging: {
      level: "structured JSON logs",
      context: "requestId, userId, service",
      sensitive: "mask PII data"
    }
  },

  // Testing Strategy
  testing: {
    unit: {
      framework: "Jest",
      coverage: ["functions", "branches", "lines", "statements"],
      mocks: "jest.mock() for external dependencies"
    },
    integration: {
      framework: "Supertest + Jest",
      scope: "API endpoints, database operations",
      cleanup: "Transaction rollback"
    },
    e2e: {
      framework: "Playwright",
      scenarios: ["user journeys", "critical paths"],
      parallel: true
    }
  }
};

// ============================================
// 6. HIVE MODE IMPLEMENTATION
// ============================================

const HIVE_MODE = {
  // Autonomous Squad Configuration
  autonomy: {
    independentDeployment: true,
    dedicatedResources: true,
    crossSquadCommunication: "API contracts + events",
    sharedServices: ["monitoring", "logging", "security"]
  },

  // Agent Architecture
  agents: {
    runtime: "Node.js worker threads",
    isolation: "Docker containers",
    communication: "NATS + Redis pub/sub",
    persistence: "PostgreSQL + Redis",
    lifecycle: {
      spawn: "On-demand by orchestrator",
      terminate: "After task completion or timeout",
      recycle: "Every 24 hours or memory threshold"
    }
  },

  // Resource Management
  resources: {
    cpu: "Burstable QoS class",
    memory: "Limit with swap disabled",
    storage: "Ephemeral for agents, persistent for services",
    network: "Service mesh with mTLS"
  },

  // Failure Recovery
  recovery: {
    circuitBreaker: {
      enabled: true,
      failureThreshold: 5,
      resetTimeout: "30s"
    },
    retry: {
      maxAttempts: 3,
      backoff: "exponential",
      jitter: true
    },
    fallback: {
      enabled: true,
      defaultResponse: "Graceful degradation"
    }
  }
};

// ============================================
// 7. IMPLEMENTATION ROADMAP
// ============================================

const IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP = [
  {
    phase: "Foundation",
    weeks: "1-2",
    deliverables: [
      "Set up monorepo with Turborepo",
      "Configure CI/CD pipeline",
      "Deploy Kubernetes cluster",
      "Set up monitoring stack"
    ]
  },
  {
    phase: "Core Services",
    weeks: "3-4",
    deliverables: [
      "Implement API Gateway",
      "Build Auth Service",
      "Set up PostgreSQL with replication",
      "Deploy NATS cluster"
    ]
  },
  {
    phase: "Agent Platform",
    weeks: "5-6",
    deliverables: [
      "Build Agent Orchestrator",
      "Implement Task Processor",
      "Set up Knowledge Base",
      "Deploy monitoring service"
    ]
  },
  {
    phase: "Hive Mode",
    weeks: "7-8",
    deliverables: [
      "Implement autonomous squad isolation",
      "Set up GitOps workflows",
      "Configure multi-region deployment",
      "Implement canary releases"
    ]
  },
  {
    phase: "Optimization",
    weeks: "9-10",
    deliverables: [
      "Performance tuning",
      "Security hardening",
      "Cost optimization",
      "Documentation completion"
    ]
  }
];

// ============================================
// 8. RISK MITIGATION
// ============================================

const RISK_MITIGATION = {
  technicalRisks: [
    {
      risk: "Microservices complexity overhead",
      mitigation: "Start with bounded contexts, gradual decomposition",
      owner: "Tech Lead"
    },
    {
      risk: "Distributed tracing complexity",
      mitigation: "Implement OpenTelemetry from day 1",
      owner: "Infra Specialist"
    },
    {
      risk: "Database consistency across regions",
      mitigation: "Use logical replication with conflict-free data types",
      owner: "Database Specialist"
    }
  ],
  operationalRisks: [
    {
      risk: "Kubernetes expertise gap",
      mitigation: "Training + managed service (EKS/GKE)",
      owner: "Squad Leader"
    },
    {
      risk: "Cost overrun with multi-region",
      mitigation: "Implement cost monitoring + alerts",
      owner: "PM"
    }
  ]
};

// ============================================
// EXPORT FOR USE IN IMPLEMENTATION
// ============================================

module.exports = {
  V12_STACK,
  MICROSERVICES_ARCHITECTURE,
  DEPLOYMENT_STRATEGY,
  CICD_PIPELINE,
  CODE_STANDARDS,
  HIVE_MODE,
  IMPLEMENTATION_ROADMAP,
  RISK_MITIGATION
};

// ============================================
// ADR CONSEQUENCES
// ============================================

/**
 * POSITIVE CONSEQUENCES:
 * 1. Independent deployment enables Hive Mode autonomy
 * 2. Microservices allow per-service scaling
 * 3. Event-driven architecture improves resilience
 * 4. GitOps ensures reproducible deployments
 * 5. Multi-region support provides disaster recovery
 * 
 * NEGATIVE CONSEQUENCES (trade-offs):
 * 1. Increased operational complexity
 * 2. Higher initial development cost
 * 3. Distributed tracing required for debugging
 * 4. Network latency between services
 * 5. Data consistency challenges
 * 
 * MITIGATION STRATEGIES:
 * 1. Comprehensive monitoring from day 1
 * 2. Gradual migration from monolith
 * 3. Feature flags for controlled rollout
 * 4. Automated testing at all levels
 * 5. Regular architecture reviews

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Sistema de Design

Como UX Designer Sênior da squad, vou criar um sistema de design completo baseado em evidências, com tokens, componentes atômicos e fluxos de usuário críticos. Vou estruturar isso como um sistema de design funcional que pode ser implementado tanto no Figma quanto no código.

// package.json
{
  "name": "core-service",

```javascript
// src/config/env.js
require('dotenv').config();

const env = {
  NODE_ENV: process.env.NODE_ENV || 'development',
  PORT: parseInt(process.env.PORT || '3000', 10),
  JWT_SECRET: process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'your-secret-key-change-in-production',
  JWT_EXPIRES_IN: process.env.JWT_EXPIRES_IN || '24h',
  RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW_MS || '900000', 10), // 15 minutes
  RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS: parseInt(process.env.RATE_LIMIT_MAX_REQUESTS || '100', 10),
  DATABASE_URL: process.env.DATABASE_URL || './database/diyapp.db',
  LOG_LEVEL: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  API_TIMEOUT_MS: parseInt(process.env.API_TIMEOUT_MS || '10000', 10),
  CIRCUIT_BREAKER_THRESHOLD: parseInt(process.env.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_THRESHOLD || '5', 10),
  CIRCUIT_BREAKER_TIMEOUT_MS: parseInt(process.env.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_TIMEOUT_MS || '30000', 10)
};

// Validate required environment variables
const requiredEnvVars = ['JWT_SECRET'];
if (env.NODE_ENV === 'production') {
  requiredEnvVars.forEach((varName) => {
    if (!process.env[varName]) {
      throw new Error(`Missing required environment variable: ${varName}`);
    }
  });
}

module.exports = env;
```

```javascript
// src/utils/logger.js
const pino = require('pino');
const env = require('../config/env');

const logger = pino({
  level: env.LOG_LEVEL,
  transport: env.NODE_ENV === 'development' ? {
    target: 'pino-pretty',
    options: {
      colorize: true,
      translateTime: 'SYS:standard',
      ignore: 'pid,hostname'
    }
  } : undefined,
  serializers: {
    req: (req) => ({
      method: req.method,
      url: req.url,
      correlationId: req.correlationId,
      userAgent: req.headers['user-agent']
    }),
    res: (res) => ({
      statusCode: res.statusCode
    }),
    err: pino.stdSerializers.err
  }
});

// Mask sensitive data in logs
const maskSensitiveData = (obj) => {
  if (!obj || typeof obj !== 'object') return obj;
  
  const masked = { ...obj };
  const sensitiveFields = ['password', 'token', 'jwt', 'authorization', 'email', 'cpf', 'credit_card', 'card_number'];
  
  sensitiveFields.forEach(field => {
    if (masked[field]) {
      masked[field] = '***MASKED***';
    }
  });
  
  return masked;
};

logger.mask = maskSensitiveData;

module.exports = logger;
```

```javascript
// src/middleware/auth.js
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const env = require('../config/env');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');

const authenticate = (req, res, next) => {
  const authHeader = req.headers.authorization;
  
  if (!authHeader || !authHeader.startsWith('Bearer ')) {
    logger.warn({ correlationId: req.correlationId, endpoint: req.path }, 'Missing or invalid Authorization header');
    return res.status(401).json({
      error: 'Unauthorized',
      message: 'Missing or invalid authentication token'
    });
  }
  
  const token = authHeader.substring(7);
  
  try {
    const decoded = jwt.verify(token, env.JWT_SECRET);
    req.user = decoded;
    req.userId = decoded.userId;
    logger.debug({ correlationId: req.correlationId, userId: decoded.userId }, 'User authenticated');
    next();
  } catch (error) {
    logger.warn({ correlationId: req.correlationId, error: error.message }, 'JWT verification failed');
    return res.status(401).json({
      error: 'Unauthorized',
      message: 'Invalid or expired token'
    });
  }
};

const authorize = (requiredRoles) => {
  return (req, res, next) => {
    if (!req.user) {
      return res.status(401).json({
        error: 'Unauthorized',
        message: 'Authentication required'
      });
    }
    
    const userRoles = req.user.roles || [];
    const hasRequiredRole = requiredRoles.some(role => userRoles.includes(role));
    
    if (!hasRequiredRole) {
      logger.warn({
        correlationId: req.correlationId,
        userId: req.userId,
        userRoles,
        requiredRoles,
        endpoint: req.path
      }, 'Authorization failed - insufficient permissions');
      
      return res.status(403).json({
        error: 'Forbidden',
        message: 'Insufficient permissions'
      });
    }
    
    next();
  };
};

module.exports = { authenticate, authorize };
```

```javascript
// src/middleware/validation.js
const Joi = require('joi');
const { validationResult } = require('express-validator');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');

// Common validation schemas
const schemas = {
  auth: {
    login: Joi.object({
      email: Joi.string().email().required(),
      password: Joi.string().min(6).required()
    }),
    register: Joi.object({
      email: Joi.string().email().required(),
      password: Joi.string().min(6).required(),
      name: Joi.string().min(2).required()
    })
  },
  user: {
    update: Joi.object({
      name: Joi.string().min(2),
      email: Joi.string().email()
    }).min(1)
  }
};

const validate = (schema, property = 'body') => {
  return (req, res, next) => {
    const { error } = schema.validate(req[property], { abortEarly: false });
    
    if (error) {
      const errors = error.details.map(detail => ({
        field: detail.path.join('.'),
        message: detail.message
      }));
      
      logger.debug({
        correlationId: req.correlationId,
        endpoint: req.path,
        errors: logger.mask(errors)
      }, 'Validation failed');
      
      return res.status(400).json({
        error: 'Validation Error',
        message: 'Invalid input data',
        details: errors
      });
    }
    
    next();
  };
};

const validateExpressValidator = (req, res, next) => {
  const errors = validationResult(req);
  
  if (!errors.isEmpty()) {
    const formattedErrors = errors.array().map(err => ({
      field: err.path,
      message: err.msg
    }));
    
    logger.debug({
      correlationId: req.correlationId,
      endpoint: req.path,
      errors: logger.mask(formattedErrors)
    }, 'Validation failed');
    
    return res.status(400).json({
      error: 'Validation Error',
      message: 'Invalid input data',
      details: formattedErrors
    });
  }
  
  next();
};

module.exports = { schemas, validate, validateExpressValidator };
```

```javascript
// src/middleware/resilience.js
const CircuitBreaker = require('circuit-breaker-js');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');
const env = require('../config/env');

class ResilienceManager {
  constructor() {
    this.circuitBreakers = new Map();
    this.defaultOptions = {
      timeoutMs: env.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_TIMEOUT_MS,
      threshold: env.CIRCUIT_BREAKER_THRESHOLD
    };
  }

  getCircuitBreaker(serviceName, options = {}) {
    const key = serviceName;
    
    if (!this.circuitBreakers.has(key)) {
      const breakerOptions = { ...this.defaultOptions, ...options };
      
      const breaker = new CircuitBreaker({
        timeoutDuration: breakerOptions.timeoutMs,
        volumeThreshold: breakerOptions.threshold,
        onCircuitOpen: (metrics) => {
          logger.warn({
            serviceName,
            metrics,
            state: 'OPEN'
          }, `Circuit breaker opened for ${serviceName}`);
        },
        onCircuitClose: () => {
          logger.info({ serviceName, state: 'CLOSED' }, `Circuit breaker closed for ${serviceName}`);
        }
      });
      
      this.circuitBreakers.set(key, breaker);
    }
    
    return this.circuitBreakers.get(key);
  }

  async executeWithResilience(serviceName, operation, fallback, options = {}) {
    const breaker = this.getCircuitBreaker(serviceName, options);
    
    try {
      return await breaker.run(operation);
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error({
        serviceName,
        error: error.message,
        correlationId: error.correlationId
      }, `Service ${serviceName} failed, using fallback`);
      
      if (fallback) {
        return fallback(error);
      }
      
      throw error;
    }
  }
}

const resilienceManager = new ResilienceManager();

// HTTP client with resilience
const axios = require('axios');
const axiosInstance = axios.create({
  timeout: env.API_TIMEOUT_MS
});

axiosInstance.interceptors.request.use((config) => {
  config.metadata = { startTime: Date.now() };
  return config;
});

axiosInstance.interceptors.response.use(
  (response) => {
    const endTime = Date.now();
    const duration = endTime - response.config.metadata.startTime;
    
    logger.debug({
      url: response.config.url,
      method: response.config.method,
      status: response.status,
      durationMs: duration
    }, 'External API call successful');
    
    return response;
  },
  async (error) => {
    const endTime = Date.now();
    const duration = endTime - (error.config?.metadata?.startTime || endTime);
    
    logger.error({
      url: error.config?.url,
      method: error.config?.method,
      status: error.response?.status,
      durationMs: duration,
      error: error.message
    }, 'External API call failed');
    
    // Retry logic for transient errors
    if (error.code === 'ECONNABORTED' || error.response?.status >= 500) {
      if (!error.config.retryCount) {
        error.config.retryCount = 0;
      }
      
      if (error.config.retryCount < 3) {
        error.config.retryCount++;
        const delay = Math.pow(2, error.config.retryCount) * 1000 + Math.random() * 1000;
        
        logger.info({
          url: error.config.url,
          retryCount: error.config.retryCount,
          delayMs: delay
        }, 'Retrying failed request');
        
        await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, delay));
        return axiosInstance(error.config);
      }
    }
    
    return Promise.reject(error);
  }
);

module.exports = { resilienceManager, axiosInstance };
```

```javascript
// src/database/knex.js
const knex = require('knex');
const env = require('../config/env');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');

const db = knex({
  client: 'sqlite3',
  connection: {
    filename: env.DATABASE_URL
  },
  useNullAsDefault: true,
  log: {
    warn(message) {
      logger.warn({ source: 'knex' }, message);
    },
    error(message) {
      logger.error({ source: 'knex' }, message);
    },
    deprecate(message) {
      logger.warn({ source: 'knex' }, message);
    },
    debug(message) {
      logger.debug({ source: 'knex' }, message);
    }
  }
});

// Test connection
db.raw('SELECT 1')
  .then(() => {
    logger.info('Database connection established');
  })
  .catch((error) => {
    logger.error({ error: error.message }, 'Failed to connect to database');
    process.exit(1);
  });

module.exports = db;
```

    table.string('email').unique().notNullable();
    table.string('password_hash').notNullable();
    table.string('name').notNullable();

    table.uuid('id').primary().defaultTo(knex.raw('(UUID())'));
    table.uuid('user_id').references('id').inTable('users').onDelete('CASCADE');
    table.string('token').notNullable();
    table.string('user_agent');
    table.string('ip_address');
    table.timestamp('expires_at').notNullable();
    table.timestamp('created_at').defaultTo(knex.fn.now());
    
    table.index(['user_id']);
    table.index(['token']);
    table.index(['expires_at']);
  });
};

exports.down = function(knex) {
  return knex.schema.dropTable('sessions');
};

```javascript
// src/database/migrations/run-migrations.js
const knex = require('../knex');
const logger = require('../../utils/logger');

async function runMigrations(direction) {
  try {
    logger.info(`Running migrations ${direction}...`);
    
    if (direction === 'up') {
      await knex.migrate.latest();
      logger.info('Migrations completed successfully');
    } else if (direction === 'down') {
      await knex.migrate.rollback(undefined, true);
      logger.info('Rollback completed successfully');
    } else {
      throw new Error('Invalid direction. Use "up" or "down"');
    }
    
    process.exit(0);
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error({ error: error.message }, 'Migration failed');
    process.exit(1);
  }
}

const direction = process.argv[2];
if (!['up', 'down'].includes(direction)) {
  logger.error('Please specify migration direction: "up" or "down"');
  process.exit(1);
}

runMigrations(direction);
```

```javascript
// src/repositories/user.repository.js
const db = require('../database/knex');
const logger = require('../utils/logger');

class UserRepository {
  async create(userData) {
    const [user] = await db('users')
      .insert(userData)
      .returning('*');
    
    logger.debug({ userId: user.id }, 'User created');
    return user;
  }

  async findByEmail(email) {
    const user = await db('users')
      .where('email', email)
      .andWhere('is_active', true)
      .first();
    
    return user;
  }

  async findById(id) {
    const user = await db('users')
      .where('id', id)
      .andWhere('is_active', true)
      .first();
    
    return user;
  }

  async update(id, updates) {
    const [user] = await db('users')
      .where('id', id)
      .update({
        ...updates,
        updated_at: db.fn.now()
      })
      .returning('*');
    
    logger.debug({ userId: id }, 'User updated');
    return user;
  }

  async delete(id) {
    await db('users')
      .where('id', id)
      .update({ is_active: false, updated_at: db.fn.now() });
    
    logger.debug({ userId: id }, 'User soft deleted');
    return true;
  }
}

module.exports = new UserRepository();
```

    {
      "files": ["**/*.stories.*"],

        "import/no-anonymous-default-export": "off"
      }
    }
  ]
}

import type { Preview } from '@storybook/react'
import '../src/app/globals.css'
import { ThemeProvider } from '../src/components/providers/ThemeProvider'

const preview: Preview = {
  parameters: {
    actions: { argTypesRegex: '^on[A-Z].*' },
    controls: {
      matchers: {
        color: /(background|color)$/i,
        date: /Date$/i,
      },
    },
    layout: 'fullscreen',
    backgrounds: {
      default: 'light',
      values: [
        { name: 'light', value: '#ffffff' },
        { name: 'dark', value: '#0a0a0a' },
      ],
    },
    a11y: {
      config: {
        rules: [
          {
            id: 'color-contrast',
            enabled: true,
          },
        ],
      },
    },
  },
  decorators: [
    (Story) => (
      <ThemeProvider attribute="class" defaultTheme="system" enableSystem>
        <div className="min-h-screen bg-background">
          <Story />
        </div>
      </ThemeProvider>
    ),
  ],
}

export default preview
