### [Sessão Paralela: Data Engineer]
```sql
-- ============================================
-- DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core
-- Database Schema and Initial Migration
-- Data Engineer: Senior Squad
-- ============================================

-- ============================================
-- 1. DATABASE CREATION (Production)
-- ============================================

-- Create main database
CREATE DATABASE diyapp_v12_prod
    WITH 
    OWNER = postgres
    ENCODING = 'UTF8'
    LC_COLLATE = 'en_US.UTF-8'
    LC_CTYPE = 'en_US.UTF-8'
    CONNECTION LIMIT = 100;

-- Create staging database
CREATE DATABASE diyapp_v12_staging
    WITH 
    OWNER = postgres
    ENCODING = 'UTF8'
    LC_COLLATE = 'en_US.UTF-8'
    LC_CTYPE = 'en_US.UTF-8'
    CONNECTION LIMIT = 50;

-- ============================================
-- 2. SCHEMA STRUCTURE
-- ============================================

-- Connect to production database
\c diyapp_v12_prod

-- Create schemas for data layers (dbt architecture)
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS raw;
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS staging;
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS marts;
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS audit;
CREATE SCHEMA IF NOT EXISTS config;

-- Set search path
SET search_path TO raw, staging, marts, audit, config, public;

-- ============================================
-- 3. RAW LAYER (bronze) - Untouched source data
-- ============================================

-- Application events (from product)
CREATE TABLE raw.app_events (
    event_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id UUID NOT NULL,
    session_id UUID NOT NULL,
    event_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    event_name VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    event_timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    event_properties JSONB,
    device_info JSONB,
    app_version VARCHAR(20),
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    source_file VARCHAR(500),
    ingestion_batch_id UUID NOT NULL
);

-- LLM Gateway calls
CREATE TABLE raw.llm_calls (
    call_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    request_id UUID NOT NULL,
    user_id UUID,
    feature_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    model_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    input_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    output_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    total_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL,
    cost_usd DECIMAL(10,6),
    latency_ms INTEGER,
    status_code INTEGER,
    error_message TEXT,
    request_timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    response_timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ,
    request_body JSONB,
    response_body JSONB,
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    ingestion_batch_id UUID NOT NULL
);

-- API Gateway logs
CREATE TABLE raw.api_logs (
    log_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    request_id UUID NOT NULL,
    user_id UUID,
    endpoint VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,
    method VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    status_code INTEGER NOT NULL,
    response_time_ms INTEGER,
    request_size_bytes INTEGER,
    response_size_bytes INTEGER,
    user_agent TEXT,
    ip_address INET,
    request_timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    ingestion_batch_id UUID NOT NULL
);

-- User data (from auth system)
CREATE TABLE raw.users (
    user_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    email VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    username VARCHAR(100),
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    last_login_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    subscription_tier VARCHAR(50),
    country_code CHAR(2),
    language_code CHAR(5),
    metadata JSONB,
    source_system VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    ingestion_timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    ingestion_batch_id UUID NOT NULL
);

-- ============================================
-- 4. STAGING LAYER (silver) - Cleaned and standardized
-- ============================================

-- Cleaned app events
CREATE TABLE staging.stg_app_events (
    event_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    user_id UUID NOT NULL,
    session_id UUID NOT NULL,
    event_type VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    event_name VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    event_timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    event_date DATE GENERATED ALWAYS AS (event_timestamp::DATE) STORED,
    event_hour INTEGER GENERATED ALWAYS AS (EXTRACT(HOUR FROM event_timestamp)) STORED,
    event_properties JSONB,
    device_type VARCHAR(50),
    os_version VARCHAR(50),
    app_version VARCHAR(20),
    is_mobile BOOLEAN,
    country_code CHAR(2),
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    ingestion_batch_id UUID NOT NULL,
    cleaned_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Cleaned LLM calls
CREATE TABLE staging.stg_llm_calls (
    call_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    request_id UUID NOT NULL,
    user_id UUID,
    feature_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    model_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    input_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL CHECK (input_tokens >= 0),
    output_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL CHECK (output_tokens >= 0),
    total_tokens INTEGER NOT NULL CHECK (total_tokens >= 0),
    cost_usd DECIMAL(10,6) CHECK (cost_usd >= 0),
    latency_ms INTEGER CHECK (latency_ms >= 0),
    status_code INTEGER,
    is_success BOOLEAN GENERATED ALWAYS AS (status_code::TEXT LIKE '2%') STORED,
    error_category VARCHAR(50),
    request_date DATE GENERATED ALWAYS AS (request_timestamp::DATE) STORED,
    request_hour INTEGER GENERATED ALWAYS AS (EXTRACT(HOUR FROM request_timestamp)) STORED,
    request_timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    response_timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ,
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    ingestion_batch_id UUID NOT NULL,
    cleaned_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Cleaned users
CREATE TABLE staging.stg_users (
    user_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    email VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    username VARCHAR(100),
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    last_login_at TIMESTAMPTZ,
    subscription_tier VARCHAR(50),
    country_code CHAR(2),
    language_code CHAR(5),
    days_since_created INTEGER GENERATED ALWAYS AS (DATE_PART('day', NOW() - created_at)) STORED,
    is_active BOOLEAN GENERATED ALWAYS AS (last_login_at > NOW() - INTERVAL '30 days') STORED,
    metadata JSONB,
    source_system VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    ingestion_timestamp TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    ingestion_batch_id UUID NOT NULL,
    cleaned_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- ============================================
-- 5. MARTS LAYER (gold) - Business-ready data
-- ============================================

-- Product metrics for PM
CREATE TABLE marts.mart_product_daily (
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    user_id UUID NOT NULL,
    -- Engagement metrics
    total_sessions INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    total_events INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    session_duration_seconds INTEGER,
    -- Feature adoption
    feature_llm_calls INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    feature_image_gen INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    feature_code_gen INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    feature_chat INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    -- Funnel metrics
    signups INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    activations INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    conversions INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    churns INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    -- User state
    subscription_tier VARCHAR(50),
    country_code CHAR(2),
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    -- Calculated fields
    events_per_session DECIMAL(5,2),
    llm_calls_per_session DECIMAL(5,2),
    PRIMARY KEY (date, user_id)
) PARTITION BY RANGE (date);

-- LLM cost and usage for AI Ops
CREATE TABLE marts.mart_llm_daily (
    date DATE NOT NULL,
    feature_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    model_name VARCHAR(100) NOT NULL,
    provider VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    -- Usage metrics
    total_calls INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    successful_calls INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    failed_calls INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    -- Token consumption
    total_input_tokens BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
    total_output_tokens BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
    total_tokens BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
    -- Cost metrics
    total_cost_usd DECIMAL(12,6) DEFAULT 0,
    avg_cost_per_call DECIMAL(10,6),
    -- Performance
    avg_latency_ms DECIMAL(10,2),
    p95_latency_ms INTEGER,
    p99_latency_ms INTEGER,
    -- Error analysis
    error_rate DECIMAL(5,4),
    top_error_category VARCHAR(50),
    PRIMARY KEY (date, feature_name, model_name, provider)
) PARTITION BY RANGE (date);

-- Operational metrics for SRE
CREATE TABLE marts.mart_ops_hourly (
    timestamp_hour TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    endpoint VARCHAR(500) NOT NULL,
    method VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    -- Volume metrics
    request_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    user_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    -- Performance
    avg_response_time_ms DECIMAL(10,2),
    p95_response_time_ms INTEGER,
    p99_response_time_ms INTEGER,
    -- Success rates
    success_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    error_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    error_rate DECIMAL(5,4),
    -- Traffic
    total_request_bytes BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
    total_response_bytes BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
    avg_request_size_bytes INTEGER,
    avg_response_size_bytes INTEGER,
    PRIMARY KEY (timestamp_hour, endpoint, method)
) PARTITION BY RANGE (timestamp_hour);

-- ============================================
-- 6. AUDIT AND CONFIGURATION SCHEMAS
-- ============================================

-- Pipeline execution logs
CREATE TABLE audit.pipeline_runs (
    run_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    pipeline_name VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    status VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL CHECK (status IN ('started', 'success', 'failed', 'warning')),
    start_time TIMESTAMPTZ NOT NULL,
    end_time TIMESTAMPTZ,
    duration_seconds INTEGER,
    rows_processed INTEGER,
    rows_failed INTEGER,
    error_message TEXT,
    config JSONB,
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Data quality test results
CREATE TABLE audit.data_quality_tests (
    test_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    run_id UUID REFERENCES audit.pipeline_runs(run_id),
    table_name VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    test_name VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    test_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    status VARCHAR(20) NOT NULL CHECK (status IN ('passed', 'failed', 'warning')),
    column_name VARCHAR(200),
    expected_value TEXT,
    actual_value TEXT,
    threshold DECIMAL(10,4),
    actual_percent DECIMAL(10,4),
    failed_rows JSONB,
    executed_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- SLA monitoring
CREATE TABLE audit.sla_monitoring (
    sla_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    dataset_name VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL,
    consumer_role VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    expected_update_frequency VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    max_delay_minutes INTEGER NOT NULL,
    last_successful_update TIMESTAMPTZ,
    next_expected_update TIMESTAMPTZ,
    current_delay_minutes INTEGER GENERATED ALWAYS AS (
        CASE 
            WHEN last_successful_update IS NULL THEN NULL
            ELSE EXTRACT(EPOCH FROM (NOW() - last_successful_update)) / 60
        END
    ) STORED,
    is_violated BOOLEAN GENERATED ALWAYS AS (
        CASE 
            WHEN last_successful_update IS NULL THEN TRUE
            ELSE (EXTRACT(EPOCH FROM (NOW() - last_successful_update)) / 60) > max_delay_minutes
        END
    ) STORED,
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- Configuration for data pipelines
CREATE TABLE config.pipeline_config (
    config_id UUID PRIMARY KEY,
    pipeline_name VARCHAR(200) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
    source_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    source_config JSONB NOT NULL,
    schedule_cron VARCHAR(50),
    enabled BOOLEAN DEFAULT TRUE,
    sla_minutes INTEGER NOT NULL,
    alert_emails TEXT[],
    dbt_model_path VARCHAR(500),
    created_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW(),
    updated_at TIMESTAMPTZ DEFAULT NOW()
);

-- ============================================
-- 7. INDEXES FOR PERFORMANCE
-- ============================================

-- Raw layer indexes
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_app_events_timestamp ON raw.app_events(event_timestamp);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_app_events_user ON raw.app_events(user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_llm_calls_timestamp ON raw.llm_calls(request_timestamp);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_llm_calls_user_feature ON raw.llm_calls(user_id, feature_name);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_api_logs_timestamp ON raw.api_logs(request_timestamp);
CREATE INDEX idx_raw_api_logs_endpoint ON raw.api_logs(endpoint);

-- Staging layer indexes
CREATE INDEX idx_stg_events_date_user ON staging.stg_app_events(event_date, user_id);
CREATE INDEX idx_stg_llm_date_feature ON staging.stg_llm_calls(request_date, feature_name);
CREATE INDEX idx_stg_users_active ON staging.stg_users(is_active);

-- Marts layer indexes
CREATE INDEX idx_mart_product_date ON marts.mart_product_daily(date);
CREATE INDEX idx_mart_llm_date_provider ON marts.mart_llm_daily(date, provider);
CREATE INDEX idx_mart_ops_hour_endpoint ON marts.mart_ops_hourly(timestamp_hour, endpoint);

-- Audit indexes
CREATE INDEX idx_pipeline_runs_status ON audit.pipeline_runs(status, start_time);
CREATE INDEX idx_quality_tests_run ON audit.data_quality_tests(run_id, status);
CREATE INDEX idx_sla_violations ON audit.sla_monitoring(is_violated);

-- ============================================
-- 8. PARTITIONING SETUP
-- ============================================

-- Create monthly partitions for current year + next year
DO $$
DECLARE
    month_date DATE;
    partition_name TEXT;
    start_date DATE := DATE_TRUNC('year', CURRENT_DATE);
    end_date DATE := start_date + INTERVAL '2 years';
BEGIN
    WHILE start_date < end_date LOOP
        month_date := start_date;
        
        -- mart_product_daily partitions
        partition_name := 'mart_product_daily_' || TO_CHAR(month_date, 'YYYY_MM');
        EXECUTE format('
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS marts.%I 
            PARTITION OF marts.mart_product_daily
            FOR VALUES FROM (%L) TO (%L)',
            partition_name,
            month_date,
            month_date + INTERVAL '1 month'
        );
        
        -- mart_llm_daily partitions
        partition_name := 'mart_llm_daily_' || TO_CHAR(month_date, 'YYYY_MM');
        EXECUTE format('
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS marts.%I 
            PARTITION OF marts.mart_llm_daily
            FOR VALUES FROM (%L) TO (%L)',
            partition_name,
            month_date,
            month_date + INTERVAL '1 month'
        );
        
        -- mart_ops_hourly partitions
        partition_name := 'mart_ops_hourly_' || TO_CHAR(month_date, 'YYYY_MM');
        EXECUTE format('
            CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS marts.%I 
            PARTITION OF marts.mart_ops_hourly
            FOR VALUES FROM (%L) TO (%L)',
            partition_name,
            month_date,
            month_date + INTERVAL '1 month'
        );
        
        start_date := start_date + INTERVAL '1 month';
    END LOOP;
END $$;

-- ============================================
-- 9. VIEWS FOR COMMON QUERIES
-- ============================================

-- View for PM dashboard (daily metrics)
CREATE VIEW marts.vw_pm_dashboard AS
SELECT 
    date,
    COUNT(DISTINCT user_id) as daily_active_users,
    SUM(total_sessions) as total_sessions,
    SUM(total_events) as total_events,
    AVG(session_duration_seconds) as avg_session_duration,
    SUM(feature_llm_calls) as total_llm_calls,
    SUM(feature_image_gen) as total_image_gen,
    SUM(feature_code_gen) as total_code_gen,
    SUM(signups) as new_signups,
    SUM(activations) as activations,
    SUM(churns) as churns
FROM marts.mart_product_daily
WHERE date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '30 days'
GROUP BY date
ORDER BY date DESC;

-- View for AI Ops cost dashboard
CREATE VIEW marts.vw_ai_ops_cost AS
SELECT 
    date,
    provider,
    model_name,
    SUM(total_cost_usd) as daily_cost,
    SUM(total_tokens) as daily_tokens,
    SUM(total_calls) as daily_calls,
    AVG(avg_latency_ms) as avg_latency,
    error_rate
FROM marts.mart_llm_daily
WHERE date >= CURRENT_DATE - INTERVAL '7 days'
GROUP BY date, provider, model_name, error_rate
ORDER BY date DESC, daily_cost DESC;

-- View for SRE reliability dashboard
CREATE VIEW marts.vw_sre_reliability AS
SELECT 
    DATE_TRUNC('day', timestamp_hour) as date,
    endpoint,
    SUM(request_count) as total_requests,
    AVG(avg_response_time_ms) as avg_response_time,
    MAX(p99_response_time_ms) as p99_response_time,
    SUM(error_count) as total_errors,
    AVG(error_rate) as avg_error_rate
FROM marts.mart_ops_hourly
WHERE

### [Sessão Paralela: Tech Leader]
```javascript
// ============================================
// DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core Architecture
// Tech Lead: Arquitetura de Sistema Autônomo
// ============================================

// ADR-001: Stack Principal V12
// Data: 2024-01-15
// Status: Aceita
// Autores: Tech Lead + Especialista Infra

/**
 * CONTEXTO:
 * A V11 enfrentou problemas de escalabilidade com monólito Node.js/Express.
 * Necessidade de deploy independente por funcionalidade, alta disponibilidade,
 * e suporte a múltiplos agentes IA rodando em paralelo.
 * 
 * DECISÃO:
 * Adotar arquitetura de microsserviços com:
 * - Backend: Node.js 20+ com Fastify (performance + schema validation)
 * - Frontend: React 18 + Next.js 14 (App Router, Server Components)
 * - Banco: PostgreSQL (dados relacionais) + Redis (cache/sessões)
 * - Mensageria: RabbitMQ para comunicação entre serviços
 * - Containerização: Docker + Kubernetes para orquestração
 * 
 * OPÇÕES CONSIDERADAS:
 * - Opção A: NestJS + GraphQL - Prós: Type-safe, estrutura robusta
 *   Contras: Overhead para microsserviços simples, curva de aprendizado
 * - Opção B: Fastify + REST - Prós: Performance extrema, simples, schema validation
 *   Contras: Menos "batteries included" que NestJS
 * - Opção escolhida: B - Justificativa: Performance crítica para agentes IA,
 *   microsserviços devem ser leves e focados
 * 
 * CONSEQUÊNCIAS:
 * Positivas: Alta performance, baixa latência, escalabilidade horizontal fácil
 * Negativas: Mais serviços para gerenciar, necessidade de service discovery
 * Riscos: Complexidade distribuída - Mitigar com observabilidade robusta
 */

// ============================================
// Engineering Standards V12
// ============================================

const engineeringStandards = {
  // 1. ESTRUTURA DE REPOSITÓRIO
  repositoryStructure: {
    monorepo: true,
    packages: [
      'apps/web',           // Next.js frontend
      'apps/api-gateway',   // Gateway principal
      'services/auth',      // Autenticação JWT
      'services/agent-core',// Núcleo dos agentes IA
      'services/task-queue',// Filas de tarefas
      'services/notification',// WhatsApp/Email
      'libs/shared',        // Código compartilhado
      'libs/database',      // Models/ORM
    ],
    configs: {
      'docker-compose.yml': 'Desenvolvimento local',
      'k8s/': 'Manifests Kubernetes',
      '.github/workflows/': 'CI/CD',
      'docs/adrs/': 'Decisões arquiteturais'
    }
  },

  // 2. PADRÕES DE CÓDIGO
  codingStandards: {
    language: 'TypeScript strict mode',
    linter: 'ESLint + Airbnb config',
    formatter: 'Prettier',
    naming: {
      files: 'kebab-case',
      components: 'PascalCase',
      variables: 'camelCase',
      constants: 'SCREAMING_SNAKE_CASE'
    },
    imports: {
      order: 'builtin → external → internal',
      noRelativePaths: 'Usar alias @lib/*, @services/*'
    }
  },

  // 3. CONTRATOS DE API
  apiStandards: {
    versioning: 'URL path (/api/v1/*)',
    responseFormat: {
      success: {
        data: 'T',
        meta: { timestamp: 'ISO string', requestId: 'string' }
      },
      error: {
        error: { code: 'string', message: 'string', details: 'object' },
        meta: { timestamp: 'ISO string', requestId: 'string' }
      }
    },
    validation: 'Zod schemas em todos os endpoints',
    documentation: 'OpenAPI 3.0 (Swagger) auto-gerada'
  },

  // 4. ESTRATÉGIA DE BRANCHING
  gitStrategy: {
    workflow: 'GitHub Flow',
    branches: {
      main: 'Deploy automático para produção',
      develop: 'Integração contínua',
      feature: 'feature/* (deletar após merge)',
      hotfix: 'hotfix/* (merge em main + develop)'
    },
    commits: 'Conventional Commits',
    prTitles: [
      'feat: Nova funcionalidade',
      'fix: Correção de bug',
      'docs: Documentação',
      'refactor: Refatoração sem mudança funcional',
      'test: Adição/ajuste de testes',
      'chore: Tarefas de build/dependências'
    ]
  },

  // 5. TESTES
  testingStandards: {
    coverage: {
      minimum: 80,
      criticalPaths: 90
    },
    levels: {
      unit: 'Jest + Supertest',
      integration: 'Testes entre serviços',
      e2e: 'Cypress para frontend'
    },
    mocks: {
      externalApis: 'MSW (Mock Service Worker)',
      database: 'Test containers'
    }
  },

  // 6. SEGURANÇA
  securityStandards: {
    authentication: 'JWT com refresh tokens',
    authorization: 'RBAC por squad/agent',
    secrets: 'HashiCorp Vault ou AWS Secrets Manager',
    headers: {
      'X-Content-Type-Options': 'nosniff',
      'X-Frame-Options': 'DENY',
      'Strict-Transport-Security': 'max-age=31536000'
    },
    validation: {
      input: 'Sanitização XSS em todos os inputs',
      output: 'Escape HTML em respostas'
    }
  }
};

// ============================================
// Microsserviços Architecture
// ============================================

const microservicesArchitecture = {
  // SERVIÇO: API Gateway
  apiGateway: {
    technology: 'Fastify + @fastify/cors + @fastify/rate-limit',
    responsibilities: [
      'Routing para microsserviços',
      'Rate limiting por IP/usuário',
      'CORS configuration',
      'Request/response logging',
      'Circuit breaker pattern'
    ],
    endpoints: {
      public: '/api/v1/public/*',
      agents: '/api/v1/agents/*',
      tasks: '/api/v1/tasks/*',
      admin: '/api/v1/admin/*'
    },
    deployment: {
      replicas: 2,
      resources: { cpu: '500m', memory: '512Mi' }
    }
  },

  // SERVIÇO: Agent Core
  agentCore: {
    technology: 'Fastify + LangChain.js + OpenAI SDK',
    responsibilities: [
      'Orquestração de agentes IA',
      'Gerenciamento de contexto',
      'Processamento de prompts',
      'Validação de respostas',
      'Logging de interações'
    ],
    communication: {
      sync: 'REST (via API Gateway)',
      async: 'RabbitMQ (tarefas longas)'
    },
    scaling: {
      strategy: 'Horizontal (por tipo de agente)',
      maxReplicas: 10,
      metrics: ['cpu > 70%', 'latency_p95 > 500ms']
    }
  },

  // SERVIÇO: Task Queue
  taskQueue: {
    technology: 'BullMQ + Redis',
    responsibilities: [
      'Processamento assíncrono',
      'Retry com backoff exponencial',
      'Dead letter queue',
      'Prioridade de tarefas',
      'Progress tracking'
    ],
    queues: {
      high: 'Tarefas críticas (0-1s delay)',
      medium: 'Tarefas normais (1-5s delay)',
      low: 'Tarefas batch (5-30s delay)'
    }
  },

  // SERVIÇO: Notification
  notificationService: {
    technology: 'Fastify + Baileys (WhatsApp) + Nodemailer',
    responsibilities: [
      'Envio de mensagens WhatsApp',
      'Envio de emails',
      'Templates de notificação',
      'Delivery tracking',
      'Fallback strategies'
    ],
    providers: {
      whatsapp: 'Baileys (self-hosted)',
      email: 'SMTP + SendGrid fallback',
      sms: 'Twilio (opcional)'
    }
  }
};

// ============================================
// Pipeline CI/CD
// ============================================

const ciCdPipeline = {
  // GITHUB ACTIONS WORKFLOWS
  workflows: {
    // PR Validation
    prValidation: {
      name: 'PR Validation',
      triggers: ['pull_request'],
      jobs: {
        lint: {
          runsOn: 'ubuntu-latest',
          steps: [
            'Checkout',
            'Setup Node.js 20',
            'Install dependencies',
            'Run ESLint',
            'Run TypeScript compiler',
            'Check commit messages (commitlint)'
          ]
        },
        test: {
          runsOn: 'ubuntu-latest',
          steps: [
            'Checkout',
            'Setup Node.js 20',
            'Install dependencies',
            'Run unit tests',
            'Generate coverage report',
            'Upload coverage to Codecov'
          ]
        },
        build: {
          runsOn: 'ubuntu-latest',
          steps: [
            'Checkout',
            'Setup Node.js 20',
            'Install dependencies',
            'Build all packages',
            'Docker build (cache layers)'
          ]
        }
      }
    },

    // Deploy to Staging
    deployStaging: {
      name: 'Deploy to Staging',
      triggers: ['push to develop'],
      jobs: {
        deploy: {
          runsOn: 'ubuntu-latest',
          environment: 'staging',
          steps: [
            'Checkout',
            'Login to Docker Registry',
            'Build and push Docker images',
            'Update k8s manifests',
            'Deploy to Kubernetes (kubectl apply)',
            'Run smoke tests',
            'Run integration tests'
          ]
        }
      }
    },

    // Deploy to Production
    deployProduction: {
      name: 'Deploy to Production',
      triggers: ['push to main'],
      jobs: {
        approval: {
          type: 'manual',
          required: ['tech-lead', 'squad-leader']
        },
        deploy: {
          runsOn: 'ubuntu-latest',
          environment: 'production',
          steps: [
            'Checkout',
            'Login to Docker Registry',
            'Build and push Docker images (with version tag)',
            'Blue-green deployment',
            'Update k8s manifests',
            'Deploy new version (maxUnavailable: 0)',
            'Run health checks',
            'Switch traffic (if health checks pass)',
            'Run e2e tests',
            'Rollback automático (se health check falhar)'
          ]
        }
      }
    }
  },

  // QUALITY GATES
  qualityGates: {
    blocking: {
      testCoverage: '>= 80%',
      lintErrors: '0',
      typeErrors: '0',
      securityScan: '0 critical vulnerabilities',
      buildTime: '< 5 minutes'
    },
    monitoring: {
      postDeploy: [
        'Error rate < 1%',
        'P95 latency < 500ms',
        'CPU usage < 70%',
        'Memory usage < 80%'
      ]
    }
  }
};

// ============================================
// Kubernetes Manifests (Simplified)
// ============================================

const kubernetesManifests = `
# api-gateway-deployment.yaml
apiVersion: apps/v1
kind: Deployment
metadata:
  name: api-gateway
  namespace: diyapp-v12
spec:
  replicas: 2
  selector:
    matchLabels:
      app: api-gateway
  template:
    metadata:
      labels:
        app: api-gateway
    spec:
      containers:
      - name: api-gateway
        image: ghcr.io/diyapp/api-gateway:latest
        ports:
        - containerPort: 3000
        env:
        - name: NODE_ENV
          value: production
        - name: REDIS_URL
          valueFrom:
            secretKeyRef:
              name: redis-secret
              key: url
        resources:
          requests:
            memory: "256Mi"
            cpu: "250m"
          limits:
            memory: "512Mi"
            cpu: "500m"
        livenessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /health
            port: 3000
          initialDelaySeconds: 30
          periodSeconds: 10
        readinessProbe:
          httpGet:
            path: /ready
            port: 3000
          initialDelaySeconds: 5
          periodSeconds: 5
---
# api-gateway-service.yaml
apiVersion: v1
kind: Service
metadata:
  name: api-gateway
  namespace: diyapp-v12
spec:
  selector:
    app: api-gateway
  ports:
  - port: 80
    targetPort: 3000
  type: ClusterIP
---
# agent-core-hpa.yaml
apiVersion: autoscaling/v2
kind: HorizontalPodAutoscaler
metadata:
  name: agent-core-hpa
  namespace: diyapp-v12
spec:
  scaleTargetRef:
    apiVersion: apps/v1
    kind: Deployment
    name: agent-core
  minReplicas: 2
  maxReplicas: 10
  metrics:
  - type: Resource
    resource:
      name: cpu
      target:
        type: Utilization
        averageUtilization: 70
  - type: Resource
    resource:
      name: memory
      target:
        type: Utilization
        averageUtilization: 80
`;

const dockerConfig = `
# docker-compose.yml (desenvolvimento)
version: '3.8'

services:
  postgres:
    image: postgres:15-alpine
    environment:
      POSTGRES_DB: diyapp
      POSTGRES_USER: diyapp
      POSTGRES_PASSWORD: diyapp_dev
    ports:
      - "5432:5432"
    volumes:
      - postgres_data:/var/lib/postgresql/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD-SHELL", "pg_isready -U diyapp"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  redis:
    image: redis:7-alpine
    ports:
      - "6379:6379"
    volumes:
      - redis_data:/data
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "redis-cli", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  rabbitmq:
    image: rabbitmq:3-management-alpine
    ports:
      - "5672:5672"
      - "15672:15672"
    environment:
      RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_USER: diyapp
      RABBITMQ_DEFAULT_PASS: diyapp_dev
    healthcheck:
      test: ["CMD", "rabbitmq-diagnostics", "ping"]
      interval: 10s
      timeout: 5s
      retries: 5

  api-gateway:
    build:
      context: ./apps/api-gateway
      dockerfile: Dockerfile.dev
    ports:
      - "3000:3000"
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: development
      DATABASE_URL: postgresql://diyapp:diyapp_dev@postgres:5432/diyapp
      REDIS_URL: redis://redis:6379
      RABBITMQ_URL: amqp://diyapp:diyapp_dev@rabbitmq:5672
    depends_on:
      postgres:
        condition: service_healthy
      redis:
        condition: service_healthy
      rabbitmq:
        condition: service_healthy
    volumes:
      - ./apps/api-gateway:/app
      - /app/node_modules

  agent-core:
    build:
      context: ./services/agent-core
      dockerfile: Dockerfile.dev
    ports:
      - "3001:3000"
    environment:
      NODE_ENV: development
      OPENAI_API_KEY: ${process.env.OPENAI_API_KEY}
    depends_on:
      - api-gateway
    volumes:
      - ./services/agent-core:/app
      - /app/node_modules

volumes:
  postgres_data:
  redis_data:
`;

### [Sessão Paralela: UX Designer]

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
```javascript
// File: src/index.js - Main entry point
const express = require('express');
const cors = require('cors');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const { createLogger, format, transports } = require('winston');
const { combine, timestamp, json, errors } = format;
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const bcrypt = require('bcryptjs');
const { v4: uuidv4 } = require('uuid');
const { Pool } = require('pg');
const Redis = require('ioredis');
const CircuitBreaker = require('opossum');

// Initialize Express app
const app = express();
const PORT = process.env.PORT || 3000;

// ======================
// 1. LOGGING CONFIGURATION
// ======================
const logger = createLogger({
  level: process.env.LOG_LEVEL || 'info',
  format: combine(
    timestamp(),
    errors({ stack: true }),
    json()
  ),
  defaultMeta: { service: 'core-api' },
  transports: [
    new transports.Console(),
    new transports.File({ filename: 'logs/error.log', level: 'error' }),
    new transports.File({ filename: 'logs/combined.log' })
  ]
});

// Request logging middleware
app.use((req, res, next) => {
  const correlationId = req.headers['x-correlation-id'] || uuidv4();
  req.correlationId = correlationId;
  
  const start = Date.now();
  
  res.on('finish', () => {
    const duration = Date.now() - start;
    
    const logData = {
      correlation_id: correlationId,
      method: req.method,
      url: req.url,
      status: res.statusCode,
      duration_ms: duration,
      user_agent: req.get('user-agent'),
      ip: req.ip,
      user_id: req.user?.id || null
    };
    
    // Mask sensitive data in logs
    if (req.body?.password) {
      logData.body = { ...req.body, password: '[MASKED]' };
    } else if (req.body?.token) {
      logData.body = { ...req.body, token: '[MASKED]' };
    } else if (req.body) {
      logData.body = req.body;
    }
    
    logger.info('HTTP Request', logData);
  });
  
  next();
});

// ======================
// 2. SECURITY MIDDLEWARE
// ======================
app.use(helmet({
  contentSecurityPolicy: {
    directives: {
      defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
      styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
      scriptSrc: ["'self'"],
      imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:", "https:"]
    }
  }
}));

app.use(cors({
  origin: process.env.CORS_ORIGIN || 'http://localhost:8080',
  credentials: true
}));

app.use(express.json({ limit: '10kb' }));

// Rate limiting
const apiLimiter = rateLimit({
  windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutes
  max: 100, // Limit each IP to 100 requests per windowMs
  message: { error: 'Too many requests, please try again later.' },
  standardHeaders: true,
  legacyHeaders: false
});

app.use('/api/', apiLimiter);

// ======================
// 3. DATABASE CONFIGURATION
// ======================
const dbPool = new Pool({
  host: process.env.DB_HOST || 'localhost',
  port: process.env.DB_PORT || 5432,
  database: process.env.DB_NAME || 'diyapp',
  user: process.env.DB_USER || 'postgres',
  password: process.env.DB_PASSWORD || 'postgres',
  max: 20,
  idleTimeoutMillis: 30000,
  connectionTimeoutMillis: 2000
});

// Database health check with circuit breaker
const dbHealthCheck = new CircuitBreaker(async () => {
  const client = await dbPool.connect();
  try {
    await client.query('SELECT 1');
    return { status: 'healthy', timestamp: new Date().toISOString() };
  } finally {
    client.release();
  }
}, {
  timeout: 5000,
  errorThresholdPercentage: 50,
  resetTimeout: 30000
});

dbHealthCheck.fallback(() => ({ 
  status: 'unhealthy', 
  error: 'Database circuit breaker open',
  timestamp: new Date().toISOString() 
}));

// Redis cache configuration
const redisClient = new Redis({
  host: process.env.REDIS_HOST || 'localhost',
  port: process.env.REDIS_PORT || 6379,
  retryStrategy: (times) => {
    const delay = Math.min(times * 50, 2000);
    return delay;
  },
  maxRetriesPerRequest: 3
});

redisClient.on('error', (err) => {
  logger.error('Redis connection error', { error: err.message });
});

// ======================
// 4. AUTHENTICATION MIDDLEWARE
// ======================
const JWT_SECRET = process.env.JWT_SECRET || 'your-secret-key-change-in-production';
const JWT_EXPIRY = process.env.JWT_EXPIRY || '24h';

// Token validation middleware
const authenticateToken = async (req, res, next) => {
  try {
    const authHeader = req.headers['authorization'];
    const token = authHeader && authHeader.split(' ')[1];
    
    if (!token) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Access token required' });
    }
    
    // Check token in Redis blacklist
    const isBlacklisted = await redisClient.get(`blacklist:${token}`);
    if (isBlacklisted) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Token has been revoked' });
    }
    
    const decoded = jwt.verify(token, JWT_SECRET);
    req.user = decoded;
    next();
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Token validation failed', { 
      correlation_id: req.correlationId,
      error: error.message 
    });
    
    if (error.name === 'TokenExpiredError') {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Token expired' });
    }
    return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Invalid token' });
  }
};

// Authorization middleware
const authorize = (...roles) => {
  return (req, res, next) => {
    if (!req.user) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Authentication required' });
    }
    
    if (!roles.includes(req.user.role)) {
      logger.warn('Unauthorized access attempt', {
        correlation_id: req.correlationId,
        user_id: req.user.id,
        attempted_role: req.user.role,
        required_roles: roles
      });
      return res.status(403).json({ error: 'Insufficient permissions' });
    }
    
    next();
  };
};

// ======================
// 5. HEALTH CHECK ENDPOINTS
// ======================
app.get('/health', async (req, res) => {
  const healthChecks = {
    api: { status: 'healthy', timestamp: new Date().toISOString() },
    database: { status: 'checking' },
    redis: { status: 'checking' }
  };
  
  try {
    // Check database with circuit breaker
    const dbStatus = await dbHealthCheck.fire();
    healthChecks.database = dbStatus;
    
    // Check Redis
    await redisClient.ping();
    healthChecks.redis = { 
      status: 'healthy', 
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString() 
    };
    
    const allHealthy = Object.values(healthChecks).every(h => h.status === 'healthy');
    const statusCode = allHealthy ? 200 : 503;
    
    res.status(statusCode).json({
      status: allHealthy ? 'healthy' : 'degraded',
      checks: healthChecks,
      uptime: process.uptime(),
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      correlation_id: req.correlationId
    });
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Health check failed', {
      correlation_id: req.correlationId,
      error: error.message
    });
    
    res.status(503).json({
      status: 'unhealthy',
      checks: healthChecks,
      error: error.message,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
      correlation_id: req.correlationId
    });
  }
});

app.get('/health/liveness', (req, res) => {
  res.status(200).json({
    status: 'alive',
    timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
  });
});

app.get('/health/readiness', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    // Quick database check
    const client = await dbPool.connect();
    await client.query('SELECT 1');
    client.release();
    
    // Quick Redis check
    await redisClient.ping();
    
    res.status(200).json({
      status: 'ready',
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    });
  } catch (error) {
    res.status(503).json({
      status: 'not_ready',
      error: error.message,
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    });
  }
});

// ======================
// 6. AUTHENTICATION ENDPOINTS
// ======================
app.post('/api/auth/register', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { email, password, name } = req.body;
    
    // Input validation
    if (!email || !password || !name) {
      return res.status(400).json({ 
        error: 'Email, password, and name are required' 
      });
    }
    
    if (password.length < 8) {
      return res.status(422).json({
        error: 'Password must be at least 8 characters long'
      });
    }
    
    // Check if user exists
    const existingUser = await dbPool.query(
      'SELECT id FROM users WHERE email = $1',
      [email]
    );
    
    if (existingUser.rows.length > 0) {
      return res.status(409).json({ error: 'User already exists' });
    }
    
    // Hash password
    const hashedPassword = await bcrypt.hash(password, 10);
    
    // Create user
    const result = await dbPool.query(
      `INSERT INTO users (email, password_hash, name, role, created_at) 
       VALUES ($1, $2, $3, $4, NOW()) 
       RETURNING id, email, name, role, created_at`,
      [email, hashedPassword, name, 'user']
    );
    
    const user = result.rows[0];
    
    // Generate JWT
    const token = jwt.sign(
      { 
        id: user.id, 
        email: user.email, 
        role: user.role,
        name: user.name 
      },
      JWT_SECRET,
      { expiresIn: JWT_EXPIRY }
    );
    
    // Store token in Redis for fast validation (optional)
    await redisClient.setex(`user:${user.id}:token`, 86400, token);
    
    logger.info('User registered successfully', {
      correlation_id: req.correlationId,
      user_id: user.id,
      email: email.replace(/.(?=.*@)/g, '*') // Mask email in logs
    });
    
    res.status(201).json({
      user: {
        id: user.id,
        email: user.email,
        name: user.name,
        role: user.role
      },
      token,
      expires_in: JWT_EXPIRY
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Registration failed', {
      correlation_id: req.correlationId,
      error: error.message,
      stack: error.stack
    });
    
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Registration failed' });
  }
});

app.post('/api/auth/login', async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { email, password } = req.body;
    
    if (!email || !password) {
      return res.status(400).json({ 
        error: 'Email and password are required' 
      });
    }
    
    // Find user
    const result = await dbPool.query(
      'SELECT id, email, password_hash, name, role FROM users WHERE email = $1',
      [email]
    );
    
    if (result.rows.length === 0) {
      // Simulate same delay to prevent timing attacks
      await bcrypt.compare(password, '$2a$10$fakehashforsecurity');
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid credentials' });
    }
    
    const user = result.rows[0];
    
    // Verify password
    const validPassword = await bcrypt.compare(password, user.password_hash);
    if (!validPassword) {
      return res.status(401).json({ error: 'Invalid credentials' });
    }
    
    // Generate JWT
    const token = jwt.sign(
      { 
        id: user.id, 
        email: user.email, 
        role: user.role,
        name: user.name 
      },
      JWT_SECRET,
      { expiresIn: JWT_EXPIRY }
    );
    
    // Update last login
    await dbPool.query(
      'UPDATE users SET last_login = NOW() WHERE id = $1',
      [user.id]
    );
    
    // Cache user data in Redis
    await redisClient.setex(`user:${user.id}`, 3600, JSON.stringify({
      id: user.id,
      email: user.email,
      name: user.name,
      role: user.role
    }));
    
    logger.info('User logged in successfully', {
      correlation_id: req.correlationId,
      user_id: user.id,
      email: email.replace(/.(?=.*@)/g, '*')
    });
    
    res.json({
      user: {
        id: user.id,
        email: user.email,
        name: user.name,
        role: user.role
      },
      token,
      expires_in: JWT_EXPIRY
    });
    
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Login failed', {
      correlation_id: req.correlationId,
      error: error.message
    });
    
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Login failed' });
  }
});

app.post('/api/auth/logout', authenticateToken, async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const token = req.headers['authorization'].split(' ')[1];
    
    // Add token to blacklist (valid until expiry)
    const decoded = jwt.decode(token);
    const ttl = Math.max(0, decoded.exp - Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000));
    
    if (ttl > 0) {
      await redisClient.setex(`blacklist:${token}`, ttl, '1');
    }
    
    // Clear user cache
    await redisClient.del(`user:${req.user.id}`);
    await redisClient.del(`user:${req.user.id}:token`);
    
    logger.info('User logged out', {
      correlation_id: req.correlationId,
      user_id: req.user.id
    });
    
    res.status(204).send();
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Logout failed', {
      correlation_id: req.correlationId,
      error: error.message
    });
    
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Logout failed' });
  }
});

app.get('/api/auth/me', authenticateToken, async (req, res) => {
  try {
    // Try to get from cache first
    const cachedUser = await redisClient.get(`user:${req.user.id}`);
    
    if (cachedUser) {
      return res.json(JSON.parse(cachedUser));
    }
    
    // Get from database
    const result = await dbPool.query(
      'SELECT id, email, name, role, created_at, last_login FROM users WHERE id = $1',
      [req.user.id]
    );
    
    if (result.rows.length === 0) {
      return res.status(404).json({ error: 'User not found' });
    }
    
    const user = result.rows[0];
    
    // Cache for future requests
    await redisClient.setex(`user:${req.user.id}`, 3600, JSON.stringify(user));
    
    res.json(user);
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Get user profile failed', {
      correlation_id: req.correlationId,
      user_id: req.user.id,
      error: error.message
    });
    
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to get user profile' });
  }
});

// ======================
// 7. PROTECTED API ENDPOINTS
// ======================
app.get('/api/protected/data', authenticateToken, async (req, res) => {
  try {
    // Example protected endpoint with caching
    const cacheKey = `protected:data:${req.user.id}`;
    
    // Try cache first
    const cachedData = await redisClient.get(cacheKey);
    if (cachedData) {
      return res.json({
        data: JSON.parse(cachedData),
        source: 'cache',
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      });
    }
    
    // Get from database (simulated)
    const result = await dbPool.query(
      'SELECT * FROM user_data WHERE user_id = $1 ORDER BY created_at DESC LIMIT 10',
      [req.user.id]
    );
    
    const data = result.rows;
    
    // Cache for 5 minutes
    await redisClient.setex(cacheKey, 300, JSON.stringify(data));
    
    res.json({
      data,
      source: 'database',
      timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
    });
  } catch (error) {
    logger.error('Protected data fetch failed', {
      correlation_id: req.correlationId,
      user_id: req.user.id,
      error: error.message
    });
    
    res.status(500).json({ error: 'Failed to fetch data' });
  }
});

app.post('/api/protected/data', authenticateToken, async (req, res) => {
  try {
    const { content } = req.body;
    
    if (!content || typeof content !== 'string') {
      return res.status(400).json({ error: 'Content is required and must be a string' });
    }
    
    // Insert data
    const result = await dbPool.query(
      `INSERT INTO user_data (user_id, content, created_at) 
       VALUES ($1, $2, NOW()) 


### [Sessão Paralela: Frontend]
Vou configurar o projeto DIYAPP Evolution V12 Core com Next.js, integrar sistema de design e implementar componentes base. Como Dev Frontend Sênior, vou garantir fidelidade ao design, performance e qualidade de código.

```bash
# Estrutura do projeto

    "dev": "next dev",
    "build": "next build",

    "lint": "next lint",
    "test": "vitest",
    "test:coverage": "vitest run --coverage",
    "storybook": "storybook dev -p 6006",

  "devDependencies": {
    "@types/node": "20.11.24",

    "@types/react-dom": "18.2.19",
    "@storybook/addon-a11y": "^7.6.17",

# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Data Engineer Task

## Arquitetura de Banco de Dados e Provisionamento

### 1. Estrutura de Pastas do Projeto

```

### 2. Script de Provisionamento do Banco de Dados (`database/scripts/provision_db.sh`)

```bash
#!/bin/bash

# DIYAPP V12 - Database Provisioning Script
# Data Engineer: Database Setup and Migration

set -e

echo "🚀 DIYAPP V12 - Database Provisioning Started"
echo "============================================"

# Load environment variables
if [ -f .env ]; then
    export $(cat .env | grep -v '^#' | xargs)
else
    echo "⚠️  .env file not found. Using defaults or requiring manual input"
fi

# Configuration
DB_HOST=${DB_HOST:-"localhost"}
DB_PORT=${DB_PORT:-5432}
DB_NAME=${DB_NAME:-"diyapp_v12"}
DB_USER=${DB_USER:-"diyapp_admin"}
DB_PASS=${DB_PASS:-$(openssl rand -base64 32)}
ENVIRONMENT=${ENVIRONMENT:-"development"}

# Colors for output
RED='\033[0;31m'
GREEN='\033[0;32m'
YELLOW='\033[1;33m'
NC='\033[0m' # No Color

# Function to log messages
log_info() {
    echo -e "${GREEN}[INFO]${NC} $1"
}

log_warn() {
    echo -e "${YELLOW}[WARN]${NC} $1"
}

log_error() {
    echo -e "${RED}[ERROR]${NC} $1"
}

# Function to check PostgreSQL connection
check_postgres_connection() {
    log_info "Checking PostgreSQL connection..."
    
    if command -v psql &> /dev/null; then
        if PGPASSWORD=$DB_PASS psql -h "$DB_HOST" -p "$DB_PORT" -U "$DB_USER" -d postgres -c "\q" 2>/dev/null; then
            log_info "✅ PostgreSQL connection successful"
            return 0
        else
            log_warn "⚠️  Cannot connect to PostgreSQL. Attempting to start service..."
            return 1
        fi
    else
        log_error "❌ psql command not found. Please install PostgreSQL client"
        exit 1
    fi
}

# Function to create database
create_database() {
    log_info "Creating database: $DB_NAME"
    
    # Create database if it doesn't exist
    if ! PGPASSWORD=$DB_PASS psql -h "$DB_HOST" -p "$DB_PORT" -U "$DB_USER" -d postgres -tc "SELECT 1 FROM pg_database WHERE datname = '$DB_NAME'" | grep -q 1; then
        PGPASSWORD=$DB_PASS psql -h "$DB_HOST" -p "$DB_PORT" -U "$DB_USER" -d postgres -c "CREATE DATABASE $DB_NAME;"
        log_info "✅ Database created"
    else
        log_info "📊 Database already exists"
    fi
    
    # Create extensions
    PGPASSWORD=$DB_PASS psql -h "$DB_HOST" -p "$DB_PORT" -U "$DB_USER" -d "$DB_NAME" -c "
        CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS \"uuid-ossp\";
        CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS \"pgcrypto\";
        CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS \"pg_stat_statements\";
    "
    log_info "✅ PostgreSQL extensions created"
}

# Function to run migrations
run_migrations() {
    log_info "Running database migrations..."
    
    local migration_dir="database/migrations"
    local migration_files=($(ls "$migration_dir"/*.sql | sort))
    
    # Create migrations tracking table
    PGPASSWORD=$DB_PASS psql -h "$DB_HOST" -p "$DB_PORT" -U "$DB_USER" -d "$DB_NAME" -c "
        CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS schema_migrations (
            id SERIAL PRIMARY KEY,
            version VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL UNIQUE,
            filename VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
            applied_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
            checksum VARCHAR(64) NOT NULL
        );
    "
    
    for migration_file in "${migration_files[@]}"; do
        local filename=$(basename "$migration_file")
        local version=$(echo "$filename" | cut -d'_' -f1)
        local checksum=$(sha256sum "$migration_file" | cut -d' ' -f1)
        
        # Check if migration already applied
        local applied=$(PGPASSWORD=$DB_PASS psql -h "$DB_HOST" -p "$DB_PORT" -U "$DB_USER" -d "$DB_NAME" -tc "
            SELECT 1 FROM schema_migrations WHERE version = '$version' AND checksum = '$checksum'
        " | xargs)
        
        if [ -z "$applied" ]; then
            log_info "Applying migration: $filename"
            
            # Apply migration
            if PGPASSWORD=$DB_PASS psql -h "$DB_HOST" -p "$DB_PORT" -U "$DB_USER" -d "$DB_NAME" -f "$migration_file"; then
                # Record migration
                PGPASSWORD=$DB_PASS psql -h "$DB_HOST" -p "$DB_PORT" -U "$DB_USER" -d "$DB_NAME" -c "
                    INSERT INTO schema_migrations (version, filename, checksum)
                    VALUES ('$version', '$filename', '$checksum')
                    ON CONFLICT (version) DO UPDATE SET
                        filename = EXCLUDED.filename,
                        checksum = EXCLUDED.checksum,
                        applied_at = CURRENT_TIMESTAMP;
                "
                log_info "✅ Migration applied: $filename"
            else
                log_error "❌ Failed to apply migration: $filename"
                exit 1
            fi
        else
            log_info "⏭️  Migration already applied: $filename"
        fi
    done
    
    log_info "✅ All migrations completed"
}

# Function to run seeds
run_seeds() {
    log_info "Running database seeds..."
    
    local seed_dir="database/seeds"
    local seed_files=($(ls "$seed_dir"/*.sql | sort))
    
    for seed_file in "${seed_files[@]}"; do
        local filename=$(basename "$seed_file")
        log_info "Seeding: $filename"
        
        if PGPASSWORD=$DB_PASS psql -h "$DB_HOST" -p "$DB_PORT" -U "$DB_USER" -d "$DB_NAME" -f "$seed_file"; then
            log_info "✅ Seed completed: $filename"
        else
            log_error "❌ Failed to seed: $filename"
            exit 1
        fi
    done
    
    log_info "✅ All seeds completed"
}

# Function to create backup
create_backup() {
    log_info "Creating database backup..."
    
    local backup_dir="database/backups"
    mkdir -p "$backup_dir"
    
    local timestamp=$(date +"%Y%m%d_%H%M%S")
    local backup_file="$backup_dir/backup_${DB_NAME}_${timestamp}.sql"
    
    if PGPASSWORD=$DB_PASS pg_dump -h "$DB_HOST" -p "$DB_PORT" -U "$DB_USER" -d "$DB_NAME" --clean --if-exists > "$backup_file"; then
        log_info "✅ Backup created: $backup_file"
        
        # Compress backup
        gzip "$backup_file"
        log_info "✅ Backup compressed: ${backup_file}.gz"
    else
        log_error "❌ Failed to create backup"
    fi
}

# Function to generate environment file
generate_env_file() {
    log_info "Generating environment configuration..."
    
    cat > .env << EOF
# DIYAPP V12 - Database Configuration
# Generated on $(date)

# Database Configuration
DB_HOST=$DB_HOST
DB_PORT=$DB_PORT
DB_NAME=$DB_NAME
DB_USER=$DB_USER
DB_PASS=$DB_PASS

# Connection Pool
DB_POOL_MIN=2
DB_POOL_MAX=20
DB_CONNECTION_TIMEOUT=30000
DB_IDLE_TIMEOUT=10000

# SSL Configuration (for production)
DB_SSL=${DB_SSL:-false}
DB_SSL_REJECT_UNAUTHORIZED=${DB_SSL_REJECT_UNAUTHORIZED:-false}

# Performance Tuning
DB_STATEMENT_TIMEOUT=30000
DB_IDLE_IN_TRANSACTION_SESSION_TIMEOUT=10000

# Monitoring
DB_ENABLE_METRICS=true
DB_LOG_LEVEL=info

# Environment
NODE_ENV=$ENVIRONMENT
APP_VERSION=v12.0.0

# Backup Configuration
BACKUP_CRON_SCHEDULE="0 2 * * *"  # Daily at 2 AM
BACKUP_RETENTION_DAYS=30

# Security
ENCRYPTION_KEY=$(openssl rand -base64 32)
JWT_SECRET=$(openssl rand -base64 64)

EOF
    
    log_info "✅ Environment file generated"
    log_warn "⚠️  IMPORTANT: Store .env file securely. Do not commit to version control!"
}

# Main execution
main() {
    log_info "Starting DIYAPP V12 Database Provisioning"
    echo ""
    
    # Check PostgreSQL
    if ! check_postgres_connection; then
        log_warn "Attempting to start PostgreSQL via Docker..."
        if command -v docker &> /dev/null; then
            docker-compose up -d postgres
            sleep 10
            check_postgres_connection || exit 1
        else
            log_error "Please ensure PostgreSQL is running on $DB_HOST:$DB_PORT"
            exit 1
        fi
    fi
    
    # Create database
    create_database
    
    # Run migrations
    run_migrations
    
    # Run seeds (only in development/staging)
    if [ "$ENVIRONMENT" != "production" ]; then
        run_seeds
    fi
    
    # Create initial backup
    create_backup
    
    # Generate environment file
    generate_env_file
    
    # Health check
    log_info "Performing health check..."
    PGPASSWORD=$DB_PASS psql -h "$DB_HOST" -p "$DB_PORT" -U "$DB_USER" -d "$DB_NAME" -f database/scripts/health_check.sql
    
    echo ""
    log_info "============================================"
    log_info "✅ DIYAPP V12 Database Provisioning Complete"
    log_info "📊 Database: $DB_NAME@$DB_HOST:$DB_PORT"
    log_info "👤 User: $DB_USER"
    log_info "🔐 Password saved in .env file"
    log_info "============================================"
}

# Execute main function
main "$@"
```

### 3. Migração Inicial do Schema (`database/migrations/001_initial_schema.sql`)

```sql
-- DIYAPP V12 - Initial Database Schema
-- Migration: 001_initial_schema.sql
-- Data Engineer: Core tables for autonomous squad operations

-- Enable UUID generation
CREATE EXTENSION IF NOT EXISTS "uuid-ossp";

-- ============================================
-- CORE TABLES
-- ============================================

-- Users table (for authentication and permissions)
CREATE TABLE users (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    email VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    username VARCHAR(100) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    full_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    
    -- Role-based access control
    role VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'user',
    squad_role VARCHAR(50), -- PM, DataEngineer, AIOps, etc.
    permissions JSONB DEFAULT '[]',
    
    -- Authentication
    password_hash VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    salt VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    mfa_enabled BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    mfa_secret VARCHAR(255),
    
    -- Status
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    is_verified BOOLEAN DEFAULT false,
    last_login_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    
    -- Audit
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    created_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
    updated_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
    
    -- Indexes
    CONSTRAINT valid_email CHECK (email ~* '^[A-Za-z0-9._%+-]+@[A-Za-z0-9.-]+\.[A-Za-z]{2,}$'),
    CONSTRAINT valid_role CHECK (role IN ('admin', 'manager', 'user', 'system')),
    CONSTRAINT valid_squad_role CHECK (squad_role IN ('ProductManager', 'DataEngineer', 'AIOps', 'LLMSpecialist', 'SRE', 'Compliance', 'SquadLeader', NULL))
);

-- API Keys for system-to-system communication
CREATE TABLE api_keys (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    key_hash VARCHAR(255) UNIQUE NOT NULL,
    prefix VARCHAR(10) NOT NULL,
    
    -- Permissions
    user_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id),
    scopes JSONB DEFAULT '["read"]',
    rate_limit_per_minute INTEGER DEFAULT 60,
    
    -- Validity
    expires_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    last_used_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    
    -- Audit
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    created_by UUID REFERENCES users(id),
    
    -- Indexes
    INDEX idx_api_keys_user_id (user_id),
    INDEX idx_api_keys_prefix (prefix)
);

-- ============================================
-- DATA PIPELINE TABLES
-- ============================================

-- Data sources configuration
CREATE TABLE data_sources (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- postgres, mysql, api, s3, etc.
    connection_config JSONB NOT NULL,
    
    -- Scheduling
    sync_frequency VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'daily', -- hourly, daily, weekly, realtime
    sync_cron_schedule VARCHAR(100),
    last_sync_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    next_sync_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    
    -- Status
    is_active BOOLEAN DEFAULT true,
    sync_status VARCHAR(50) DEFAULT 'pending',
    error_message TEXT,
    
    -- Ownership
    owner_id UUID NOT NULL REFERENCES users(id),
    squad_role_owner VARCHAR(50), -- Which squad role owns this
    
    -- Audit
    created_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    updated_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    
    -- Indexes
    CONSTRAINT valid_source_type CHECK (type IN ('postgres', 'mysql', 'mongodb', 'api', 's3', 'kafka', 'bigquery', 'snowflake')),
    CONSTRAINT valid_sync_status CHECK (sync_status IN ('pending', 'running', 'success', 'failed', 'partial')),
    INDEX idx_data_sources_owner (owner_id),
    INDEX idx_data_sources_status (sync_status, next_sync_at)
);

-- Pipeline executions
CREATE TABLE pipeline_executions (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    pipeline_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    pipeline_version VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL,
    
    -- Execution details
    data_source_id UUID REFERENCES data_sources(id),
    started_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE DEFAULT CURRENT_TIMESTAMP,
    completed_at TIMESTAMP WITH TIME ZONE,
    duration_ms INTEGER,
    
    -- Status and metrics
    status VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL DEFAULT 'running',
    records_processed INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    records_failed INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    bytes_processed BIGINT DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Error handling
    error_message TEXT,
    stack_trace TEXT,
    retry_count INTEGER DEFAULT 0,
    
    -- Output
    output_location VARCHAR(500),
    output_metadata JSONB,
    
    -- Indexes
    CONSTRAINT valid_pipeline_status CHECK (status IN ('running', 'success', 'failed', 'partial', 'cancelled')),
    INDEX idx_pipeline_executions_status (status),
    INDEX idx_pipeline_executions_timing (started_at, completed_at),
    INDEX idx_pipeline_executions_source (data_source_id)
);

-- Data quality tests
CREATE TABLE data_quality_tests (
    id UUID PRIMARY KEY DEFAULT uuid_generate_v4(),
    name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    description TEXT,
    
    -- Test configuration
    dataset_name VARCHAR(255) NOT NULL,
    test_type VARCHAR(50) NOT NULL, -- completeness, uniqueness, validity, consistency
    test_query TEXT NOT NULL,
    expected_result JSONB,
    
    -- Thresholds
    severity VARCHAR(20) DEFAULT 'warning', -- critical, warning, info
    threshold_value DECIMAL(5,2),
    threshold_operator VARCHAR

### [Sessão Paralela: Compliance]

## 2. Modelo de Registro de Processamento (ROPA)

**src/compliance/models/DataProcessingRecord.js**
```javascript
const { DataTypes } = require('sequelize');
const sequelize = require('../../config/database');

const DataProcessingRecord = sequelize.define('DataProcessingRecord', {
  id: {
    type: DataTypes.UUID,
    defaultValue: DataTypes.UUIDV4,
    primaryKey: true
  },
  processing_activity: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false
  },
  data_categories: {
    type: DataTypes.JSON,
    allowNull: false,
    validate: {
      isValidCategories(value) {
        const validCategories = require('../../../config/data-categories.json');
        value.forEach(cat => {
          if (!validCategories.includes(cat)) {
            throw new Error(`Categoria inválida: ${cat}`);
          }
        });
      }
    }
  },
  legal_basis: {
    type: DataTypes.ENUM(
      'consentimento',
      'contrato',
      'obrigacao_legal',
      'interesse_vital',
      'interesse_publico',
      'legitimo_interesse'
    ),
    allowNull: false
  },
  purpose: {
    type: DataTypes.TEXT,
    allowNull: false
  },
  data_subjects: {
    type: DataTypes.ENUM(
      'clientes',
      'funcionarios',
      'fornecedores',
      'visitantes',
      'crianças'
    ),
    allowNull: false
  },
  recipients: {
    type: DataTypes.JSON,
    defaultValue: []
  },
  third_country_transfers: {
    type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
    defaultValue: false
  },
  retention_period: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING,
    allowNull: false
  },
  security_measures: {
    type: DataTypes.JSON,
    defaultValue: []
  },
  dpia_required: {
    type: DataTypes.BOOLEAN,
    defaultValue: false
  },
  dpia_reference: {
    type: DataTypes.STRING
  },
  created_at: {
    type: DataTypes.DATE,
    defaultValue: DataTypes.NOW
  },
  updated_at: {
    type: DataTypes.DATE,
    defaultValue: DataTypes.NOW
  },
  status: {
    type: DataTypes.ENUM('ativo', 'inativo', 'revisao_pendente'),
    defaultValue: 'ativo'
  }
}, {
  tableName: 'data_processing_records',
  timestamps: true,
  underscored: true
});

// Índices para performance
DataProcessingRecord.addIndex(['legal_basis']);
DataProcessingRecord.addIndex(['dpia_required']);
DataProcessingRecord.addIndex(['status']);

module.exports = DataProcessingRecord;
```

## 3. Serviço de Retenção Automatizada

**src/compliance/services/RetentionService.js**
```javascript
const cron = require('node-cron');
const { Op } = require('sequelize');
const logger = require('../../utils/logger');
const DataProcessingRecord = require('../models/DataProcessingRecord');
const User = require('../../users/models/User');
const AuditService = require('./AuditService');

class RetentionService {
  constructor() {
    this.retentionPolicies = require('../../../config/retention-policies.json');
    this.initScheduler();
  }

  initScheduler() {
    // Agendamento de limpeza automática
    cron.schedule(this.retentionPolicies.global_settings.automatic_deletion_cron, () => {
      this.executeRetentionCleanup();
    });

    // Verificação diária de políticas
    cron.schedule('0 0 * * *', () => {
      this.validateRetentionCompliance();
    });

    logger.info('Serviço de retenção inicializado');
  }

  async executeRetentionCleanup() {
    try {
      const policies = this.retentionPolicies.retention_policies;
      const now = new Date();
      let totalDeleted = 0;

      for (const [policyKey, policy] of Object.entries(policies)) {
        const retentionMonths = parseInt(policy.retention_period);
        const cutoffDate = new Date();
        cutoffDate.setMonth(cutoffDate.getMonth() - retentionMonths);

        switch (policyKey) {
          case 'user_account_data':
            totalDeleted += await this.cleanupUserData(cutoffDate, policy);
            break;
          case 'llm_interactions':
            totalDeleted += await this.cleanupLLMInteractions(cutoffDate, policy);
            break;
          case 'usage_analytics':
            totalDeleted += await this.cleanupAnalyticsData(cutoffDate, policy);
            break;
        }
      }

      await AuditService.logRetentionCleanup({
        timestamp: now,
        records_deleted: totalDeleted,
        policies_applied: Object.keys(policies).length
      });

      logger.info(`Limpeza de retenção concluída: ${totalDeleted} registros removidos`);
      
      return {
        success: true,
        records_deleted: totalDeleted,
        timestamp: now.toISOString()
      };
    } catch (error) {
      logger.error('Erro na limpeza de retenção:', error);
      throw error;
    }
  }

  async cleanupUserData(cutoffDate, policy) {
    const usersToAnonymize = await User.findAll({
      where: {
        last_active: { [Op.lt]: cutoffDate },
        account_status: 'inactive',
        data_retention_hold: false
      }
    });

    let deletedCount = 0;
    
    for (const user of usersToAnonymize) {
      if (policy.anonymization_required) {
        await this.anonymizeUserData(user);
      } else {
        await user.destroy();
      }
      deletedCount++;
    }

    return deletedCount;
  }

  async anonymizeUserData(user) {
    // Anonimização pseudônima (mantém ID para referência)
    await user.update({
      email: `anon_${user.id}@redacted.com`,
      name: 'Usuário Anônimo',
      phone: null,
      birth_date: null,
      ip_address: '0.0.0.0',
      anonymized_at: new Date()
    });

    // Remove dados sensíveis relacionados
    await this.removeRelatedSensitiveData(user.id);
  }

  async removeRelatedSensitiveData(userId) {
    // Remove logs sensíveis
    await Log.destroy({
      where: {
        user_id: userId,
        sensitivity_level: { [Op.in]: ['high', 'critical'] }
      }
    });

    // Anonimiza interações com LLM
    await LLMInteraction.update(
      { prompt: '[REDACTED]', response: '[REDACTED]' },
      { where: { user_id: userId } }
    );
  }

  async validateRetentionCompliance() {
    const violations = [];
    const policies = this.retentionPolicies.retention_policies;

    for (const [policyKey, policy] of Object.entries(policies)) {
      const maxAge = this.parseRetentionPeriod(policy.retention_period);
      const violation = await this.checkPolicyCompliance(policyKey, maxAge);
      
      if (violation) {
        violations.push(violation);
      }
    }

    if (violations.length > 0) {
      await this.notifyComplianceOfficer(violations);
    }

    return violations;
  }

  parseRetentionPeriod(period) {
    const match = period.match(/(\d+)\s*(meses|anos|dias)/);
    if (!match) return 24; // Default 24 meses
    
    const value = parseInt(match[1]);
    const unit = match[2];
    
    switch (unit) {
      case 'anos': return value * 12;
      case 'meses': return value;
      case 'dias': return Math.ceil(value / 30);
      default: return 24;
    }
  }

  async checkPolicyCompliance(policyKey, maxAgeMonths) {
    const cutoffDate = new Date();
    cutoffDate.setMonth(cutoffDate.getMonth() - maxAgeMonths);

    let violation = null;
    
    switch (policyKey) {
      case 'user_account_data':
        const oldUsers = await User.count({
          where: {
            last_active: { [Op.lt]: cutoffDate },
            anonymized_at: null
          }
        });
        
        if (oldUsers > 0) {
          violation = {
            policy: policyKey,
            violation_type: 'excesso_retencao',
            records_count: oldUsers,
            max_age_allowed: `${maxAgeMonths} meses`
          };
        }
        break;
    }

    return violation;
  }

  async notifyComplianceOfficer(violations) {
    const emailService = require('../../services/EmailService');
    const officerEmail = this.retentionPolicies.global_settings.compliance_officer_email;

    const violationSummary = violations.map(v => 
      `- ${v.policy}: ${v.records_count} registros excedem ${v.max_age_allowed}`
    ).join('\n');

    await emailService.send({
      to: officerEmail,
      subject: 'ALERTA: Violações de Política de Retenção',
      template: 'compliance_alert',
      data: {
        violations: violationSummary,
        total_violations: violations.length,
        timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
      }
    });

    logger.warn(`Notificado DPO sobre ${violations.length} violações de retenção`);
  }

  async applyEmergencyHold(userId, reason) {
    await User.update(
      { data_retention_hold: true, hold_reason: reason },
      { where: { id: userId } }
    );

    await AuditService.logEmergencyHold({
      user_id: userId,
      reason: reason,
      applied_by: 'system',
      timestamp: new Date()
    });

    return { success: true, message: 'Retenção de emergência aplicada' };
  }

  async getRetentionReport() {
    const policies = this.retentionPolicies.retention_policies;
    const report = {};

    for (const [policyKey, policy] of Object.entries(policies)) {
      const maxAge = this.parseRetentionPeriod(policy.retention_period);
      const cutoffDate = new Date();
      cutoffDate.setMonth(cutoffDate.getMonth() - maxAge);

      report[policyKey] = {
        policy: policy,
        max_age_months: maxAge,
        cutoff_date: cutoffDate,
        compliance_status: await this.getPolicyComplianceStatus(policyKey, cutoffDate)
      };
    }

    return report;
  }

  async getPolicyComplianceStatus(policyKey, cutoffDate) {
    // Implementação específica por política
    return 'compliant'; // ou 'non_compliant' com detalhes
  }
}

module.exports = new RetentionService();
```

## 4. Controlador de Direitos do Titular

**src/compliance/controllers/DataSubjectRightsController.js**
```javascript
const express = require('express');
const router = express.Router();
const { body, validationResult } = require('express-validator');
const logger = require('../../utils/logger');
const DataSubjectRequest = require('../models/DataSubjectRequest');
const GDPRComplianceService = require('../services/GDPRComplianceService');
const AuditService = require('../services/AuditService');

class DataSubjectRightsController {
  constructor() {
    this.router = router;
    this.setupRoutes();
  }

  setupRoutes() {
    // Endpoint para solicitação de direitos
    router.post('/rights-request', [
      body('request_type').isIn(['access', 'rectification', 'erasure', 'portability', 'restriction', 'objection']),
      body('user_email').isEmail(),
      body('user_id').optional().isString(),
      body('additional_info').optional().isString()
    ], this.handleRightsRequest.bind(this));

    // Endpoint para verificar status
    router.get('/request-status/:requestId', this.getRequestStatus.bind(this));

    // Endpoint para DPO
    router.get('/pending-requests', this.getPendingRequests.bind(this));
    router.put('/process-request/:requestId', this.processRequest.bind(this));
  }

  async handleRightsRequest(req, res) {
    try {
      const errors = validationResult(req);
      if (!errors.isEmpty()) {
        return res.status(400).json({ errors: errors.array() });
      }

      const {
        request_type,
        user_email,
        user_id,
        additional_info
      } = req.body;

      // Validação de segurança
      const validation = await this.validateRequest(user_email, user_id);
      if (!validation.valid) {
        return res.status(403).json({ 
          error: 'Falha na validação',
          details: validation.reason 
        });
      }

      // Cria registro da solicitação
      const request = await DataSubjectRequest.create({
        request_id: this.generateRequestId(),
        request_type: request_type,
        user_email: user_email,
        user_id: user_id,
        additional_info: additional_info,
        status: 'received',
        received_at: new Date(),
        sla_deadline: this.calculateSLADeadline(),
        verification_token: this.generateVerificationToken()
      });

      // Notificação automática
      await this.sendAcknowledgement(request);

      // Log de auditoria
      await AuditService.logDataSubjectRequest({
        request_id: request.request_id,
        request_type: request_type,
        user_email: user_email,
        timestamp: new Date()
      });

      res.status(

### [Sessão Paralela: Segurança]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Threat Modeling e Padrões de Segurança

## 1. Análise de Threat Modeling STRIDE para V12

### 1.1 Assets Críticos Identificados
```
1. Dados de Usuário (PII): nome, email, telefone, documentos
2. Credenciais: tokens JWT, refresh tokens, senhas hash
3. Dados de Transação: histórico de ações, logs de auditoria
4. Configurações do Sistema: secrets, chaves de API, configurações de LLM
5. Modelos de IA: prompts do sistema, contextos de treinamento
```

### 1.2 Matriz de Ameaças STRIDE

#### **Spoofing (Falsificação)**
```
- A1: Ataque de força bruta em endpoints de login
- A2: Token JWT roubado/reutilizado
- A3: Credenciais de serviço vazadas (chaves de API)
- A4: Prompt injection em LLMs para se passar por sistema
```

#### **Tampering (Manipulação)**
```
- B1: SQL Injection em queries do banco
- B2: Manipulação de payloads JWT não assinados
- B3: Alteração não autorizada de dados de auditoria
- B4: Modificação de prompts do sistema em trânsito
```

#### **Repudiation (Repúdio)**
```
- C1: Usuário nega ação realizada (falta de logs imutáveis)
- C2: Logs de auditoria modificáveis por administrador
- C3: Transações sem assinatura digital
```

#### **Information Disclosure (Divulgação)**
```
- D1: Vazamento de PII em respostas de API
- D2: Logs contendo dados sensíveis
- D3: Exposição de secrets em variáveis de ambiente
- D4: Data exfiltration via LLM (modelo revela dados do contexto)
```

#### **Denial of Service (Negação)**
```
- E1: Ataque DDoS em endpoints públicos
- E2: Rate limiting inadequado em APIs
- E3: Exaustão de recursos por prompts maliciosos em LLM
```

#### **Elevation of Privilege (Elevação)**
```
- F1: IDOR (Insecure Direct Object Reference)
- F2: Falha de autorização em nível de recurso
- F3: Prompt injection para execução de comandos privilegiados
- F4: JWT com claims de role manipuladas
```

## 2. Padrões de Segurança V12 - Implementação

### 2.1 Estrutura do Projeto
```bash
diyapp-v12/
├── src/
│   ├── security/
│   │   ├── auth/

│   │   │   └── hash.service.js
