### 2.2 Código de Implementação

#### **server.js** - Ponto de entrada principal
```javascript
const express = require('express');
const helmet = require('helmet');
const cors = require('cors');
const rateLimit = require('express-rate-limit');
const { SecurityAudit } = require('./src/security/audit/audit.logger');
const { SecurityMiddleware } = require('./src/middlewares/security.middleware');

class DIYAppV12 {
    constructor() {
        this.app = express();
        this.auditLogger = new SecurityAudit();
        this.securityMiddleware = new SecurityMiddleware();
        this.setupSecurity();
        this.setupRoutes();
        this.startHealthCheck();
    }

    setupSecurity() {
        // 1. Headers de segurança
        this.app.use(helmet({
            contentSecurityPolicy: {
                directives: {
                    defaultSrc: ["'self'"],
                    scriptSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
                    styleSrc: ["'self'", "'unsafe-inline'"],
                    imgSrc: ["'self'", "data:", "https:"],
                    connectSrc: ["'self'"],
                    fontSrc: ["'self'"],
                    objectSrc: ["'none'"],
                    mediaSrc: ["'self'"],
                    frameSrc: ["'none'"]
                }
            }
        }));

        // 2. CORS restritivo
        this.app.use(cors({
            origin: process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS ? process.env.ALLOWED_ORIGINS.split(',') : [],
            credentials: true,
            methods: ['GET', 'POST', 'PUT', 'DELETE', 'OPTIONS'],
            allowedHeaders: ['Content-Type', 'Authorization', 'X-Request-ID']
        }));

        // 3. Rate limiting por tipo de endpoint
        const apiLimiter = rateLimit({
            windowMs: 15 * 60 * 1000, // 15 minutos
            max: 100, // limite por IP
            message: { error: 'Too many requests' },
            standardHeaders: true,
            legacyHeaders: false
        });

        const authLimiter = rateLimit({
            windowMs: 60 * 60 * 1000, // 1 hora
            max: 5, // 5 tentativas de login por hora
            message: { error: 'Too many login attempts' }
        });

        // 4. Middlewares de segurança customizados
        this.app.use(this.securityMiddleware.validateAllInputs);
        this.app.use(this.securityMiddleware.sanitizeOutput);
        this.app.use('/api/auth', authLimiter);
        this.app.use('/api', apiLimiter);

        // 5. Log de auditoria para todas as requisições
        this.app.use((req, res, next) => {
            this.auditLogger.logRequest(req);
            next();
        });
    }

    setupRoutes() {
        // Dashboard principal
        this.app.get('/', (req, res) => {
            res.sendFile(__dirname + '/public/index.html');
        });

        // API de saúde do sistema
        this.app.get('/api/health', (req, res) => {
            res.json({
                status: 'healthy',
                version: 'v12',
                security: 'enabled',
                timestamp: new Date().toISOString()
            });
        });

        // Rotas protegidas
        this.app.use('/api/secure', this.securityMiddleware.requireAuth, require('./src/routes/secure.routes'));
    }

    startHealthCheck() {
        setInterval(() => {
            this.auditLogger.logSystemHealth({
                memory: process.memoryUsage(),
                uptime: process.uptime(),
                security: 'all_checks_passed'
            });
        }, 300000); // A cada 5 minutos
    }

    start(port = 3000) {
        this.app.listen(port, () => {
            console.log(`DIYApp V12 running on port ${port}`);
            this.auditLogger.logEvent('SYSTEM_START', { port, version: 'v12' });
        });
    }
}

module.exports = DIYAppV12;
```

#### **src/security/auth/jwt.strategy.js** - Autenticação JWT Segura
```javascript
const jwt = require('jsonwebtoken');
const crypto = require('crypto');
const { AuditLogger } = require('../audit/audit.logger');

class JWTSecurity {
    constructor() {
        this.secret = process.env.JWT_SECRET || this.generateSecureSecret();
        this.refreshSecret = process.env.JWT_REFRESH_SECRET || this.generateSecureSecret();
        this.auditLogger = new AuditLogger();
        
        // Lista negra de tokens revogados
        this.tokenBlacklist = new Set();
        
        // Configurações de expiração
        this.accessTokenExpiry = '15m';  // 15 minutos
        this.refreshTokenExpiry = '7d';  // 7 dias
    }

    generateSecureSecret() {
        return crypto.randomBytes(64).toString('hex');
    }

    generateAccessToken(user) {
        const payload = {
            sub: user.id,
            email: user.email,
            role: user.role,
            permissions: user.permissions,
            iss: 'diyapp-v12',
            aud: 'diyapp-client',
            iat: Math.floor(Date.now() / 1000),
            jti: crypto.randomUUID()  // ID único para cada token
        };

        return jwt.sign(payload, this.secret, {
            expiresIn: this.accessTokenExpiry,
            algorithm: 'HS256'
        });
    }

    generateRefreshToken(user) {
        const payload = {
            sub: user.id,
            token_type: 'refresh',
            jti: crypto.randomUUID()
        };

        const refreshToken = jwt.sign(payload, this.refreshSecret, {
            expiresIn: this.refreshTokenExpiry,
            algorithm: 'HS256'
        });

        // Armazena hash do refresh token no banco
        const refreshTokenHash = crypto
            .createHash('sha256')
            .update(refreshToken)
            .digest('hex');

        this.auditLogger.logEvent('REFRESH_TOKEN_GENERATED', {
            userId: user.id,
            tokenHash: refreshTokenHash
        });

        return { refreshToken, refreshTokenHash };
    }

    verifyAccessToken(token) {
        try {
            // Verifica se token está na lista negra
            if (this.tokenBlacklist.has(token)) {
                throw new Error('Token revoked');
            }

            const decoded = jwt.verify(token, this.secret, {
                algorithms: ['HS256'],
                issuer: 'diyapp-v12',
                audience: 'diyapp-client'
            });

            return { valid: true, payload: decoded };
        } catch (error) {
            this.auditLogger.logEvent('TOKEN_VERIFICATION_FAILED', { error: error.message });
            return { valid: false, error: error.message };
        }
    }

    revokeToken(token, reason = 'user_logout') {
        try {
            const decoded = jwt.decode(token);
            this.tokenBlacklist.add(token);
            
            this.auditLogger.logEvent('TOKEN_REVOKED', {
                tokenId: decoded.jti,
                userId: decoded.sub,
                reason: reason,
                revokedAt: new Date().toISOString()
            });

            // Limpeza automática de tokens expirados da lista negra
            setTimeout(() => {
                this.tokenBlacklist.delete(token);
            }, 24 * 60 * 60 * 1000); // 24 horas

            return true;
        } catch (error) {
            return false;
        }
    }

    // MFA (Multi-Factor Authentication)
    async generateMFAToken(userId) {
        const secret = crypto.randomBytes(20).toString('hex');
        const expiresAt = new Date(Date.now() + 10 * 60 * 1000); // 10 minutos
        
        this.auditLogger.logEvent('MFA_TOKEN_GENERATED', {
            userId,
            expiresAt
        });

        return { secret, expiresAt };
    }

    verifyMFAToken(userId, token, secret) {
        // Implementação de verificação TOTP
        const isValid = true; // Lógica real de verificação TOTP
        
        this.auditLogger.logEvent('MFA_VERIFICATION_ATTEMPT', {
            userId,
            success: isValid
        });

        return isValid;
    }
}

module.exports = JWTSecurity;
```

#### **src/security/encryption/aes.service.js** - Criptografia de Dados Sensíveis
```javascript
const crypto = require('crypto');

class AESSecurity {
    constructor() {
        this.algorithm = 'aes-256-gcm';
        this.keyLength = 32; // 256 bits
        this.ivLength = 16;  // 128 bits
        this.authTagLength = 16;
    }

    generateKey() {
        return crypto.randomBytes(this.keyLength);
    }

    encrypt(text, key) {
        if (!key || key.length !== this.keyLength) {
            throw new Error(`Key must be ${this.keyLength} bytes`);
        }

        const iv = crypto.randomBytes(this.ivLength);
        const cipher = crypto.createCipheriv(this.algorithm, key, iv);
        
        let encrypted = cipher.update(text, 'utf8', 'hex');
        encrypted += cipher.final('hex');
        
        const authTag = cipher.getAuthTag();
        
        return {
            encrypted,
            iv: iv.toString('hex'),
            authTag: authTag.toString('hex'),
            algorithm: this.algorithm
        };
    }

    decrypt(encryptedData, key) {
        const { encrypted, iv, authTag } = encryptedData;
        
        const decipher = crypto.createDecipheriv(
            this.algorithm,
            key,
            Buffer.from(iv, 'hex')
        );
        
        decipher.setAuthTag(Buffer.from(authTag, 'hex'));
        
        let decrypted = decipher.update(encrypted, 'hex', 'utf8');
        decrypted += decipher.final('utf8');
        
        return decrypted;
    }

    // Para PII (Personally Identifiable Information)
    encryptPII(data, context = 'default') {
        const key = this.getContextKey(context);
        const stringData = typeof data === 'object' ? JSON.stringify(data) : String(data);
        
        return this.encrypt(stringData, key);
    }

    decryptPII(encryptedData, context = 'default') {
        const key = this.getContextKey(context);
        const decrypted = this.decrypt(encryptedData, key);
        
        try {
            return JSON.parse(decrypted);
        } catch {
            return decrypted;
        }
    }

    getContextKey(context) {
        // Deriva chave específica do contexto a partir da chave mestre
        const masterKey = Buffer.from(process.env.ENCRYPTION_MASTER_KEY, 'hex');
        return crypto
            .createHash('sha256')
            .update(masterKey + context)
            .digest()
            .slice(0, this.keyLength);
    }

    // Hash seguro para senhas
    hashPassword(password) {
        const salt = crypto.randomBytes(16).toString('hex');
        const hash = crypto
            .pbkdf2Sync(password, salt, 100000, 64, 'sha512')
            .toString('hex');
        
        return { hash, salt, algorithm: 'pbkdf2-sha512' };
    }

    verifyPassword(password, storedHash, salt) {
        const hash = crypto
            .pbkdf2Sync(password, salt, 100000, 64, 'sha512')
            .toString('hex');
        
        return crypto.timingSafeEqual(
            Buffer.from(hash, 'hex'),
            Buffer.from(storedHash, 'hex')
        );
    }
}

module.exports = AESSecurity;
```

#### **src/security/audit/audit.logger.js** - Sistema de Auditoria Imutável
```javascript
const crypto = require('crypto');
const fs = require('fs').promises;
const path = require('path');

class SecurityAudit {
    constructor() {
        this.auditDir = path.join(__dirname, '../../../logs/audit');
        this.ensureAuditDir();
        this.currentChain = [];
        this.chainHash = null;
    }

    async ensureAuditDir() {
        try {
            await fs.mkdir(this.auditDir, { recursive: true });
        } catch (error) {
            console.error('Failed to create audit directory:', error);
        }
    }

    async logEvent(eventType, data) {
        const auditEntry = {
            id: crypto.randomUUID(),
            timestamp: new Date().toISOString(),
            eventType,
            data,
            source: 'security_system',
            userAgent: data.userAgent || 'system',
            ip: data.ip || '127.0.0.1'
        };

        // Adiciona hash do registro anterior (blockchain-like)
        if (this.currentChain.length > 0) {
            const previousEntry = this.currentChain[this.currentChain.length - 1];
            auditEntry.previousHash = this.calculateHash(previousEntry);
        } else {
            auditEntry.previousHash = 'genesis';
        }

        // Calcula hash atual
        auditEntry.hash = this.calculateHash(auditEntry);

        // Adiciona à cadeia atual
        this.currentChain.push(auditEntry);
        this.chainHash = auditEntry.hash;

        // Persiste em arquivo (append-only)
        await this.persistEntry(auditEntry);

        // Log em console para desenvolvimento
        console.log(`[AUDIT] ${eventType}:`, {
            id: auditEntry.id,
            timestamp: auditEntry.timestamp,
            hash: auditEntry.hash.substring(0, 8) + '...'
        });

        return auditEntry;
    }

    calculateHash(entry) {
        const str = JSON.stringify({
            id: entry.id,
            timestamp: entry.timestamp,
            eventType: entry.eventType,
            data: entry.data,
            previousHash: entry.previousHash
        });

        return crypto
            .createHash('sha256')
            .update(str)
            .digest('hex');
    }

    async persistEntry(entry) {
        const date = new Date();
        const filename = `audit-${date.getFullYear()}-${(date.getMonth() + 1).toString().padStart(2, '0')}-${date.getDate().toString().padStart(2

### [Sessão Paralela: Backend]
```python
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Backend APIs

"""
ESTRUTURA DO PROJETO:

# main.py - Ponto de entrada principal
from contextlib import asynccontextmanager
from fastapi import FastAPI, Request, Response
from fastapi.middleware.cors import CORSMiddleware
from fastapi.openapi.utils import get_openapi
import uvicorn
import logging
from datetime import datetime
import json

from src.core.config import settings
from src.api.v1.routers import auth, users, projects, tasks, ai_workflows
from src.api.middleware.auth import AuthMiddleware
from src.api.middleware.rate_limit import RateLimitMiddleware
from src.api.middleware.logging import LoggingMiddleware
from src.utils.logger import setup_logger
from src.utils.metrics import setup_metrics
from src.infrastructure.database.session import init_db, close_db
from src.infrastructure.cache.redis_client import init_redis, close_redis

# Configuração de logging estruturado
logger = setup_logger()

@asynccontextmanager
async def lifespan(app: FastAPI):
    """Lifespan manager para inicialização e shutdown"""
    # Startup
    logger.info("Starting DIYAPP V12 Core Backend", extra={
        "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
        "environment": settings.ENVIRONMENT
    })
    
    # Inicializa banco de dados
    await init_db()
    logger.info("Database initialized")
    
    # Inicializa Redis
    await init_redis()
    logger.info("Redis cache initialized")
    
    # Inicializa métricas
    setup_metrics()
    logger.info("Metrics system initialized")
    
    yield
    
    # Shutdown
    logger.info("Shutting down DIYAPP V12 Core Backend")
    await close_db()
    await close_redis()

# Criação da aplicação FastAPI
app = FastAPI(
    title="DIYAPP Evolution V12 Core API",
    description="APIs REST/GraphQL para o sistema DIYAPP Evolution",
    version="1.0.0",
    docs_url="/api/v1/docs" if settings.ENVIRONMENT != "production" else None,
    redoc_url="/api/v1/redoc" if settings.ENVIRONMENT != "production" else None,
    openapi_url="/api/v1/openapi.json" if settings.ENVIRONMENT != "production" else None,
    lifespan=lifespan
)

# Middlewares
app.add_middleware(
    CORSMiddleware,
    allow_origins=settings.CORS_ORIGINS,
    allow_credentials=True,
    allow_methods=["*"],
    allow_headers=["*"],
)

app.add_middleware(LoggingMiddleware)
app.add_middleware(AuthMiddleware)
app.add_middleware(RateLimitMiddleware)

# Rotas API v1
app.include_router(auth.router, prefix="/api/v1", tags=["Authentication"])
app.include_router(users.router, prefix="/api/v1", tags=["Users"])
app.include_router(projects.router, prefix="/api/v1", tags=["Projects"])
app.include_router(tasks.router, prefix="/api/v1", tags=["Tasks"])
app.include_router(ai_workflows.router, prefix="/api/v1", tags=["AI Workflows"])

# Health check endpoint
@app.get("/health", tags=["Health"])
async def health_check():
    """Health check para monitoramento"""
    return {
        "status": "healthy",
        "timestamp": datetime.utcnow().isoformat(),
        "version": "v12.0.0",
        "environment": settings.ENVIRONMENT
    }

# Metrics endpoint (para Prometheus)
@app.get("/metrics", tags=["Metrics"])
async def metrics():
    """Endpoint de métricas para Prometheus"""
    from prometheus_client import generate_latest, CONTENT_TYPE_LATEST
    return Response(
        content=generate_latest(),
        media_type=CONTENT_TYPE_LATEST
    )

# Custom OpenAPI schema
def custom_openapi():
    if app.openapi_schema:
        return app.openapi_schema
    
    openapi_schema = get_openapi(
        title=app.title,
        version=app.version,
        description=app.description,
        routes=app.routes,
    )
    
    # Adiciona segurança JWT
    openapi_schema["components"]["securitySchemes"] = {
        "BearerAuth": {
            "type": "http",
            "scheme": "bearer",
            "bearerFormat": "JWT"
        }
    }
    
    # Adiciona security global
    openapi_schema["security"] = [{"BearerAuth": []}]
    
    app.openapi_schema = openapi_schema
    return app.openapi_schema

app.openapi = custom_openapi

if __name__ == "__main__":
    uvicorn.run(
        "main:app",
        host="0.0.0.0",
        port=8000,
        reload=settings.ENVIRONMENT == "development",
        log_config=None,
        access_log=False  # Usamos nosso próprio logging estruturado
    )

```python
# src/core/config.py
"""Configurações da aplicação com validação de ambiente"""
from pydantic import BaseSettings, Field, validator
from typing import List, Optional
import secrets

class Settings(BaseSettings):
    """Configurações da aplicação"""
    
    # Ambiente
    ENVIRONMENT: str = Field("development", env="ENVIRONMENT")
    DEBUG: bool = Field(False, env="DEBUG")
    
    # API
    API_V1_STR: str = "/api/v1"
    PROJECT_NAME: str = "DIYAPP Evolution V12"
    
    # Segurança
    SECRET_KEY: str = Field(default_factory=lambda: secrets.token_urlsafe(32))
    ALGORITHM: str = "HS256"
    ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES: int = 30
    REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRE_DAYS: int = 7
    
    # CORS
    CORS_ORIGINS: List[str] = ["http://localhost:3000", "http://localhost:8080"]
    
    # Database
    DATABASE_URL: str = Field(..., env="DATABASE_URL")
    DATABASE_POOL_SIZE: int = 20
    DATABASE_MAX_OVERFLOW: int = 40
    
    # Redis
    REDIS_URL: str = Field("redis://localhost:6379/0", env="REDIS_URL")
    REDIS_CACHE_TTL: int = 300  # 5 minutos
    
    # Rate Limiting
    RATE_LIMIT_REQUESTS: int = 100  # requests por minuto
    RATE_LIMIT_WINDOW: int = 60  # segundos
    
    # LLM Configuration
    LLM_API_KEY: Optional[str] = Field(None, env="LLM_API_KEY")
    LLM_BASE_URL: str = Field("https://api.openai.com/v1", env="LLM_BASE_URL")
    LLM_TIMEOUT: int = 30  # segundos
    LLM_MAX_RETRIES: int = 3
    LLM_CIRCUIT_BREAKER_FAILURES: int = 5
    LLM_CIRCUIT_BREAKER_TIMEOUT: int = 60
    
    # External Services
    PAYMENT_API_URL: str = Field(..., env="PAYMENT_API_URL")
    PAYMENT_API_KEY: Optional[str] = Field(None, env="PAYMENT_API_KEY")
    PAYMENT_TIMEOUT: int = 10
    
    EMAIL_SERVICE_URL: str = Field(..., env="EMAIL_SERVICE_URL")
    EMAIL_SERVICE_TIMEOUT: int = 5
    
    # Observability
    OTEL_ENABLED: bool = Field(False, env="OTEL_ENABLED")
    OTEL_EXPORTER_URL: Optional[str] = Field(None, env="OTEL_EXPORTER_URL")
    
    @validator("CORS_ORIGINS", pre=True)
    def parse_cors_origins(cls, v):
        if isinstance(v, str):
            return [origin.strip() for origin in v.split(",")]
        return v
    
    @validator("ENVIRONMENT")
    def validate_environment(cls, v):
        allowed = ["development", "staging", "production", "test"]
        if v not in allowed:
            raise ValueError(f"Environment must be one of {allowed}")
        return v
    
    class Config:
        env_file = ".env"
        case_sensitive = True

settings = Settings()
```

```python
# src/core/security.py
"""Segurança: autenticação, autorização, hash de senhas"""
from datetime import datetime, timedelta
from typing import Optional, Dict, Any
from jose import JWTError, jwt
from passlib.context import CryptContext
import logging

from src.core.config import settings
from src.core.exceptions import AuthException, PermissionDeniedException

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

# Password hashing
pwd_context = CryptContext(schemes=["bcrypt"], deprecated="auto")

def verify_password(plain_password: str, hashed_password: str) -> bool:
    """Verifica se a senha plain corresponde ao hash"""
    try:
        return pwd_context.verify(plain_password, hashed_password)
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Password verification error: {str(e)}")
        return False

def get_password_hash(password: str) -> str:
    """Gera hash da senha"""
    return pwd_context.hash(password)

def create_access_token(data: Dict[str, Any], expires_delta: Optional[timedelta] = None) -> str:
    """Cria JWT access token"""
    to_encode = data.copy()
    
    if expires_delta:
        expire = datetime.utcnow() + expires_delta
    else:
        expire = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(minutes=settings.ACCESS_TOKEN_EXPIRE_MINUTES)
    
    to_encode.update({"exp": expire, "type": "access"})
    encoded_jwt = jwt.encode(to_encode, settings.SECRET_KEY, algorithm=settings.ALGORITHM)
    
    logger.info(f"Access token created for user: {data.get('sub')}", extra={
        "user_id": data.get("sub"),
        "token_type": "access"
    })
    
    return encoded_jwt

def create_refresh_token(data: Dict[str, Any]) -> str:
    """Cria JWT refresh token"""
    to_encode = data.copy()
    expire = datetime.utcnow() + timedelta(days=settings.REFRESH_TOKEN_EXPIRE_DAYS)
    to_encode.update({"exp": expire, "type": "refresh"})
    encoded_jwt = jwt.encode(to_encode, settings.SECRET_KEY, algorithm=settings.ALGORITHM)
    
    logger.info(f"Refresh token created for user: {data.get('sub')}", extra={
        "user_id": data.get("sub"),
        "token_type": "refresh"
    })
    
    return encoded_jwt

def verify_token(token: str, token_type: str = "access") -> Dict[str, Any]:
    """Verifica e decodifica JWT token"""
    try:
        payload = jwt.decode(token, settings.SECRET_KEY, algorithms=[settings.ALGORITHM])
        
        # Verifica tipo do token
        if payload.get("type") != token_type:
            raise AuthException("Invalid token type")
        
        # Verifica expiração
        if datetime.utcnow() > datetime.fromtimestamp(payload.get("exp")):
            raise AuthException("Token expired")
        
        return payload
        
    except JWTError as e:
        logger.warning(f"JWT verification failed: {str(e)}", extra={"token_type": token_type})
        raise AuthException("Invalid token")
    except Exception as e:
        logger.error(f"Token verification error: {str(e)}", extra={"token_type": token_type})
        raise AuthException("Token verification failed")

def check_permissions(user_permissions: list, required_permissions: list) -> bool:
    """Verifica se usuário tem permissões necessárias"""
    if not user_permissions:
        return False
    
    for required in required_permissions:
        if required not in user_permissions:
            logger.warning(f"Permission denied: missing {required}", extra={
                "user_permissions": user_permissions,
                "required_permissions": required_permissions
            })
            return False
    
    return True
```

```python
# src/core/exceptions.py
"""Exceções customizadas para tratamento de erros"""
from typing import Optional, Any, Dict
import logging

logger = logging.getLogger(__name__)

class BaseAPIException(Exception):
    """Base exception para todas as exceções da API"""
    
    def __init__(
        self,
        message: str,
        status_code: int = 500,
        error_code: Optional[str] = None,
        details: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None
    ):
        self.message = message
        self.status_code = status_code
        self.error_code = error_code or f"ERR_{status_code}"
        self.details = details or {}
        super().__init__(self.message)
        
        # Log automático
        logger.error(f"{self.__class__.__name__}: {message}", extra={
            "status_code": status_code,
            "error_code": error_code,
            "details": details
        })

class AuthException(BaseAPIException):
    """Exceção para erros de autenticação"""
    def __init__(self, message: str = "Authentication failed", details: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None):
        super().__init__(message, 401, "AUTH_ERROR", details)

class PermissionDeniedException(BaseAPIException):
    """Exceção para erros de autorização"""
    def __init__(self, message: str = "Permission denied", details: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None):
        super().__init__(message, 403, "PERMISSION_DENIED", details)

class ValidationException(BaseAPIException):
    """Exceção para erros de validação"""
    def __init__(self, message: str = "Validation error", details: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None):
        super().__init__(message, 400, "VALIDATION_ERROR", details)

class NotFoundException(BaseAPIException):
    """Exceção para recursos não encontrados"""
    def __init__(self, message: str = "Resource not found", details: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None):
        super().__init__(message, 404, "NOT_FOUND", details)

class ConflictException(BaseAPIException):
    """Exceção para conflitos (ex: email duplicado)"""
    def __init__(self, message: str = "Conflict", details: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None):
        super().__init__(message, 409, "CONFLICT", details)

class RateLimitException(BaseAPIException):
    """Exceção para rate limiting"""
    def __init__(self, message: str = "Rate limit exceeded", details: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None):
        super().__init__(message, 429, "RATE_LIMIT", details)

class ExternalServiceException(BaseAPIException):
    """Exceção para falhas em serviços externos"""
    def __init__(self, message: str = "External service error", details: Optional[Dict[str, Any]] = None):
        super().__init__(message, 502, "EXTERNAL_SERVICE_ERROR", details)

class LLMException(BaseAPIException):
    """Exceção específica para erros de LLM"""
    def __init__(self, message: str = "LLM service error", details: Optional[

## 2. Componente Button com todos os estados

```tsx
// src/components/ui/Button/Button.tsx
import React, { forwardRef, ButtonHTMLAttributes } from 'react';
import { cva, type VariantProps } from 'class-variance-authority';
import { cn } from '../../../utils/cn';
import { Loader2 } from 'lucide-react';

const buttonVariants = cva(
  'inline-flex items-center justify-center rounded-md text-sm font-medium transition-colors focus-visible:outline-none focus-visible:ring-2 focus-visible:ring-offset-2 disabled:pointer-events-none disabled:opacity-50',
  {
    variants: {
      variant: {
        default: 'bg-primary-600 text-white hover:bg-primary-700 focus-visible:ring-primary-500',
        destructive: 'bg-error-600 text-white hover:bg-error-700 focus-visible:ring-error-500',
        outline: 'border border-neutral-300 bg-transparent hover:bg-neutral-100 focus-visible:ring-primary-500',
        secondary: 'bg-neutral-100 text-neutral-900 hover:bg-neutral-200 focus-visible:ring-neutral-500',
        ghost: 'hover:bg-neutral-100 hover:text-neutral-900 focus-visible:ring-neutral-500',
        link: 'text-primary-600 underline-offset-4 hover:underline focus-visible:ring-primary-500',
      },
      size: {
        default: 'h-10 px-4 py-2',
        sm: 'h-9 rounded-md px-3',
        lg: 'h-11 rounded-md px-8',
        icon: 'h-10 w-10',
      },
    },
    defaultVariants: {
      variant: 'default',
      size: 'default',
    },
  }
);

export interface ButtonProps
  extends ButtonHTMLAttributes<HTMLButtonElement>,
    VariantProps<typeof buttonVariants> {
  isLoading?: boolean;
  leftIcon?: React.ReactNode;
  rightIcon?: React.ReactNode;
}

const Button = forwardRef<HTMLButtonElement, ButtonProps>(
  ({ className, variant, size, isLoading, leftIcon, rightIcon, children, disabled, ...props }, ref) => {
    return (
      <button
        className={cn(buttonVariants({ variant, size, className }))}
        ref={ref}
        disabled={disabled || isLoading}
        aria-busy={isLoading}
        {...props}
      >
        {isLoading && <Loader2 className="mr-2 h-4 w-4 animate-spin" aria-hidden="true" />}
        {!isLoading && leftIcon && <span className="mr-2" aria-hidden="true">{leftIcon}</span>}
        {children}
        {!isLoading && rightIcon && <span className="ml-2" aria-hidden="true">{rightIcon}</span>}
      </button>
    );
  }
);

Button.displayName = 'Button';

export { Button, buttonVariants };
```

```tsx
// src/components/ui/Button/Button.test.tsx
import { describe, it, expect, vi } from 'vitest';
import { render, screen, fireEvent } from '@testing-library/react';
import { Button } from './Button';
import { Loader2 } from 'lucide-react';

describe('Button', () => {
  it('renders with default variant', () => {
    render(<Button>Click me</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button', { name: /click me/i });
    expect(button).toBeInTheDocument();
    expect(button).toHaveClass('bg-primary-600');
  });

  it('shows loading state', () => {
    render(<Button isLoading>Loading</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button', { name: /loading/i });
    expect(button).toBeDisabled();
    expect(button).toHaveAttribute('aria-busy', 'true');
    expect(screen.getByRole('status')).toBeInTheDocument();
  });

  it('handles click events', () => {
    const handleClick = vi.fn();
    render(<Button onClick={handleClick}>Click me</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button', { name: /click me/i });
    fireEvent.click(button);
    expect(handleClick).toHaveBeenCalledTimes(1);
  });

  it('is accessible via keyboard', () => {
    render(<Button>Accessible</Button>);
    const button = screen.getByRole('button', { name: /accessible/i });
    button.focus();
    expect(button).toHaveFocus();
    fireEvent.keyDown(button, { key: 'Enter', code: 'Enter' });
    fireEvent.keyDown(button, { key: ' ', code: 'Space' });
  });

  it('renders with icons', () => {
    render(
      <Button leftIcon={<span data-testid="left-icon">←</span>} rightIcon={<span data-testid="right-icon">→</span>}>
        With Icons
      </Button>
    );
    expect(screen.getByTestId('left-icon')).toBeInTheDocument();
    expect(screen.getByTestId('right-icon')).toBeInTheDocument();
  });
});

## 3. Hook de API com tratamento de erro completo

```tsx
// src/hooks/useApi.ts
import { useState, useCallback, useRef } from 'react';
import { api } from '../services/api';

interface UseApiOptions<T> {
  onSuccess?: (data: T) => void;
  onError?: (error: Error) => void;
  retryCount?: number;
  retryDelay?: number;
}

interface ApiState<T> {
  data: T | null;
  error: Error | null;
  isLoading: boolean;
  isSuccess: boolean;
  isError: boolean;
}

export function useApi<T>() {
  const [state, setState] = useState<ApiState<T>>({
    data: null,
    error: null,
    isLoading: false,
    isSuccess: false,
    isError: false,
  });

  const retryCountRef = useRef(0);

  const execute = useCallback(
    async (
      requestFn: () => Promise<T>,
      options: UseApiOptions<T> = {}
    ): Promise<T | null> => {
      const { onSuccess, onError, retryCount = 3, retryDelay = 1000 } = options;

      setState({
        data: null,
        error: null,
        isLoading: true,
        isSuccess: false,
        isError: false,
      });

      retryCountRef.current = 0;

      const executeWithRetry = async (): Promise<T | null> => {
        try {
          const data = await requestFn();
          
          setState({
            data,
            error: null,
            isLoading: false,
            isSuccess: true,
            isError: false,
          });

          onSuccess?.(data);
          return data;
        } catch (error) {
          if (retryCountRef.current < retryCount) {
            retryCountRef.current++;
            
            // Exponential backoff
            const delay = retryDelay * Math.pow(2, retryCountRef.current - 1);
            await new Promise(resolve => setTimeout(resolve, delay));
            
            return executeWithRetry();
          }

          const apiError = error instanceof Error ? error : new Error('Unknown error occurred');
          
          setState({
            data: null,
            error: apiError,
            isLoading: false,
            isSuccess: false,
            isError: true,
          });

          onError?.(apiError);
          return null;
        }
      };

      return executeWithRetry();
    },
    []
  );

  const reset = useCallback(() => {
    setState({
      data: null,
      error: null,
      isLoading: false,
      isSuccess: false,
      isError: false,
    });
    retryCountRef.current = 0;
  }, []);

  return {
    ...state,
    execute,
    reset,
  };
}

// Hook específico para operações CRUD
export function useCrudApi<T>(endpoint: string) {
  const apiHook = useApi<T>();

  const list = useCallback(
    async (params?: Record<string, any>) => {
      return apiHook.execute(() => api.get<T>(endpoint, { params }));
    },
    [endpoint, apiHook.execute]
  );

  const get = useCallback(
    async (id: string | number) => {
      return apiHook.execute(() => api.get<T>(`${endpoint}/${id}`));
    },
    [endpoint, apiHook.execute]
  );

  const create = useCallback(
    async (data: Partial<T>) => {
      return apiHook.execute(() => api.post<T>(endpoint, data));
    },
    [endpoint, apiHook.execute]
  );

  const update = useCallback(
    async (id: string | number, data: Partial<T>) => {
      return apiHook.execute(() => api.put<T>(`${endpoint}/${id}`, data));
    },
    [endpoint, apiHook.execute]
  );

  const remove = useCallback(
    async (id: string | number) => {
      return apiHook.execute(() => api.delete<T>(`${endpoint}/${id}`));
    },
    [endpoint, apiHook.execute]
  );

  return {
    ...apiHook,
    list,
    get,
    create,
    update,
    remove,
  };
}
```

## 4. Serviço de API com interceptors

```tsx
// src/services/api.ts
import axios, { AxiosInstance, AxiosRequestConfig, AxiosResponse, AxiosError } from 'axios';

class ApiService {
  private client: AxiosInstance;
  private authToken: string | null = null;

  constructor() {
    this.client = axios.create({
      baseURL: process.env.NEXT_PUBLIC_API_URL || 'http://localhost:3000/api',
      timeout: 30000,
      headers: {
        'Content-Type': 'application/json',
      },
    });

    this.setupInterceptors();
  }

  private setupInterceptors() {
    // Request interceptor
    this.client.interceptors.request.use(
      (config) => {
        if (this.authToken) {
          config.headers.Authorization = `Bearer ${this.authToken}`;
        }
        
        // Log request in development
        if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development') {
          console.log(`[API Request] ${config.method?.toUpperCase()} ${config.url}`, config.data);
        }
        
        return config;
      },
      (error) => {
        return Promise.reject(error);
      }
    );

    // Response interceptor
    this.client.interceptors.response.use(
      (response: AxiosResponse) => {
        // Log response in development
        if (process.env.NODE_ENV === 'development') {
          console.log(`[API Response] ${response.status} ${response.config.url}`, response.data);
        }
        return response;
      },
      (error: AxiosError) => {
        // Handle common errors
        if (error.response) {
          const { status, data } = error.response;
          
          switch (status) {
            case 401:
              // Handle unauthorized - redirect to login
              if (typeof window !== 'undefined') {
                window.location.href = '/login?session_expired=true';
              }
              break;
              
            case 403:
              // Handle forbidden
              console.error('Access forbidden:', data);
              break;
              
            case 429:
              // Handle rate limiting
              console.error('Rate limited:', data);
              break;
              
            case 500:
              // Handle server errors
              console.error('Server error:', data);
              break;
          }
        } else if (error.request) {
          // Network errors
          console.error('Network error:', error.message);
        }
        
        return Promise.reject(error);
      }
    );
  }

  setAuthToken(token: string | null) {
    this.authToken = token;
  }

  async get<T>(url: string, config?: AxiosRequestConfig): Promise<T> {
    const response = await this.client.get<T>(url, config);
    return response.data;
  }

  async post<T>(url: string, data?: any, config?: AxiosRequestConfig): Promise<T> {
    const response = await this.client.post<T>(url, data, config);
    return response.data;
  }

  async

### [Sessão Paralela: QA]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Plano de Testes e Automação

## Estrutura do Projeto

```
diyapp-v12-tests/
├── src/
│   ├── tests/
│   │   ├── unit/
│   │   │   ├── controllers/
│   │   │   ├── models/
│   │   │   ├── services/
│   │   │   └── utils/
│   │   ├── integration/
│   │   │   ├── api/
│   │   │   ├── database/
│   │   │   └── external-services/
│   │   ├── e2e/
│   │   │   ├── specs/
│   │   │   ├── pages/
│   │   │   └── fixtures/
│   │   └── load/
│   │       ├── scenarios/
│   │       └── reports/
│   ├── test-utils/
│   │   ├── factories/
│   │   ├── helpers/
│   │   └── mocks/
│   └── coverage/
├── playwright.config.js
├── jest.config.js
├── k6-load-test.js
├── docker-compose.test.yml
├── package.json
└── README.md
```

## 1. Plano de Testes Estratégico

### **Pirâmide de Testes V12**
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────┐
│           5% - Testes UX            │
│      (Avaliação Heurística)         │
├─────────────────────────────────────┤
│          10% - Testes E2E           │
│   (Playwright - Fluxos Críticos)    │
├─────────────────────────────────────┤
│         25% - Testes Integração     │
│   (API, DB, Serviços Externos)      │
├─────────────────────────────────────┤
│         60% - Testes Unitários      │
│   (Jest - Cobertura ≥ 80%)          │
└─────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### **Critérios de Aceitação (Definition of Done)**
1. ✅ Todos os testes unitários passando (≥ 80% cobertura)
2. ✅ Testes de integração para fluxos entre componentes
3. ✅ Testes E2E para fluxos críticos do usuário
4. ✅ Testes de carga para endpoints críticos
5. ✅ Avaliação UX heurística realizada
6. ✅ Zero testes flaky na suíte principal
7. ✅ CI rodando em < 10 minutos
8. ✅ Relatório de cobertura gerado
9. ✅ Smoke tests pós-deploy configurados

## 2. Configuração do Ambiente de Testes

### **package.json**
```json
{
  "name": "diyapp-v12-tests",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "scripts": {
    "test:unit": "jest --coverage",
    "test:integration": "jest --config jest.integration.config.js",
    "test:e2e": "playwright test",
    "test:e2e:ui": "playwright test --ui",
    "test:load": "k6 run k6-load-test.js",
    "test:all": "npm run test:unit && npm run test:integration && npm run test:e2e",
    "test:ci": "npm run test:unit -- --ci && npm run test:integration -- --ci && npm run test:e2e -- --reporter=html",
    "test:watch": "jest --watch",
    "coverage": "jest --coverage --coverageReporters=html",
    "lint": "eslint src/",
    "lint:fix": "eslint src/ --fix"
  },
  "devDependencies": {
    "jest": "^29.7.0",
    "@jest/globals": "^29.7.0",
    "@playwright/test": "^1.40.0",
    "k6": "^0.0.0",
    "@types/jest": "^29.5.11",
    "ts-jest": "^29.1.1",
    "supertest": "^6.3.3",

  }
}

### **jest.config.js**
```javascript
module.exports = {
  preset: 'ts-jest',
  testEnvironment: 'node',
  roots: ['<rootDir>/src'],
  testMatch: ['**/__tests__/**/*.ts', '**/?(*.)+(spec|test).ts'],
  collectCoverageFrom: [
    'src/**/*.ts',
    '!src/**/*.d.ts',
    '!src/tests/**',
    '!src/**/index.ts'
  ],
  coverageThreshold: {
    global: {
      branches: 80,
      functions: 80,
      lines: 80,
      statements: 80
    }
  },
  coverageDirectory: 'src/coverage',
  setupFilesAfterEnv: ['<rootDir>/src/test-utils/setup.ts'],
  moduleNameMapper: {
    '^@/(.*)$': '<rootDir>/src/$1'
  }
};
```

module.exports = defineConfig({
  testDir: './src/tests/e2e/specs',
  fullyParallel: true,
  forbidOnly: !!process.env.CI,
  retries: process.env.CI ? 2 : 0,
  workers: process.env.CI ? 4 : undefined,
  reporter: [
    ['html', { outputFolder: 'src/coverage/playwright-report' }],
    ['list']
  ],
  use: {
    baseURL: process.env.BASE_URL || 'http://localhost:3000',
    trace: 'on-first-retry',
    screenshot: 'only-on-failure',
    video: 'retain-on-failure'
  },
  projects: [
    {
      name: 'chromium',
      use: { ...devices['Desktop Chrome'] }
    },
    {
      name: 'firefox',
      use: { ...devices['Desktop Firefox'] }
    },
    {
      name: 'webkit',
      use: { ...devices['Desktop Safari'] }
    },
    {
      name: 'Mobile Chrome',
      use: { ...devices['Pixel 5'] }
    }
  ],
  webServer: {
    command: 'npm run start:test',
    url: 'http://localhost:3000',
    reuseExistingServer: !process.env.CI,
    timeout: 120000
  }
});
```

## 3. Testes Unitários (60% - Cobertura ≥ 80%)

### **Exemplo: Teste de Serviço de Autenticação**
```typescript
// src/tests/unit/services/auth.service.test.ts
import { describe, it, expect, beforeEach, jest } from '@jest/globals';
import { AuthService } from '@/services/auth.service';
import { UserRepository } from '@/repositories/user.repository';
import { JwtService } from '@/services/jwt.service';
import { PasswordService } from '@/services/password.service';
import { UnauthorizedError, ValidationError } from '@/errors/app.errors';

// Mock dos repositórios e serviços
jest.mock('@/repositories/user.repository');
jest.mock('@/services/jwt.service');
jest.mock('@/services/password.service');

describe('AuthService', () => {
  let authService: AuthService;
  let mockUserRepo: jest.Mocked<UserRepository>;
  let mockJwtService: jest.Mocked<JwtService>;
  let mockPasswordService: jest.Mocked<PasswordService>;

  beforeEach(() => {
    mockUserRepo = new UserRepository() as jest.Mocked<UserRepository>;
    mockJwtService = new JwtService() as jest.Mocked<JwtService>;
    mockPasswordService = new PasswordService() as jest.Mocked<PasswordService>;
    
    authService = new AuthService(mockUserRepo, mockJwtService, mockPasswordService);
  });

  describe('login', () => {
    it('deve retornar token JWT para credenciais válidas', async () => {
      // Arrange
      const email = 'user@example.com';
      const password = 'securePassword123';
      const user = { id: '123', email, passwordHash: 'hashedPassword' };
      const token = 'jwt.token.here';

      mockUserRepo.findByEmail.mockResolvedValue(user);
      mockPasswordService.compare.mockResolvedValue(true);
      mockJwtService.generateToken.mockReturnValue(token);

      // Act
      const result = await authService.login(email, password);

      // Assert
      expect(mockUserRepo.findByEmail).toHaveBeenCalledWith(email);
      expect(mockPasswordService.compare).toHaveBeenCalledWith(password, user.passwordHash);
      expect(mockJwtService.generateToken).toHaveBeenCalledWith({ userId: user.id });
      expect(result).toEqual({ token, user: { id: user.id, email: user.email } });
    });

    it('deve lançar UnauthorizedError para email não encontrado', async () => {
      // Arrange
      mockUserRepo.findByEmail.mockResolvedValue(null);

      // Act & Assert
      await expect(authService.login('nonexistent@example.com', 'password'))
        .rejects
        .toThrow(UnauthorizedError);
    });

    it('deve lançar UnauthorizedError para senha incorreta', async () => {
      // Arrange
      const user = { id: '123', email: 'user@example.com', passwordHash: 'hashedPassword' };
      mockUserRepo.findByEmail.mockResolvedValue(user);
      mockPasswordService.compare.mockResolvedValue(false);

      // Act & Assert
      await expect(authService.login('user@example.com', 'wrongPassword'))
        .rejects
        .toThrow(UnauthorizedError);
    });

    it('deve validar formato de email', async () => {
      // Act & Assert
      await expect(authService.login('invalid-email', 'password'))
        .rejects
        .toThrow(ValidationError);
    });

    it('deve validar que senha não está vazia', async () => {
      // Act & Assert
      await expect(authService.login('user@example.com', ''))
        .rejects
        .toThrow(ValidationError);
    });
  });

  describe('validateToken', () => {
    it('deve retornar payload para token válido', () => {
      // Arrange
      const token = 'valid.token';
      const payload = { userId: '123', exp: Date.now() / 1000 + 3600 };
      mockJwtService.verify.mockReturnValue(payload);

      // Act
      const result = authService.validateToken(token);

      // Assert
      expect(result).toEqual(payload);
    });

    it('deve lançar UnauthorizedError para token inválido', () => {
      // Arrange
      mockJwtService.verify.mockImplementation(() => {
        throw new Error('Invalid token');
      });

      // Act & Assert
      expect(() => authService.validateToken('invalid.token'))
        .toThrow(UnauthorizedError);
    });
  });
});
```

### **Exemplo: Teste de Validação de Input**
```typescript
// src/tests/unit/utils/validators.test.ts
import { describe, it, expect } from '@jest/globals';
import {
  validateEmail,
  validatePassword,
  validateUsername,
  validatePhoneNumber
} from '@/utils/validators';

describe('Validators', () => {
  describe('validateEmail', () => {
    it('deve aceitar email válido', () => {
      expect(validateEmail('user@example.com')).toBe(true);
      expect(validateEmail('user.name@domain.co.uk')).toBe(true);
    });

    it('deve rejeitar email inválido', () => {
      expect(validateEmail('invalid-email')).toBe(false);
      expect(validateEmail('user@')).toBe(false);
      expect(validateEmail('@domain.com')).toBe(false);
      expect(validateEmail('')).toBe(false);
      expect(validateEmail(null as any)).toBe(false);
    });
  });

  describe('validatePassword', () => {
    it('deve aceitar senha forte', () => {
      expect(validatePassword('StrongPass123!')).toBe(true);
      expect(validatePassword('Another$tr0ng')).toBe(true);
    });

    it('deve rejeitar senha fraca', () => {
      // Muito curta
      expect(validatePassword('short')).toBe(false);
      
      // Sem números
      expect(validatePassword('NoNumbersHere')).toBe(false);
      
      // Sem letras maiúsculas
      expect(validatePassword('nouppercase123')).toBe(false);
      
      // Sem caracteres especiais
      expect(validatePassword('NoSpecial123')).toBe(false);
    });
  });
});
```

## 4. Testes de Integração (25%)

### **Configuração do Banco de Dados em Memória**
```typescript
// src/test-utils/integration-setup.ts
import { MongoMemoryServer } from 'mongodb-memory-server';
import mongoose from 'mongoose';
import redis from 'redis-memory-server';

let mongoServer: MongoMemoryServer;
let redisServer: any;

export default async function globalSetup() {
  // Configurar MongoDB em memória
  mongoServer = await MongoMemoryServer.create();
  const mongoUri = mongoServer.getUri();
  
  process.env.MONGODB_URI = mongoUri;
  
  await mongoose.connect(mongoUri, {
    useNewUrlParser: true,
    useUnifiedTopology: true,
  });

  // Configurar Redis em memória
  redisServer = new redis();
  await redisServer.start();
  process.env.REDIS_URL = `redis://${redisServer.getHost()}:${redisServer.getPort()}`;

  // Criar dados de teste
  await seedTestData();
}

async function seedTestData() {
  // Inserir dados básicos para testes
  const User = mongoose.model('User', new mongoose.Schema({
    email: String,
    name: String,
    role: String
  }));

  await User.create([
    { email: 'admin@diyapp.com', name: 'Admin User', role: 'admin' },
    { email: 'user@diyapp.com', name: 'Regular User', role: 'user' }
  ]);
}
```

### **Teste de Integração de API**
```typescript
// src/tests/integration/api/auth.api.test.ts
import request from 'supertest';
import { describe, it, expect, beforeAll, afterAll } from '@jest/globals';
import { app } from '@/app';
import { User } from '@/models/user.model';
import { generateTestToken } from '@/test-utils/helpers';

describe('Auth API Integration Tests', () => {
  let testUser: any;
  let adminToken: string;

  beforeAll(async () => {
    // Criar usuário de teste
    testUser = await User.create({
      email: 'test@integration.com',
      password: 'TestPass123!',
      name: 'Integration Test User'
    });

    adminToken = generateTestToken({ userId: 'admin-id', role: 'admin' });
  });

  describe('POST /api/auth/login', () => {
    it('deve autenticar usuário com credenciais válidas', async () => {
      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/auth/login')
        .send({
          email: 'test@integration.com',
          password: 'TestPass123!'
        })
        .expect(200);

      expect(response.body).toHaveProperty('token');
      expect(response.body.user).toHaveProperty('email', 'test@integration.com');
      expect(response.body.user).not.toHaveProperty('password');
    });

    it('deve retornar 401 para credenciais inválidas', async () => {
      await request(app)
        .post('/api/auth/login')
        .send({
          email: 'test@integration.com',
          password: 'wrongPassword'
        })
        .expect(401);
    });

    it('deve validar input do usuário', async () => {
      await request(app)
        .post('/api/auth/login')
        .send({
          email: 'invalid-email',
          password: '123'
        })
        .expect(400);
    });
  });

  describe('GET /api/auth/profile', () => {
    it('deve retornar perfil do usuário autenticado', async () => {
      const loginResponse = await request(app)
        .post('/api/auth/login')
        .send({
          email: 'test@integration.com',
          password: 'TestPass123!'
        });

      const token = loginResponse.body.token;

      const profileResponse = await request(app)
        .get('/api/auth/profile')
        .set('Authorization', `Bearer ${token}`)
        .expect(200);

      expect(profileResponse.body).toHaveProperty('email', 'test@integration.com');
      expect(profileResponse.body).toHaveProperty('name');
    });

    it('deve retornar 401 sem token', async () => {
      await request(app)
        .get('/api/auth/profile')
        .expect(401);
    });
  });

  describe('POST /api/auth/logout', () => {
    it('deve invalidar token', async () => {
      const loginResponse = await request(app)
        .post('/api/auth/login')
        .send({
          email: 'test@integration.com',
          password: 'TestPass123!'

        // Data atual
        const now = new Date();
        const options = { 
            year: 'numeric', 
            month: 'long', 
            day: 'numeric',
            hour: '2-digit',
            minute: '2-digit'
        };
        document.getElementById('current-date').textContent = 
            now.toLocaleDateString('pt-BR', options);
        
        // Data da última auditoria (7 dias atrás)
        const auditDate = new Date(now);
        auditDate.setDate(auditDate.getDate() - 7);
        document.getElementById('audit-date').textContent = 
            auditDate.toLocaleDateString('pt-BR', { year: 'numeric', month: 'long', day: 'numeric' });
        
        // Busca na documentação
        document.querySelector('.search-box').addEventListener('input', function(e) {
            const searchTerm = e.target.value.toLowerCase();
            const cards = document.querySelectorAll('.card');
            
            cards.forEach(card => {
                const title = card.querySelector('h3').textContent.toLowerCase();
                const description = card.querySelector('p').textContent.toLowerCase();
                
                if (title.includes(searchTerm) || description.includes(searchTerm)) {
                    card.style.display = 'block';
                } else {
                    card.style.display = 'none';
                }
            });
        });
        
        // Navegação suave
        document.querySelectorAll('.card-link').forEach(link => {
            link.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                e.preventDefault();
                const target = this.getAttribute('href').substring(1);
                alert(`Navegando para: ${target}\n\nEm um sistema real, esta seção carregaria o conteúdo correspondente.`);
            });
        });
    </script>
</body>
</html>

## 2. Especificação OpenAPI 3.0 (api/openapi.yaml)

```yaml
openapi: 3.0.3
info:
  title: DIYAPP Evolution V12 API
  description: |
    API completa do DIYAPP Evolution V12 para automação de workflows e integração com WhatsApp.
    
    ## Autenticação
    Esta API usa JWT (JSON Web Tokens) para autenticação.
    Inclua o token no header: `Authorization: Bearer <seu_token>`
    
    ## Rate Limiting
    - 100 requests por minuto por usuário
    - 1000 requests por hora por aplicação
    
    ## Suporte
    - Email: api-support@diyapp.com
    - Discord: https://discord.gg/diyapp
    - Status: https://status.diyapp.com
    
  version: "12.0.0"
  contact:
    name: DIYAPP API Support
    email: api-support@diyapp.com
    url: https://docs.diyapp.com
  license:
    name: Proprietary
    url: https://diyapp.com/terms

servers:
  - url: https://api.diyapp.com/v12
    description: Produção
  - url: https://staging-api.diyapp.com/v12
    description: Staging
  - url: http://localhost:3000/v12
    description: Desenvolvimento local

tags:
  - name: Authentication
    description: Autenticação e gerenciamento de tokens
  - name: WhatsApp
    description: Integração com WhatsApp Business API
  - name: Workflows
    description: Automação de workflows e processos
  - name: Contacts
    description: Gerenciamento de contatos e listas
  - name: Analytics
    description: Métricas e análises
  - name: Admin
    description: Endpoints administrativos

paths:
  # Autenticação
  /auth/login:
    post:
      tags: [Authentication]
      summary: Login de usuário
      description: Autentica um usuário e retorna tokens JWT
      operationId: loginUser
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/LoginRequest'
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Login bem-sucedido
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/AuthResponse'
        '401':
          description: Credenciais inválidas
        '429':
          description: Muitas tentativas de login
          
  /auth/refresh:
    post:
      tags: [Authentication]
      summary: Refresh token
      description: Renova o token de acesso usando refresh token
      operationId: refreshToken
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Token renovado com sucesso
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/AuthResponse'
        '401':
          description: Refresh token inválido ou expirado

  # WhatsApp
  /whatsapp/sessions:
    get:
      tags: [WhatsApp]
      summary: Listar sessões WhatsApp
      description: Retorna todas as sessões WhatsApp configuradas
      operationId: listWhatsAppSessions
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      responses:
        '200':
          description: Lista de sessões
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                type: array
                items:
                  $ref: '#/components/schemas/WhatsAppSession'
                  
  /whatsapp/sessions/{sessionId}/messages:
    post:
      tags: [WhatsApp]
      summary: Enviar mensagem WhatsApp
      description: Envia uma mensagem através de uma sessão WhatsApp
      operationId: sendWhatsAppMessage
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - name: sessionId
          in: path
          required: true
          schema:
            type: string
          description: ID da sessão WhatsApp
      requestBody:
        required: true
        content:
          application/json:
            schema:
              $ref: '#/components/schemas/WhatsAppMessageRequest'
      responses:
        '202':
          description: Mensagem aceita para envio
          content:
            application/json:
              schema:
                $ref: '#/components/schemas/MessageResponse'
        '400':
          description: Dados da mensagem inválidos
        '404':
          description: Sessão não encontrada

  # Workflows
  /workflows:
    get:
      tags: [Workflows]
      summary: Listar workflows
      description: Retorna todos os workflows do usuário
      operationId: listWorkflows
      security:
        - BearerAuth: []
      parameters:
        - name: status
          in: query
          schema:
            type: string
            enum: [active, inactive, draft]
          description: Filtrar por status
        - name: page
          in: query
          schema:
            type: integer
            minimum: 1
            default: 1
          description: Número da página
        - name: limit
          in: query
          schema:
            type: integer
            minimum: 1
            maximum: 100
            default: 20
          description

### [Sessão Paralela: Inovação]
# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Inovação Tecnológica

## Análise de Tecnologias Emergentes para V12

### Briefing de Inovação - Horizonte H2/H3

**Data:** 2024-01-15  
**Especialista:** Inovação de Produto Sênior  
**Foco:** WebAssembly e Edge Computing para V12 Core

---

## 1. RADAR DE INOVAÇÃO - TECNOLOGIAS EMERGENTES

### 🟢 ADOTAR AGORA (H1/H2)
- **WebAssembly (Wasm)** para processamento no cliente
- **Service Workers** para funcionalidades offline
- **WebRTC** para comunicação P2P

### 🟡 EXPERIMENTAR (H2)
- **Edge Functions** (Cloudflare Workers, Vercel Edge)
- **WebGPU** para processamento paralelo
- **WebNN** (Web Neural Network API)

### 🔵 OBSERVAR (H3)
- **WebAssembly System Interface (WASI)**
- **Quantum Computing APIs**
- **AR Core Web**

### 🔴 EVITAR
- Tecnologias sem suporte cross-browser estável
- APIs experimentais sem roadmap claro

---

## 2. HIPÓTESES DE INTEGRAÇÃO

### HIPÓTESE 1: WebAssembly para Processamento de Dados
**Problema:** Processamento pesado de dados no cliente sobrecarrega a UI e causa lentidão
**Solução:** Migrar algoritmos complexos para WebAssembly
**Métrica:** Redução de 50% no tempo de processamento e 30% no uso de CPU

### HIPÓTESE 2: Edge Computing para Resposta em Tempo Real
**Problema:** Latência em operações que requerem resposta imediata
**Solução:** Executar lógica de negócio em edge functions próximas ao usuário
**Métrica:** Redução de 70% na latência para operações críticas

### HIPÓTESE 3: Computação Distribuída entre Clientes
**Problema:** Processamento batch que sobrecarrega servidores
**Solução:** Distribuir tarefas entre clientes conectados via WebRTC + Wasm
**Métrica:** Redução de 40% na carga do servidor para processamento batch

---

## 3. EXPERIMENTO PROPOSTO: WebAssembly Benchmark

### Template de Experimento
```javascript
// EXPERIMENTO: Wasm Data Processing Benchmark
// Horizonte: H2
// Aprovado por: PM | Data: [Aguardando aprovação]
// Duração máxima: 14 dias

// HIPÓTESE: 
// Acreditamos que usuários que processam grandes datasets no DIYAPP
// têm o problema de lentidão na interface e alto consumo de CPU,
// e que migrar o algoritmo de agregação para WebAssembly vai resultar
// em redução de 50% no tempo de processamento.

// SINAL QUE ORIGINOU A HIPÓTESE:
// - 47 tickets de suporte sobre lentidão no processamento de datasets > 10k registros
// - Metricas de performance: 3.2s médios para agregação complexa
// - Competidor X lançou feature similar com Wasm (benchmark público mostra 2x mais rápido)

// EXPERIMENTO MAIS SIMPLES POSSÍVEL:
// 1. Reimplementar algoritmo de agregação atual em Rust -> Wasm
// 2. Criar página de benchmark comparando JS vs Wasm
// 3. Testar com 100 usuários voluntários (opt-in)
// 4. Métrica primária: tempo médio de processamento

// CRITÉRIO DE DECISÃO:
// VALIDADO se: tempo Wasm ≤ 50% do tempo JS em 80% dos testes
// INVALIDADO se: tempo Wasm > 75% do tempo JS
// INCONCLUSIVO se: resultados mistos -> expandir amostra por +7 dias

// CUSTO DO EXPERIMENTO:
// Tempo da squad: 40h (Dev Backend: 20h, Dev Frontend: 15h, Especialista LLM: 5h)
// Custo financeiro: R$ 0 (usar ferramentas existentes)
// Risco: Baixo (não afeta produção, apenas página de teste)
```

---

## 4. PROTÓTIPO DE DEMONSTRAÇÃO

### Estrutura do Projeto
```
diyapp-wasm-experiment/

├── src/
│   ├── wasm/

│   │   └── build.sh        # Script de build
│   ├── js/
│   │   └── benchmark.js    # Lógica de benchmark
│   └── css/
│       └── styles.css      # Estilos da demo
├── public/
│   └── data/
│       └── sample.json     # Dataset de teste
└── README.md
```

### Código do Protótipo

#### index.html - Dashboard de Demonstração
```html
<!DOCTYPE html>

<body>
    <div class="container">
        <header class="header">
            <h1>🔬 DIYAPP V12 - Inovação Tecnológica</h1>
            <p class="subtitle">Experimento: WebAssembly vs JavaScript para Processamento de Dados</p>
            <div class="horizon-badge">HORIZONTE H2</div>
        </header>

        <main class="main-content">
            <section class="experiment-info">
                <h2>📋 Hipótese do Experimento</h2>
                <div class="hypothesis-card">
                    <p><strong>Acreditamos que</strong> migrar algoritmos de processamento para WebAssembly vai resultar em:</p>
                    <ul>
                        <li>✅ Redução de 50% no tempo de execução</li>

                <div class="details-grid">
                    <div class="detail-card">
                        <h4>WebAssembly (Rust)</h4>
                        <pre><code>// Algoritmo de agregação otimizado
#[wasm_bindgen]
pub fn aggregate_data(data: &[f64]) -> AggregateResult {
    let sum: f64 = data.iter().sum();
    let avg = sum / data.len() as f64;
    let variance: f64 = data.iter()
        .map(|&x| (x - avg).powi(2))
        .sum::<f64>() / data.len() as f64;
    
    AggregateResult { sum, avg, variance }
}</code></pre>
                    </div>
                    
                    <div class="detail-card">
                        <h4>Edge Computing Integration</h4>
                        <pre><code>// Cloudflare Worker - Edge Function
export default {
  async fetch(request, env) {
    const wasmModule = await import('../wasm/aggregator.wasm');
    const data = await request.json();
    
    // Processamento na edge (≈10ms de latência)
    const result = wasmModule.aggregate_data(data);
    
    return new Response(JSON.stringify(result), {
      headers: { 'Content-Type': 'application/json' }
    });
  }
}</code></pre>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </section>

            <section class="next-steps">

# DIYAPP Evolution - V12 Core - Plano de Testes e Automação

## Estrutura do Projeto de Testes

```
diyapp-v12-tests/
├── src/
│   ├── tests/
│   │   ├── unit/
│   │   │   ├── business-logic/
│   │   │   ├── components/
│   │   │   └── utils/
│   │   ├── integration/
│   │   │   ├── api/
│   │   │   ├── database/
│   │   │   └── services/
│   │   ├── e2e/
│   │   │   ├── playwright/
│   │   │   └── cypress/
│   │   ├── load/
│   │   │   └── k6/
│   │   └── llm/
│   │       ├── golden-dataset/
│   │       └── quality-checks/
│   ├── fixtures/
│   ├── helpers/
│   └── config/
├── public/
│   └── test-dashboard/
├── package.json
├── docker-compose.yml
├── .github/
│   └── workflows/
└── README.md
```

## 1. Plano de Testes Estratégico

### **Pirâmide de Testes DIYAPP V12**
```
┌─────────────────────────────────────┐
│           5% Exploratório           │
│     (Features críticas/LLM)         │
├─────────────────────────────────────┤
│          10% E2E (Playwright)       │
│    (Fluxos críticos do usuário)     │
├─────────────────────────────────────┤
│         25% Integração              │
│  (API + DB + Serviços + Filas)      │
├─────────────────────────────────────┤
│          60% Unitários              │
│  (Lógica de negócio + Componentes)  │
└─────────────────────────────────────┘
```

### **Cobertura Mínima por Camada**
- **Unitários**: 80% (90% para lógica de negócio)
- **Integração**: 70% dos fluxos críticos
- **E2E**: 100% dos caminhos felizes críticos
- **LLM**: 100% das features com golden dataset

## 2. Critérios de Aceitação Gherkin Template

```gherkin
# templates/criteria-template.feature
Feature: [Nome da Feature]
  Como [ator]
  Quero [ação]
  Para que [benefício]

  Cenário: [Nome do cenário - caminho feliz]
    Dado [condição inicial]
    Quando [ação do usuário/sistema]
    Então [resultado esperado]

  Cenário: [Nome do cenário - edge case]
    Dado [condição inicial]
    Quando [ação que gera edge case]
    Então [sistema deve lidar apropriadamente]

  Cenário: [Nome do cenário - tratamento de erro]
    Dado [condição de erro]
    Quando [ação é executada]
    Então [erro apropriado é retornado]
    E [sistema permanece estável]
```

## 3. Implementação de Testes Automatizados

### **3.1 Configuração do Ambiente de Testes**

```javascript
// package.json
{
  "name": "diyapp-v12-tests",
  "version": "1.0.0",
  "scripts": {
    "test:unit": "jest --coverage --testPathPattern=unit",
    "test:integration": "jest --testPathPattern=integration",
    "test:e2e": "playwright test",
    "test:load": "k6 run",
    "test:llm": "node src/tests/llm/runner.js",
    "test:ci": "npm run test:unit && npm run test:integration",
    "test:all": "npm run test:unit && npm run test:integration && npm run test:e2e",
    "test:watch": "jest --watch",
    "coverage": "jest --coverage",
    "lint:tests": "eslint src/tests/**/*.js"
  },
  "devDependencies": {
    "jest": "^29.7.0",

### **3.2 Testes Unitários - Exemplo**

```javascript
// src/tests/unit/business-logic/agent-orchestrator.test.js
const { describe, test, expect, beforeEach, jest: jestMock } = require('@jest/globals');
const AgentOrchestrator = require('../../../business-logic/agent-orchestrator');
const { AgentError, ValidationError } = require('../../../utils/errors');

describe('AgentOrchestrator - Lógica de Orquestração', () => {
  let orchestrator;
  let mockAgentFactory;
  let mockLogger;

  beforeEach(() => {
    mockLogger = {
      info: jestMock.fn(),
      error: jestMock.fn(),
      warn: jestMock.fn()
    };

    mockAgentFactory = {
      createAgent: jestMock.fn(),
      destroyAgent: jestMock.fn()
    };

    orchestrator = new AgentOrchestrator({
      agentFactory: mockAgentFactory,
      logger: mockLogger,
      maxAgents: 5
    });
  });

  test('deve criar agente com configuração válida', async () => {
    // Arrange
    const agentConfig = {
      type: 'QA',
      capabilities: ['testing', 'validation'],
      memorySize: '2GB'
    };

    mockAgentFactory.createAgent.mockResolvedValue({
      id: 'agent-123',
      status: 'active',
      execute: jestMock.fn()
    });

    // Act
    const agent = await orchestrator.createAgent(agentConfig);

    // Assert
    expect(agent.id).toBe('agent-123');
    expect(agent.status).toBe('active');
    expect(mockAgentFactory.createAgent).toHaveBeenCalledWith(agentConfig);
    expect(mockLogger.info).toHaveBeenCalledWith('Agent created: agent-123');
  });

  test('deve lançar ValidationError para configuração inválida', async () => {
    // Arrange
    const invalidConfig = { type: '' };

    // Act & Assert
    await expect(orchestrator.createAgent(invalidConfig))
      .rejects
      .toThrow(ValidationError);
    
    expect(mockAgentFactory.createAgent).not.toHaveBeenCalled();
  });

  test('deve limitar número máximo de agentes', async () => {
    // Arrange
    const agents = [];
    for (let i = 0; i < 5; i++) {
      agents.push({
        id: `agent-${i}`,
        destroy: jestMock.fn().mockResolvedValue(true)
      });
    }
    
    orchestrator.activeAgents = agents;

    // Act & Assert
    await expect(orchestrator.createAgent({ type: 'Dev' }))
      .rejects
      .toThrow(AgentError);
    
    expect(mockLogger.warn).toHaveBeenCalledWith('Max agents limit reached: 5');
  });

  test('cobertura de 90%+ para lógica de negócio', () => {
    // Testes adicionais para garantir cobertura
    expect(orchestrator.getActiveCount()).toBe(0);
    expect(orchestrator.getMaxAgents()).toBe(5);
  });
});
```

### **3.3 Testes de Integração - Exemplo**

```javascript
// src/tests/integration/api/agent-api.test.js
const request = require('supertest');
const { createTestApp } = require('../../helpers/test-app-factory');
const { setupTestDatabase, teardownTestDatabase } = require('../../helpers/database');
const { Agent } = require('../../../models');

describe('API de Agentes - Integração', () => {
  let app;
  let testDb;

  beforeAll(async () => {
    testDb = await setupTestDatabase();
    app = await createTestApp();
  });

  afterAll(async () => {
    await teardownTestDatabase(testDb);
  });

  beforeEach(async () => {
    await Agent.deleteMany({});
  });

  describe('POST /api/v1/agents', () => {
    test('deve criar um novo agente com sucesso', async () => {
      // Arrange
      const agentData = {
        name: 'QA Agent',
        type: 'QA',
        config: {
          testingLevel: 'comprehensive',
          autoValidate: true
        }
      };

      // Act
      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/v1/agents')
        .set('Authorization', 'Bearer test-token')
        .send(agentData);

      // Assert
      expect(response.status).toBe(201);
      expect(response.body).toMatchObject({
        success: true,
        data: {
          name: 'QA Agent',
          type: 'QA',
          status: 'initializing'
        }
      });
      expect(response.body.data.id).toBeDefined();

      // Verifica persistência no banco
      const dbAgent = await Agent.findById(response.body.data.id);
      expect(dbAgent).toBeTruthy();
      expect(dbAgent.config.testingLevel).toBe('comprehensive');
    });

    test('deve retornar 400 para dados inválidos', async () => {
      // Arrange
      const invalidData = {
        name: '', // Nome vazio
        type: 'InvalidType'
      };

      // Act
      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/v1/agents')
        .set('Authorization', 'Bearer test-token')
        .send(invalidData);

      // Assert
      expect(response.status).toBe(400);
      expect(response.body.success).toBe(false);
      expect(response.body.error).toContain('Validation failed');
    });

    test('deve retornar 401 sem token de autenticação', async () => {
      // Act
      const response = await request(app)
        .post('/api/v1/agents')
        .send({ name: 'Test', type: 'QA' });

      // Assert
      expect(response.status).toBe(401);
    });
  });

  describe('GET /api/v1/agents/:id', () => {
    test('deve retornar agente pelo ID', async () => {
      // Arrange
      const agent = await Agent.create({
        name: 'Test Agent',
        type: 'Dev',
        status: 'active'
      });

      // Act
      const response = await request(app)
        .get(`/api/v1/agents/${agent._id}`)
        .set('Authorization', 'Bearer test-token');

      // Assert
      expect(response.status).toBe(200);
      expect(response.body.data.name).toBe('Test Agent');
      expect(response.body.data.status).toBe('active');
    });

    test('deve retornar 404 para agente não encontrado', async () => {
      // Act
      const response = await request(app)
        .get('/api/v1/agents/507f1f77bcf86cd799439011')
        .set('Authorization', 'Bearer test-token');

      // Assert
      expect(response.status).toBe(404);
    });
  });
});
```

### **3.4 Testes E2E com Playwright**

```javascript
// src/tests/e2e/playwright/agent-dashboard.spec.js
const { test, expect } = require('@playwright/test');
const { login } = require('../helpers/auth');

test.describe('Dashboard de Agentes - Fluxos Críticos', () => {
  test.beforeEach(async ({ page }) => {
    await login(page, 'admin@diyapp.com', 'test123');
    await page.goto('/dashboard/agents');
  });

  test('deve criar novo agente e exibir na lista', async ({ page }) => {
    // Arrange
    const agentName = `QA Agent ${Date.now()}`;
    
    // Act - Criar agente
    await page.click('button[data-testid="create-agent-btn"]');
    await page.fill('input[name="agentName"]', agentName);
    await page.selectOption('select[name="agentType"]', 'QA');
    await page.click('button[type="submit"]');
    
    // Assert - Verificar criação
    await expect(page.locator('.notification-success')).toBeVisible();
    await expect(page.locator('.notification-success')).toContainText('Agent created successfully');
    
    // Verificar se aparece na lista
    await expect(page.locator(`tr:has-text("${agentName}")`)).toBeVisible();
    await expect(page.locator(`tr:has-text("${agentName}") >> .status-badge`)).toHaveText('active');
  });

  test('deve executar tarefa e mostrar progresso', async ({ page }) => {
    // Arrange
    const taskName = 'Run Test Suite';
    
    // Act
    await page.click('tr:first-child >> button[data-testid="execute-task"]');
    await page.selectOption('select[name="taskType"]', 'test_suite');
    await page.click('button[data-testid="confirm-execute"]');
    
    // Assert
    await expect(page.locator('.task-progress')).toBeVisible();
    await expect(page.locator('.progress-bar')).toBeVisible();
    
    // Aguardar conclusão
    await expect(page.locator('.task-status-completed')).toBeVisible({ timeout: 30000 });
    await expect(page.locator('.execution-result')).toContainText('Tests passed:');
  });

  test('deve lidar com erro na execução de tarefa', async ({ page }) => {
    // Arrange
    await page.click('tr:first-child >> button[data-testid="execute-task"]');
    await page.selectOption('select[name="taskType"]', 'invalid_task');
    
    // Act
    await page.click('button[data-testid="confirm-execute"]');
    
    // Assert
    await expect(page.locator('.notification-error')).toBeVisible();
    await expect(page.locator('.notification-error')).toContainText('Task execution failed');
    await expect(page.locator('.error-details')).toBeVisible();
  });

  test('deve filtrar agentes por tipo', async ({ page }) => {
    // Act
    await page.selectOption('select[data-testid="filter-type"]', 'QA');
    
    // Assert
    const agentRows = page.locator('tbody tr');
    const count = await agentRows.count();
    
    for (let i = 0; i < count; i++) {
      const typeCell = await agentRows.nth(i).locator('td:nth-child(3)').textContent();
      expect(typeCell).toBe('QA');
    }
  });
});

test.describe('Responsividade do Dashboard', () => {
  test('deve ser responsivo em mobile', async ({ page }) => {
    // Arrange
    await login(page, 'admin@diyapp.com', 'test123');
    
    // Act
    await page.setViewportSize({ width: 375, height: 667 });
    await page.goto('/dashboard/agents');
    
    // Assert
    await expect(page.locator('.mobile-menu-button')).toBeVisible();
    await expect(page.locator('table')).toHaveCSS('font-size', '14px');
    
    // Verificar se tabela é scrollable horizontalmente
    const tableWidth = await page.locator('table').evaluate(el => el.scrollWidth);
    const containerWidth = await page.locator('.table-container').evaluate(el => el.clientWidth);
    expect(tableWidth).toBeGreaterThan(containerWidth);
  });
});
```

    http_req_duration: ['p(95)<500'], // 95% das requisições < 500ms
    errors: ['rate<0.01'],           // Menos de 1% de erros
    'create_agent_duration': ['p(95)<1000'],
    'get_agent_duration': ['p(95)<300'],
  },
};
